iuſtyce oute way ryghtwyſenes gone awey thus loke euery halue men ſeen ſoore without ſalue whiche al world hath ouertake ther reygne al take euery clymat hath dyele tornynge whele whiche blyude fortune ouerthroweth wherof certayne noman knoweth heuene wote done duelle vnder mone stond world vppon namely power hem ben worldes guydes good counſeylle euery ſides ben kept vpright ſuche wyſe hate breke nought thaſſiſe loue whiche al chyef kepe reygne oute meſchyef al reſon wold vnto hym whiche heued membres buxom ſhal bo ſholde eke trouth alowe al hert make hem chere good counſeyl good al forſake amonge men yeuen pee men tellen netheles loue world departed ſtant pee vneuene parted hem lyuen dayes loke al aſſayes hym wold reſon ſeche comon worldes ſpeche wonder thylk werre none wote hath yt werre lond hym ſelf deceyueth dyſeſe parte receyueth yet take men kepe thylk lord whiche al may kepe whome counſeyl may hyd vpon world whiche tyd amende wherof men pleynen trewe hertes pleyne hath expellyd pacyence fro clerge ſpecyal ſhewyd oueral euery thyng whan greuyd yf gregory beleuyd bokes wryte doth v ſomdele wete cauſe thylke prelacye god nought companye euery werke foundyd shal bytwene twoo ſtoles lyth fall whan men wenen beſt ſytte holy chirche ſuche flytte rewe vnto v alle god graunte mote wel byfalle towardes hym whiche hath ye trouth ofte ſeen mochel ſlouth whan men ben drynke cuppe doth moche harme whā ye fire vppe yf ſomwho flamme ſtaūche ſo ſpeke vpon braūche proud enuye hath made spring ſcyſme cauſeth bringe newe ſecte lollardye alſo many hereſye among clerkes reſyſtence thus ryght hath noo defence ther loue ther hold • thus broke criſtes fold wherof flok withoute guyde deuoured euery ſyde lak hem vnwar shepeherdes wyttes beware vpon world halue ſharp pryk hem leſe • feynen chalk cheſe though ſpeke teche well done • em ſelf therof dele yf wolf come wey gooſtly ſtaf thenne aweye wherof ſhold flok defende yf poure ſhepe offende ony thyng though lyte ben al▪redy ſmyte thus euer tale ſtrokes falle vpon ſmale vpon ben grete hem lacketh hert bete vnder clerkes lawe men ſeen merel al myſdrawe wol ſaye general ther ſomme ſpecyal whome al vertue duelleth tho ben thappoſtel telleth qiu vocatur deo tanquam aaron god electyon hath cleped perfectyon maner aawn nothyng thylk caas symon whiche foldes gate hath lete goth gate gone ryght weye ther ben alſo ſomme men ſaye folowen symon atte heles who carte goth vpon wheles couetyſe worldes pryde holy chirche goth beſyde whiche ſhe weth ward vyſage nought courage yf men loke holy chirche bitwene word werche ther ful grete difference prechen v audyence noman ſhal ſoule empeyre al chery feyre worldes good ſo telle also fayen ther helle whiche vnto mannys ſynne due bydden v therfor eſchewe wykked good wordes vnderſtode thenketh wold ſame yet bytwene erneſt game ful oftyme torned wyſe holy tale deuyſe merytory thylke dede charyte clothe fede poure folk parte worldes good departe noo thyng nought haue also feyn good ſaue penaunce abſtynence chaſtyte contynence pleynly ſpeke ylke body fat whiche deynte mete kepe leyen ſofte ſlepe whan hath elles al wylle chaſtyte ſhal ſtonde ſtylle hath proued ofte er thus comyn clamour euery lond peple duelleth eche compleynt telleth world myſwent therupon iugement yeueth euery man ſondry wyſe man wold hym ſelf auyſe conſeyence nought myſuſe et demerita hominum dig der iudicio proueniunt netheles ſomme men wryte ſayn fortune wyte ſom men holde oppinion conſtellacion whiche cauſeth al man dothe god w • te bothe whiche ſothe world propre kynde euer vntre w blynde inproperlyche demeth fame blameth nought blame preyfeth nought preyſe thus whan ſhal thynges peyſe ther deceyt balaunce al varyaunce v ſhold v better auyſe falle ryſe world areſteth fallith al man ouer al owne cauſe wele wo fortune clepe ſoo▪ man hym ſelf groweth otherwyſe troweth beholde peple iſrael euer whyle dyden wel fortune hem debonayre whan dyden contrayre euery • ryd hath choſe make thēketh myrthes make loue hath acheued ſo nothynge releued forther fro loue erthe heuene aboue ſpeke ony ſpede wyſt none rede man fare • nto wode gan fare ſynge byrdes whan j ye wode amyddes fonde ſoote grene pleyne gan wo compleyne wyſſhyng wepyng al myn one myrthes made none hard ylke throwe ofte ſythes ouerthrowe ground withoute breth euer wyſſhed deth whan oute peyne awoke caſt vp many pytous look vnto heuene ſayd thus thou cupyde thou venus thou god loue thou goddeſſe pyte mekeneſſe doth playnly lyue dye certes ſuche maladye haue long haue myght make wyſe man mad ſhold long endure venus quene loues cure thou lyf thou luſt thou mannes hele behold cauſe quarelle yeue ſompart thy grace may fynde place thou gracious none word ſaw anone kyng loue quene kyng eyen wroth chere aweyward fro caſt forth paſſed laſt netheles forth went fyry dart thought ſent threwe thorugh myn hert rote hym fonde none bote benger hym lyſt • duelle ſhe whiche ſource welle wele wo ſhal betyde hem louen tyde abode allen caſt uoo goodly chere thus netheles ſhe ſayde art thou ſone abrayde ryght man doth oute ſlepe therof ſhe took ryght good kepe bad • nothyng adrad al nothyng glad ne ſawe cauſe efte ſhe axed ſayde caytyf lyeth wolde ye lady dere shal hool elles deye ſayd telle thy maladye thy ſoore whiche thou pley neſt ne hyde nouȝt yf thou feyneſt medycyne madame man thyne thy court haue long ſerued aſke haue deſerued som wele long wo ſhe bygan loure thoo ſayd ther many yow faytours ſo may thou art ryght ſuche one feyntyſe seyſt thou haſt ſeruyſe netheles ſhe wyſt wele word ſtode whele withoute ony feyterye algate maladye bud telle ſay trouthe madame yf ye wold haue routhe quod thenne wold telle yow sey forth quod ſhe telle hou thy ſekenes euery dele madame wele ſo lyf therto wol laſt loke ſhe caſt ſhe ſayd aunter yf thou lyue wylle fyrſt thou ſhryue netheles wote ſelf al vnto preeſt whiche cometh anone wol thou telle one one bothe thy thought al thy werk genius myn owne clerk come forth mannes ſhryft quod venus tho vplyft hede gan beholde ſelf preeſt whiche ſhe wolde redy ſet hym doune confeſſyon confeſſus genio ſi ſit medicina ſalutis experiar morbis quos tulit ipſa venus leſa quidem ferro medicantur membra ſaluti raro tamen medicum vulnus amoris habet ic dicit qualiter genio pro confeſſione ſedenti prouolutus amās ad confitendum ſe flexis genibus incuruatur ſupplicans tamen vt ad ſui ſē ſus informacionē confeſſor ille dicē dis opponere ſibi benignꝰ dignaretur worthy preeſt holy mā ſpekend thus began ſeyde benedicite ſone felycyte loue eke wo alſo thou ſhalt ſhryue bothe two thou loues ſake haſt felt lete nothyng forſake telle pleynlyche byfalle aud yt word gan doun falle knee deuocyon ful grete contrycyon ſayd domiuus myn holy fadre genius thou haſt experyence loue who reuerence thou ſhalt ſhryne tyme pray lete myſtyme ſhryfte dyſtourbed al myn hert ſo conturbed ne may wyttes gete ſhal moche thyng foryete yf thou wolt ſynne oppoſe fro poynt poynt ſuppoſe ther ſhal thyng left behynde wyttes ſo blynde ne ſelf teche tho bygan anone preche wordes debonayre ſayd ſofte fayre place ſet thy ſhryfte oppoſe venus goddeſſe aboue touchend who preeſt loue sermo genij ſacerdotis ſuper confeſſione ad amantem bvt netheles certayne ſkylle mote algate nedes wylle nought make ſpekynges loue thynges touchen cauſe vyce bylongeth thoffyce preſtes who ordre bere wol nothyng forbere eche vyces one one ſhal ſhewe euerychone wherof thou myght take euydence rewle thy conſcyence concluſyon fynal conclude wold ſpecyal loue who ſeruaunt cauſe cam thynke bothe two fyrſte myn ordre longeth vyces telle rewe next abouen al ſhewe loue wol propyrtees ſtond degree diſpoſicyon veuus who condycyon muſt folowe hold loue al withholde leſſe wyte though ne conne lyte thynges wyſe taught ſuche wyſe nought comyn vſe ſpeke vyces vertuſe al loue lore venus bookes nomore techen nether text ne gloſe moche ſuppoſe ſyt preeſt wel wyd aud ſhame yf lewed preſthode forme wol thy ſhryfte ſo enforme laſt thou ſhalt vyces thy matere loue ſhal hem ſo remeue yu ſhalt knowe meue man ſhal axe ſeyne touchend ſhryft mote pleyne nedeth nought make queynt trouth wordes wol peinte wol axe thy ſone ſhal ſo pleynly thou ſhalt knowe vnderſtonde poyntes ſhryfte ſtōde viſꝰ et auditꝰ fragiles ſūt oſtia mētis que vicioſa manꝰ claudere nulla pt eſt ibi largo via graditur qua cordis ad antrum hoſtis ingrediens foſſa talenta rapit hec michi confeſſor genius pamordia profert dum ſit extremis vita remorſa mali nunc tn̄ vt potent feminina loquela fateri ver ba per o timide conſcia mentis agam hic confeſſio amantis cui de duobns precipue quin que ſenſ • bꝰ hoc eſt de viſu auditu confeſſor pre ceteris opponit byytwene lyf deth herde preſtes tale er āſuerd prayd hym ſay wyl wold obeye forme appryſe tho ſpak ſuche wyſe bad ſhold ſhryue couchend wyttes fyue ſhare amended hem myſpended tho properly gate thorugh whiche herte algates cometh al thyng vnto feyre whiche may mānys ſoule empeyre mater brouȝt ynne ſone thynk fyrſt begynne wyce thyn eye hath ſtonde whiche vnderſtonde mooſt princypal alle thorugh whome ye perylle may befalle ſpeke loues kynde ful many ſuche man may fynde whiche euer caſt eye loke yf myght aſpye ful ofte thyng ne toucheth herte ſoucheth hyndrynge another wyght thus ful many worthy kynȝt many luſty lady bothe hath ful ofte ſythe wrothe eye theef loue doth ful grete meſchyef alſo owne part ful ofte ylke fyry dart loue euery mā brenneth thorugh hym hert renneth thus mannes eye firſt hym ſelf greueth alder werſt many tyme knoweth vnto owne harme groweth ſone herkne thy tale ware therby thyn eye kepe warde see paſſe nought warde hic narrat confeſſor exemplum de viſu ab illicitis preſeruando dicens qualiter acceon cadmi regis thebarum nepos dum quadam foreſta venacionis cauſa ſpaaretur accidit vt ipſe quendam fontem nemoroſa arborum pulcritudine circū uentum ſuperueniens vidit enim dia nam cum ſuis nimphis nudam flu mine balncantem quam diligencius intuens oculos ſuos muliebri nudita te nullatenns auertere volebat vnde indignata diana ipſum cerui figuram tranſformauit vyde ſayth booke enſample touchend myſloke ſayth whilome ther one worthy lord whiche acceone hote coſyn nyghe hym be fyrſt hyghe vpſet whiche kyng cadme hyght acceon wel myght aboue al caſt chere vſed yere yere houndes grete horne among wodes thornes make huntyng chace hym beſt thought euery place fyude game way ther rood hunte play hym felle vpon tyde huntyng cam ryde foreſt one ſawe vpon grene gras fayre freſſh flonres ſprynge herd among leues ſynge throſtel nyghtyngalc thus er wyſt dale cam wher lytel pleyne al round wel beſeyn bnſſhes grene cedres hyghe ther within caſte eye myddes pleyne ſawe welle fayr ther myght noman telle whiche dyana naked ſtood bathe play hyr flood many nimphe ſerueth eye awey ne ſuerueth fro whiche naked al ſhe wonder wroth al hym ſhe whiche goddeſſe forſhoop anone lykeneſſe made hym take herte whiche fore hoūdes ſterte ronne beſylyche aboute many horne many route maden moche noyſe crye laſt vnhappelye hert owne hoūdes ſlough hym vengeaūce al drough lo ſone man caſte eye amys whiche acceon hath dere abought beware thy nought ofte hede toke better wynke loke proue ſo ouyde poete alſo tale whiche matere acordeth ſayth al thou ſhalt hic ponit aliud exemplum de eo dē vbi dicit ꝙ quidam princeps nomine phorceꝰ tres progenuit filias gorgones vulgo nuncupatas que vno partu exorte deformitatem monſtrorum ſerpentinam obtinuerunt qui bus citra etatem peruenerant talis deſtinata fuerat natura ꝙ quicum que ea aſpiceret lapidem ſubito mutabatur et ſic ꝙ plures incaute reſpicientes viſis illis perierunt fed perſeus mile clipeo palladis gladio que mercu rij munitus ea extra montem athelantis cohabitantes auimo audaci abſ que ſui periculo interfecit methamor telleth thus yt lord phorcheꝰ w hote doughters thre bnt vpon natyuyte suche conſtellacyon mannes nacyon fro kynde ſo myſwent lykenes ſerpent bothe one hem cleped ſtellybone ſuſter snryale thyrd tellyth tale meouſa hyght netheles comon name gorgones euery countrey ther monſtres whiche men doute men clepe hem one eye among hem thre poure partye whiche myght ſee hath hath ſhe cauſe nede lad throwes eche hem wonder thyng yet amys ther wherof telle al man hem chere caſt hem byhelde al faſt oute man ſtone ſhape thus many one deceyued wolde myſloke ne ſholde perſeus worthy knyght whome pallas grete myght halpe took hym ſheld therto eke god mercurye alſo lent hym ſwerd felle beyonde athlans hyghe hylle theſe monſtres foughte ther fond dyuerſe men thylk lond thorugh ſyght hem myſtorned standed ſtones whiche wyſedome pro weſſe god goddeſſe ſheld pallas gan embrace whiche couerd ſauf face mercurius ſwerd oute drough ſo bare hym ſlough theſe dredeful monſtres al thre confeſſor • ſone auyſe thou thy ſyght myſuſe caſe thyn eye vpon meduſe thou torned ſtone ſo wyſe man neuer none yf wol eye kepe take foule delyte kepe luſt ny ofte nome thorugh ſtreugthe loue • come myllokyng hath ferd haue told haſt thou herd good ſonne take good hede ouer yet vede thou beware thyne heryng whiche hert tydynge many wnyte hath brought tarye mannes thonght netheles good 〈…〉 thyng wherof man maye lere vertu accordaūt toward al remenaunt good torne ere fro eſſes yf man ſoo hym may ful ofte myſbefalle rede enſample amonges alle wherof kepe wel ere ought put man fere hic confeſſor exemplum narrat vt non ab auris exaudicione fatua animus deceptus inuoluatur et dicit qualiter ille ſerpens qui aſpis wcatur quendam precioſiſſimum lapidem nomine carbunculum ſue frontis medi geſtās contra verba ī cantantis aurē vnam aſſigendo promit et aliam ſue caude ſtimulo firmiſſime obturat aserpent whiche aſpydis cleped kynde hath ſtone nobleſt alle whiche mē carbūcle calle bereth hede aboue hight whiche man ſliyghte ſtone wynne hym daunte corecte hym wold enchaūte anone perceyueth leyth doune one ere al plat vnto gronnde hold faſt eke tother al faſte ſtoppeth taylle ſo ſore wordes laſſe ne enchauntement ne heveth wyſe hym ſelf ſkyeveth hath wordes wayued thns ere nought deceyued aliud exemplum ſuper eodem qualiter rex vlixes cum bello troiano verſus greciam nauigio remearet et prope illa monſtra maximum sirenes nuncupata angelica voce canorano ipſum ventorum aduerſitate nauigare oporteret omnium nautarum ſuorum aures obturari coegit thyng yt recordeth lyche vnto ſample acordeth whiche tale troye fynde syrenes wonder kynde ben monſtres bookes bellen greete ſee duellen body bothe vyſage lyke woman yong age vp fro nauyl highe doune bynethe men may ſee bere fyſſhes fygure oner ſuche nature ſo ſwete ſteuene lyke melodye heuene woman wy ſynge note ſo grete lykyng ſuche meſure ſuche myſyke wherof ſhippes beſwyke paſſen coſtes whan ſhipmen lay ere vnto wyce advyce wene paradys whiche hem helle reſon may hem duelle whan grete luſtes ſhippes ſtere beſylyche vppon note herkene ſuche wyſe aſſote hyr ryght cours weye foryete ere obeye ſaylen tyl ſo byfalle perylle falle ſhippes drawe monſtres ſlawe fro perylle netheles wyſedom kyng vlyxes eſcapeth ouer paſſeth fore hyr hand compaſſeth noman companye hath power vnto folye ere luſt caſt hem ſtopped al faſt none hem maye hem ſyng whan forth come ſaylyng ſuche gouernaūce honde monſtres haue withſtōd ſlough hem grete partye thus ſaut nauye wyſe kyng thorugh gouernaūce confeſſor wherof ſone remembraūce thou myght enſample take haue told thou wel ware yeue credence yf thou ſee euydence yf thou woldeſt take kepe wyſely coutheſt warde kepe thyne eye ere haue ſpoke haddeſt thou gate ſtoke fro ſuche felye comyth wynne thyn hertes wytte whiche within wherof thy loue excedeth meſure many peyne bredeth yf thou coutheſt ſette rewle tho two thre ethe rewle thy thy wyttes fyue wol ſhryue theſe ylke two tel therfor yf ſo haſt thou thyne eye ought myſchrow▪ amans fader ye bekuowe haue hem caſt vpon meduſe therof may nought excuſe myn hert growen ſtone lady therupon hath ſuche prynte ſuche graue nought ſelf ſaue opponit confeſſor ſayſt yu ſone thyn ere fader gyltyf whan may lady wyt hath loſt ſteve nought ulyxes dede falle anon vpon ſtede ſee lady ſtonde ther yow vnderſtonde ſo pulled thought reaſon leueth nought wherof may defende — confeſſor good ſonne god amende thynketh thy ſpech thy wyttes ryght ſeche thyn ere thyne eye wol ſpecyfye wol axen ouer thynges celſior eſt aquila que leone forcior ille quem tumor elati cordis ad alta mouet sunt ſpecies quin que quibus eſt ſuperbia ductrix clamat et multis mundus adheret eis lauando faciem ficto pallore ſubornat fraudibus ipocriſis melle verba ſuis sic que pios animos ꝙ ſepe ruit muliebres ex humili verbo ſub latitante dolo hic loquitur ꝙ ſeptem ſunt peccata mortalia quorum caput ſuperbia vanas ſpecies habet et carum prima ipocriſis dicitur cuius proprietatem ſecundum vicium confeſſor amanti declarat ſone ſhal enforme ther ben yet another forme dedly vyces ſeuen applyed wherof herte ofte plyed thyng ſhal hym greue • fyrſt hem thou ſhalt byleue pryde whiche princypal hath hym eſpecyal mynyſtres ſyue ful dyuerſe whiche ſhal reherce fyrſt ſayd ipocryſye thou art compauye telle forth ſone ſhryue clene amans iwote fadre ye mene bnt wold yow beſeche ye ſomwey teche ben ipocryte yf wyte wol beknowe ſone ypocryte man whiche feyneth cōſeyen though al innocence withoute ſo within doth ſo wold wynne deſyre wyne aſtate anone whan come ther ſhe weth corne torned gras roſe thorne lambe byforne wolf thus malyce vnder colour iustyce peple telleth theſe ordres wyten duelleth counſeyll thylk world whiche forſaketh drawen ayene cloteth ryches men ſeyn vnder ſympleſt pouerte doth ſeme grete deſerte thyng whiche lytel worth within ſeyth open fy ſynne ſecreet ther vyce whiche ny noryce euer chere ſobre ſofte goth bleſſyd ofte wherof blynde world dretcheth yet al ne ſtretcheth rewle vpon relygyon next condicyon ſuche clepe hem holy chirche ſheweth eke worche among wyde furred hodes gete hem worldly goodes hem ſelf thylke ſame ſetten mooſt world blame yet contrarye lore ther nothyng louen ſemed lyght werke dedes whiche inward derke thus double ypocryſye whiche deuoute apparancye byſer ſet vpon face wherof toward worldes grace ſemeth wel ryght thewed yet herte al beſhrewed netheles ſtant byleued hath purpoos ofte acheued worſhip worldes welthe takyth ſayd ſtelthe thorugh couerture falla ryght ſo ſemblable caas vyce hath eke offycers among theſe ſeculeres grete men ſinale accompte ſet tale paſſe comune ſuche hem lyke comune ſayth wold ſocoure peple wol deuoure day many one whiche ſpeketh peter iohn thynketh iudas hert ther ſhal worldes good aſtert hand yet geueth almeſſe faſteth ofte hereth meſſe mea culpa whiche ſeyth vpon breſte ful ofte leyth hond caſe vp ward eye though cryſtes face ſyghe soo ſemeth ſyght alone al myght reſcue holy dede yet hert ſtede among bedys mooſt deuoute goth worldes cauſe aboute myght waryſon encreſe cōparyſon hic tractat confeſſor cum amā te ſuper illa jpocriſia que ſub amoris facie fraudulenter lat tando mulieres ipſiꝰ ficticijs credulas ſepiſſime decepit innocentes ther louers ſuche ſort feynē hem hūble port al ypocryſye whiche deceyte flaterye hath many worthy wyght begyled whan hath tonge fyled ſofte ſpeche leſyng forth fals pytous lokyng wold make woman wene gone vpon fayre grene whan ſhe fallyth myre may haue deſyre ſo falleth remenaunt halt word couenaunt tyme helſpede ther ſloygthe thylk deede whiche ony lones faytour may ne put aſſay hym belonged done colour reyny mone medycyne vpon face ſet axeth grace whiche hath ſykenes feyned whan vyſage ſo deſteyned eye vp caſt ſyketh many contenaunce pyketh bryngen hyr byleue thyng whiche wold acheue wherof bereth pale hewe wold ſeme trewe maketh ſeke whā heyle whan bereſt loweſt ſeyle ſwyfeeſt begyle woman whiche ylke whyle set vpon hym fayth credence ſone yf thou thy conſeyence entamed haſt ſuch wyſe ſhryfte thou myght auyſe telle yf ſo amans myn holy fadre certes feyne ſuche ſykeneſſe nedeth nought wytneſſe take god courage hath ſeke vyſage eke thus wel may auowe lowe couthe neuer bo feyne humylyte withoute lyſt better loute al thoughtes myn herte thyng ſhal neuer ſterte ſpeke lady dere make hyr ony feyned chere god wote wel ther lye nought chere hath ſuche thought good feith leueth wele wyll better thouſand dele ony chere couthe syre haue yougthe done otherwyſe place put therof grace excuſen ne ſhal haue elles oueral loue companye pleyne withoute ypocryſye ther one whiche ſer • e al though may thank deſerue whome yet neuer vnto daye ſayd onlyche ye nay yf ſo thought touchend ſay nought ſomdele wyte ye clepe ipocryte confeſſor ſone ſyt wel euery wyght kepe thonȝt trouth vp ryght towardes loue al wyſe wolde hym wel aduyſe hath byfalle matere ſhold nought feyned chere deceyue loue degre loue enery hert fre deceyt thou feyneſt therupon thy luſt atteyneſt thou haſt wonne thy wyle though lyke whyle thou ſhalt afterward repente proue myn entente fynde enſample crony que hem loue ſo beſwyke quod ipocriſia ſit amore pericu loſa narrat exemplum qualiter ſub reg tiberij imperatoris quidam mile nomine mundns qui romanorū dux milicie tune prefuit dominam paulinam pulcherrimā caſtitatis • famoſiſſimam mediantibus duobus falſis preſbiteris templo iſys domini ſui ſe eſſe fingens ſub fic • e ſauctitatis ipocriſi nocturno tempore vicia •• vn̄ idem dux exilium preſbiteri mortem ob ſui criminis enormitatem damp nati extiterant byfeſſe old dayes thus whylome emperour tiberius monarche rome thus lad ther worthy romayn wyf ſhe pauline hyght whiche euery mannys ſyght al cyte fayreſt men ſayden eke leſt hath ben euer yet ſo ſtrong man wyt whiche thurgh beaute ne may drawe loue vnder lawe thylke frele bore kynde whiche maketh hert eyen blynde reſon may comuned wyſe ſo fortuned tale whiche wol mene wyf whiche luſtes grene freſſhe tendre age may let courage hym wol hyr aſſote ther duk hote mundus whiche bayllye lede alle chyualrye rome worthy knyght nought ſuche myght ſtrengthe loue withſtōde ne brought honde maulgry wold yong wyf loueth ſo hath put al aſſay wynne thyng whiche ne may gete hyr graunt maner yefte gold ne prayer whan ſa mede toward loue myght ſpede ſleyght feyned wrought therupon hym bythought ther cyte temple ſuche auctoryte whiche grete deuocyon noble woman toune moſt comonlyche pylgremage gone pray thylke ymage whiche goddeſſe chyldyng cleped name iſys temple rewle mynyſtre lawe whiche tho abouen al preſtes two duk whiche thouȝt loue gete vpon day hem two mete hath bede come haſte ryche feſte mete preuy place lord whiche wold thank pur chace eche hem gaf gift ſpak ſoo waye ſhryfte drough hem couyne helpe ſhape paulyne luſt deceyue myght trouthes plyght nyght ſhold wynne temple therynne shal haue hyr al entent thus acorded forth wente lyſte thorugh whiche ipocryſye ordeyned trecherye wherof lady deceyued theſe preſtes hadden wel conceyued ſhe grete holyneſſe counterfeyt ſympleneſſe whiche hyd fals courage feyned heuenly meſſage come ſayd hyr thus paulyne god anubus hath ſente v preſtes ſayth wol appere nyghtes tyme hym ſelf allone loue hath thy perſone therupon hath v bede iſys temple ſtede honeſtly purueye thou nyght ſeye hym ſhalt take vyſyon vpon thy condycyon whiche chaſt ful feyth suche pryce v tolde leyth wol ſtonde thyn acord bere herof record ſend v hyder bothe two glad innocence tho ſuche wordes ſhe herd humble chere thus anſuerd ſeyd goddes wylle al redy fulfylle houſbondes leue wold iſys temple eue vpon goddes grace abyde ſeruen hym nyght tyde preſtes gone home tho ageyne ſhe goth ſouerayne goddes wylle told hym al pleyne ca wherof deceyued eke bad ſhe ſhold meke al hoole vnto goddes heeſte thus ſhe whiche honeſte god ward hyr entent nyght temple went fals preſtes receyuen hyr ſuche tokue▪ holyneſſe though ſawen hyr goddeſſe al within preuy place ſofte bed large ſpace made enterc • rteyned ſhe afterward engyned ſhe whiche al honour ſuppoſeth fals preſtes oppoſeth axeth obſeruaunce myght mooſt pleſaūce god nyghtes reule kepe hyr bydden ſlepe lyggend vpon bed lofte ſo ſayden al ſtylle ſofte god anubus wold awake counſeylle wyſe take preeſtes fro lady gone ſhe wyſt gyle none maner ſayd tho ſlepe vpon bed leyd hope ſhe ſhold acheue thyng ſtood vpon bileue fulfylled holyneſſe ſhe hath fayled geſſe cloſet faſt duk hyd ſo pryuely ſhe myght perceyue thought deceyue hath ſuche aray vpon nome whan wold vnto hyr come ſhold ſeme hir eye though ſhe veryly ſyghe god anubus ſuche wyſe ypocryyte queyntyſe awayteth euer tyl ſhe ſlepte oute place crepte ſtylle ſhe nothyng herde aud bed ſtalkynge ferde ſodenly ſhe wyſt beclypt armes hyr kyſt wherof womannyſſhe • rede wooke nyſt rede ſofte wordes mylde comfort ſayd child wold make ſuche kynde al world ſhal haue mynde worſhip ylke ſone ſhal goddes wone ben hym ſelf god alſo ſuch wordes moo whiche feyneth ſpeche ladyes wytte al ſeche ſhe whiche al trouth weneth al vntrouthe meneth blynde tale ſo lad al wyl whan hym thouȝt ynouȝ agayne day hym withdrough pryuely ſhe ne wyſte bycome lyſte oute temple goth waye ſhe bygan bydde praye vpond bare ground knelend made offrende preſtes yeftes grete yafe home ward ſtrete dnke met ſayd thus myghty god whiche annbus • hote ſaue paulyne thou art diſciplyne holy mannes myght may hath nyght thyng whiche thou haſt euer eſche ued grace haue ſo purſued made lyeutenaunt thy way couenaunt fro day ward thyne yf lyke myne ſtond vpon thyne owne wylle ſhe herd tale bare ſtylle home ſhe went bifelle chambr • ther ſhe fille •• hyr bed wepe crye ſayd derke ypocryſye thorugh who diſſimulacyon fals ymagynacyon wykkedly thus deceyued haue apperceyued thanke vuto goddes alle though thus byfalle ſhal neuer eft while lyue thylk auowe god yeue thus wepend ſhe compleyneth hyr fayr face al dyſteyneth woful teres eye vpon agonye houſbond come ſawe ſhe ouercome ſow axeth hyr hyr ey leth ſhe yt hir ſelf bewei • eth wel ſhe dyde therfore ſayd allas wyfhode love whiche whyſome honeſte beeſte defouled two ſhe myght ſpeke tho aſhamed pytous onde told vnto houſbonde ſothe al hole tale ſpeche dede pale ſwouneth wele nyghe laſte hyr armes faſte vphelde ofte ſwore othe hyr nothyng wroth wel wote ſhe maye ther nouȝt netheles within thought hert ſtood ſory plyght ſayd wold deſpyte auengyd ſo euer falle ſente vnto frendes alle whan comen fere told hem vpon matere axed hem done auyſed ſone ſayd thought hem beſt ſet wyf fyrſt reſt pleyne kyng vpon mater thyng tho woful wyf comforted al wayes diſported tyl ſhe ſomdele amended thus day tuo diſpēded thyrd day ſhe goth pleyne many worthy cytezeyne many cytezeyne themperour herd ſeyne knewe falſhede vyce ſayd wold iuſtyee fyrſte lete preſtes take ſhold forſake put hem queſtion ſuggeſtion ne coude one word refuſe bnt wold hem ſelf excuſe blame vpon duke layd ther ayene coūſeyl ſayd nought excuſed ſo one two two haue wytte one thylke excuſement none ouer ſayd hem eke whan men wold vertue ſeke men ſhold preſtes fynde hir ordre ſo hyghe kynde tuterers weye thy yf ony man forſwey thorugh hem excuſable thus lawe reſonable among wyſe inge preſtes bothe dampned preuy trecherye hyd vnder fals ypocryſye openly ſhewed many mā hem hath beſhrewed whan preſtes dede temple thylke horryble dede thoughten purge thylk ymage who cauſe pylgremage drouen alſo faſt fer tyber caſt ryuer hath defyed thus temple puryfyed haue thylke horryble ſynne whiche tyme therynne poynt thus aduyſe duk otherwyſe loue beſtad dome nought ſo hard lad loue put reſon awey nought ſee ryght wey cauſe reſpyted deth hym acquyted al exybed loue ſo begyled ſhal neuer come ayene trouthe vnpleyne may faylen vengeaunce taken remembraunce ypocryſye hath wrought halue men ſhal nought lyghtly leue al ſhold wyſeman ſtere ſhyp ſuche wyndes blowe fyrſt thouh begynne lowe ende nought meuable al broke maſt cable ſhyp ſodeyne blaſt whan men leſte wene ouer caſt fuloften man may ſee old tyme hath fynde grete experyence wherof take euydence good war alſo perylle hym wo hic vlterius ponit exemplum de illa eciā ipocriſia que inter virū virū decipiēs periculoſiſſima conſiſtit et narrat qualiter greci obſidione ciuitatis troye cum ipſam vi apprehendene nnllatenns potuerunt fallaci animo cum troianis vt dicūt ꝓ perpetuo ſtatuebant ſuper hoc quendam equm mire groſſionis de ere fabricatum ad ſacrificandum templo minerue confingentes hem yt ben ſo derk wit • troye alſo begyn • ipocryſye hath bytrayd whan ye grekes al aſſayed fonde bataill ne ſyege myght auayll toune wynne thurgh pro weſſe vyce feyned ſympleſſe thorugh ſleyghte calcas cryſe wan ſuche maner wyſe hors bra lete forge ſuche entaylle ſuche forge world neuer man ſuche another werk began crafty werkman epius made telle thus grekes thoughten begyle kyng troye thylke whyle anthenor enee bothe cyte counſeylle wyſeſt rycheſt myghtyeſt pryue place ſo trete fayr byheſtes yeftes grete gold haue engyned gedre whan couyned feynen make pee vnder yet neuertheles ſhopen deſtructyon bothe kynge towne thus fals pee take hem grece vndertake therupon fonde awey ſtrengthe myght awey ſleyghte ſhold helpe thanne ynche large ſpanne colour pee made telden glade ſtonden acord ſhal ben record vnto kyng troye ſayden way loue thus pra yden wold thank deſerue ſacryfyce vnto myuerne pers kepe good entent muſt offre went kyng counſeyled ca anthenor eneas therto hath youen aſſent pleyne trouthe blent thorugh counterfete ypocryſye ſholden ſacryfye grekes vnder holyneſſe anone al beſyneſſe hors bra lete fayr dyghte whiche ſeen wonder ſyghte trapped hym ſelue ſmale wheles twelue vpon whiche men ynough craft toward ye town drough goth glyſtrend ayenſt ſonne tho ther ioye ynough begonne troye grete denocyon came alſo proceſſion ayenſt noble ſacryfyſe grete honour wyſe vnto gate broughte entent whan ſoughte gate al ſmale therupon many tale worſhip mynerue whome comen ſerue towne whiche vnderſtode al thyng goode pee wherof glade gate neptunus made thouſand wynter ther fore haue anon broke tore ſtrong wally doune breke large ſtrete hors grete ſolempnyte brought within cyte offred grete reuerence whiche troye euydence loue pee euermo gregoys token leue tho al hole felauſhip forth wenten ſhip croſſen ſayle made hem yare anone though wolden fare whan blak wynter nyght withoute mone ſterre lyght bederked hath water ſtronde al pryuely gone londe ful armed oute nauye symon whiche made efpye within troye cōſpyred whan tyme tokne fyred theyr wey holden comen ryght wolden gate broke purpoos ful take ſpoke er ony man may take kepe whyle cyte ſlepe ſlowen al within token myght wyn ſuche good ſuffyſaunt brenden vp remenaunt thus come oute trecherye whiche vnder fals ypocryſye hyd wened pee tho myghten fynde relees thylk ſwerd whiche al deuoured fulofte thus ſwete ſoured whan knowe taſt ſpylleth many worde waſt ſhal ſuche peple trete whan weneth moſt beyete ſhape moſt leeſe ryght ſo yf woman cheſe vpon wordes ſhe hereth som mā moſte trewe appereth fortheſt fro trouthe yet fulofte routhe ſpeden moſt vntrewe louen euery day newe wherof lyef loth loue hath cauſe wroth man luſte deſyreth loue therupon conſpyreth weedes feyned deceyue ſhal fayle receyue peyne ofte ſene confeſſor thy ſone mene fyt wel take hede thou eſchewe thy manhede ipocryſye ſemblaunt thou ne nought deceyuaunt make woman byleue thyng whiche thy byleue ſuche feynt ipocryſye loue al trecherye thorugh whiche loue deceyned ofte feyned ſemblannt ſo ſofte vnnethes loue may beware ſone wel dare charge fle vyce many womā hath made nyce loke thou dele al iwys fadre nomore ſhal confeſſor ſone kepe thou haſt ſwore thou haſt herd byfore ſayd fyrſt poynt pryde next vpon ſyde ſhryne ſpeke ouer touchend pryde yet ther poynt ſecond behote whiche inobedyence hote flectere ꝙ frāgi meliꝰ reputatur olle fictilis ad cacabū pugna valere neqit quē neꝫ lex hoīm neꝫ lex diuīa valebit flectere multociēs corde reflectit amor quē non flectit amor non flec tendꝰ ab illo sed rigor illiꝰ plus ele phante riget ded gnatur amor poterit quos ſcire rebelles et rudibꝰ ſortē preſtat habere rudem sed qui ſpōte ſui ſubicit ſe cordis amore frangit aduerſis omnia fata pius hic loquitur de ſecūda ſpecie ſuꝑbie que inobediencia dicitur et primo illius vicij naturā ſimpliciter declarat et tractat cōſequente▪ ſuper illa obediēcia que curia cupidinis exoſa amoris cam̄ ex ſua ībeſillitate ſepiſſime retardat ti vyce inobediencie ageyne reule cōſeyence al yt hūble diſaloweth toward god ne boweth lawes heſte man beſte whiche goth vpon luſtes wylde goth proude vyce vnmylde dyſdeyneth al lawe felawe ſerue may pryde led euery ſyde ſelue whome mē ſpeke whiche wol bowe breke yf loue myght hym plye elles iuſtyfye hert myght duayle thy ſone ſuche entayle thyn hert diſpoſed telle oute lete nought gloſed yf thou vnbuxome loue degre thou ſhalt thy good world acheue amans fadre ye ſhal wel byleue yong whelpe whiche affayted hath mayſter better wayted couche whan ſeyth go lowe anone may knowe lady wylle ne bowe grutche ſore ſom thynges ſhe doth wherof tha wol telle ſoth two poyntes bethouȝt wold myght nought obeye vnto lady heſt dar make byheſt sauf ylke two vnbuxome mo confeſſor opponit ben tho two telle quod fader one ſhe cōmaūdeth mouthe cloſe aud ſhold nought oppoſe loue whiche ofte preche preuelyche ſuche ſpeche forbere ſuffre pee ne myght netheles al world obeye wy ſhe though ſhe tale nought alowe ayene hir wyll yet mote bowe ſeche yf myght haue grace thynge may embrace ought ſpeke yet ful ofte ſpeke ſo ſhe wroth ſayth ſtylle heeſt ſhal fulfylle therto ben obedyent cauſe fully ſhent ſpeche le maye noman ſpede wote rede certes may nought obeye ne mote algates ſeye somwhat wold mene euer alyche grene grete loue whiche haue wherof ſaue ſpeche obedyence thus fulofte ſylence breke fyrſt poynt wherof oute poynt yet pryde vpon ſyde telle diſobeyſaunce ful ſore ſtant greuaunce may ſynke wytt oftyme ſhe bytt leue hyr cheſe newe ſayth yf ſoth knewe fer ſtonde oute grace ſhold loue place therof wol diſobeye alſo wel ſhe myght ſeye go take mone ſytte bryng wytte neuer roted tre ſtood ſo faſt degre ne ſtonde faſt vpon hyr loue may caſt myn hert awey though wolde god wote though neuer ſholde seen hyr eye daye yet ſtont ſo ne maye hyr loue oute breſt renue wondre retenue maulgre ſhe wol none myn hert euer one none cheſe whether wynne leſe mote hyr loue tyl deye thus breke weye heſtes commaūdynges trulyche none thynges thy fadre touchand ylke lore yow byſeche forme ye pleynly wold enforme myght myn hert reule loues cauſe reule murmur aduerſis ita cōcipit ille ſuperbꝰ • ena quod ex bina ſorte pur get eum bina fortune cum ſpes amore reſiſtit non ſine mentali murmure plangit amans h ic loquitur de murmure plāc tu qui ſuper oēs alios inobediēcie ſecreciores vt miniſtre illi deſeruiant toward vyce trete ther twey thilk eſtrete▪ name murmur cōpleynt ther noman chere peynt ſet glad ſēblaunt therinne though fortune make hem wynne yet grutche yf leſe weye cheſe wherof myght ſtonde appeſed comonlych dyſeſed may welthe ne pouerte attempren hem deſerte buxomneſſe wyſe oftyme deſpyſe good fortune badde mannes reſon hadde thorugh pryde wherof blynde ryght ſuche maner kynde ther louers though haue loue al wold craue yet wol grutche ſomme weye wold nought loue obeye vpon trouthe doo ſholde hem lakketh wolde anone ſhal ſuche peyne euer vnbuxomly pleyne vpon fortune curſe crye wold hertes plye ſuffre tyll better falle thy yf thou amonges alle haſt vſed condycyon ſone thy confeſſion telle pleynly thou art fadre knowe wel part ye telle aboue murmur compleynt loue ſee ſpede comende ageynſt fortune compleynende ſayth euermo eke fuloftyme alſo whan ſo ſee heuy word heuy chere lady grutche anone wordes dar ſpeke none wherof ſhe myght diſpleſyd myn hert dyſeſed many murmour god wote thus drynke myn owne ſwote though make ſemblaunt myn hert al diſobeyſaunt wyſe confeſſe ye clepe vnbuxomneſſe telle counſeyl confeſſor ſone rede ſo byfalle weye thou loues luſt obeye fer thou myght ſuffyſe fulofte ſyth ſuche wyſe obedyence loue auayleth al mannes ſtrengthe fayleth wherof yf thou lyſt wyte crony que wryte grete enſample thou myght fynde whiche comen mynde ic contra amori inobedientes ad cōmendacionē obediencie confeſſor ſuper eodem exemplum ponit vbi di que q̄dam regis sealie filia ſue iuuentucis floribꝰ pulcherrime ex eius nouerce incantacionibus vetulam turpiſſimam tranſformata excitit flo rencius tunc imperatoris claudi nepos mile armis ſtrennuiſſimus amoroſus que legibus intendens ex ſua obediencia pulcritudinem priſtinam reformauit ther whylom dayes old worthy knyght men • old neue perour court courteour wyfles florent hyghte man mochel myght armes deſyrous chyualrous amerous fame worldes ſpeche straunge auentures ſeche rood march aboute felle tyme whan oute fortune whiche may euery threde breke knytte mannes ſpede shope knyght rood pa ſtrengthe take caſtel hym ladde fewe frendes hadde ſo felle ylke ſtoūde dedely wounde frghtend owne handes ſlayn branchus whiche capytayn ſone heyre wherof ben wroth fadre modre knyȝt branchꝰ hōde worthyeſt al londe ſeyn wold vengeaunce vpon florent remembraunce toke worthynes knyghthode gentylnes ſtood coſynage themperour toke aſſuage durſt ſleyn hym fere grete deſpute ſon among hem ſelf beſt lady ſlyeſt al men knewe tho old ſhe myght vnnethes go grandame vnto dede bygan rede ſhe ſaid ſhe wold bring ynne ſhe ſhal hym deth wynne al owne graūt thorugh ſtrengthe veray couenaūt withoute blame ony wyght anone ſhe ſent knyght ſone ſhe aleyde deth thus hym ſhe ſeyde florent hou ſo thou wyte branchus deth men ſhal reſpyte take • engement ſo thou ſtonde iugement vpon certeyne condycyon thou vnto queſtyon whiche ſhal axe ſhalt anſuere ouer thou ſhalt eke ſwere yf thou ſoth fayle ther ſhal none thyng auayle thou ne ſhalt deth receyue men ſhal deceyue thou therof myght aduyſed thou ſhalt haue day tyme aſſyſed loue ſaufly wende ſo thy dayes ende thou come ageyne thyn auyſe knyȝt worthy wiſe lady prayeth may wyte haue vnder ſeales wryte queſtion ſhold whiche ſhal degre stonde lyf ieopardye ſhe feyneth companye ſayth florent loue longeth al myn axyng longeth al woman mooſt deſyre wol axe thempyre thou haſt moſt knoulechyng take counceylle axyng florent thyng hath vndertake tyme ſet day take vnder ſeal wrote oth ſuche wyſe forth goth home emes court ageyne whome auenture pleyne told hym byfalle vpon alle wyſeſt lond aſſent netheles one aſſent myght acorde plat one ſayde another diſpoſicion natural complexyon ſomme woman pleſaūce another greuaunce ſuche thyng ſpecyal whiche hem al general moſt pleſaunt mooſt deſyred aboue al mooſt conſpyred suche one fynde conſtellacyon ne kynde thus florent withoute cure muſt ſtonde vpon auenture al ſhape vnto lyere defaulte anſuere knyght hath leuer dye breke trouthe lye place ſwore ſhapith hym gone ayene therfore whan tyme come toke leue lenger wold byleue prayth eme wroth poynt oth ſayth noman ſhal hym wreke though afterward men ſpeke parauenture dye thus went forth weye alone knyght auenturous ryght curyous wyte beſt rode alone ſo cam nyghe ther wold foreſt ther vnder tre ſawe ſate creature lothly womannyſſh fygure ſpeke fleſſh bone foule yet ſawe neuer none knyght byheld hyr redely wold haue paſſed cleped hym bad hym abyde hors hede ſyde tho torned hyr rode houed abode wyte ſhe wold mene ſhe bygan hym mene ſayd florent thy name thou haſt honde ſuche game yf thou better auyſed thy deth ſhapen deuyſed al world ne may ſaue yf thou counceyl haue florent whan tale herd vnto old wyght anſuerd counſeyl prayd ſhe ayene hym thus ſayd florent yf ſo ſhape thou thorugh thy deth eſcape take worſhip thy dede ſhal haue mede thyng qd yt thou wold axe byd neuer better taxe quod ſhe fyrſt thou ſped thou ſhalt leue ſuche wed wol haue thy trouth honde thou ſhalt myn huſbonde nay ſayd florent may ryde forth thy wey quod ſhe yf thou go forth withoute rede thou ſhalt ſekerlyche dede florent behyght good ynough lond rent parke plough al ſhe compteth nought tho felle knyȝt mochel thouȝt goth • forth cometh ayene beſt ſeyne thought rode fro choſe mote one two take hyr wyf elles leſe lyf caſt auauntage ſhe ſo grete age ſhe may lyue whyle thought put ile noman ſhold knowe tyl ſhe deth ouerthrowe thus yong luſty▪ knyght vnto old lothely wyght tho ſayd yf none chaunce may make delyueraunce thylke ſame ſpeche whiche thou • eyſt thou ſhalt teche haue myn hōd ſhal ye wedde thus trouth leid wedde • yt ſhe froūceth vp yt browe couenaunt wol alowe ſayth yf ony thyng thou haſt techyng fro deth thy body may reſpyte wol thy trouthe acquyte elles none weye herken ſhal ſeye whan thou art come place maken grete manace vpon thy comyng abyde wol anone ſame tyde oppoſe thyne anſuere wote thou wolt thyng forbere thou weneſt thy beſt yf thou myght ſo fynde reſt wel ther elles ſhal lore thou ſhalt ſay vpon molde al woman leueſt wolde ſouerayne mannes loue woman ſo aboue ſayth ſayth al wylle elles may ſhe nought fulfylle thyng leueſt haue anſuer thou ſhalt ſaue thy ſelf otherwyſe nought whan thou haſt thy ende wrouȝt come ayene thou ſhalt fynde lete nothyng oute thy mynde goth hym forth heuy chere • e manere may worldes ioye atteyne yf dye hath peyne yf lyue mote hym bynde ſuche wytche old kynde woman vnſemelyeſt thus wote beſt hym lyef hym ▪loth vnto caſtel forth goth ful anſuere yeue dye lyue forth counſeyll cam lord thynges ſtonden record ſend vp lady ſone forth ſhe cam old mone preſence remenaunt ſtrengthe al couenaunt tho reherced openly florent ſhe bad par dy ſhal tellen auys wote pry florent ſayth al euer couthe ſuche word cam none mouthe yefte byheſte myght ony wyſe deth areſte thus taryeth long late tyl lady bad algate ſhal dome fynal yeue anſuere ſpecyal ſhe fyrſt oppoſed hath truly ſuppoſed hym may nothyng yelpe yf ſo tho wordes helpe whiche woman hath hym tauȝt wherof hath hope caught ſhal excuſed ſo told oute pleyne wylle tho whan matrone herd maner knyght anſuerd ſayd treſon wo haſt thus told pryuyte whiche al woman moſt deſyre wold thou fyre netheles ſuche plyght florent auſuer quyt tho bygan ſoro newe mote gone vntrewe whiche trouthe whiche al ſhame drad goth forth ſtede penaunce taketh fortune chaūce trouth affayted olde wyght hym hath awayted place where▪ in▪ lefte florent woful hede vp lyfte ſawe ſhe ſytte lotheſt wyghte euer man caſt eye noſe • baa ▪her browes hyghe hyr eyen ſmal depe ſett hyr chekes ben teres weet ryuelyn empty ſkyn hangyng doune vnto chyn lyppes ben ſhronken age ther▪ grace vyſage hyr front narwe hir locke hore loketh forth doth neck ſhort ſhulders courbe myght mannes luſt diſtourbe body grete thyng ſmall ſhortly deſcryue hyr hath lyth withoute lak lyche vnto wolle ſak profereth hyr vnto knyght bad hym behyght ſhe bath warrant hyr helde couenaunt brydel ſhe hym ſeſeth god wote yt ſhe hym pleſeth ſuche wordes ſhe ſpeketh hym thynketh wel nyghe hert bre keth ▪for ſorowe may fle yf wold vntrewe loke ſeke man hele taketh baldemony canele myrre ſucre ryght ſuche maner lucre stant florent dyete drynketh bitter ſwete medleth ſorowe lykyng lyueth ſayth deyng thought ſhal caſt awey vpon ſuche one wey old lothly oueralle nede mote nede ſhalle wold algate trouthe holde euery knyght therto holde hap ſo euer hym falle though ſhe fouleſt alle honour womanhede hym thought ſhold take heede pure gentilneſſe couthe hyr beſt adreſſe ragges ſhe tore ſet hir hors fore forth taketh weye ſofte wonder though ſygheth ofte oule fleeth nyght al byrdes ſyght ryght ſo knyght dayes brode cloſe hym helde ſhope rode nyghtes tyme tyll tyde come ther wold abyde pryuely withoute noyſe bryngeth foule grete coyſe caſtel ſuche wyſe noman myght ſhap auyſe tyl ſhe chambre came preuy counſeylle name ſuche men moſt truſt told hem nedes muſt beſte wedde vnto wyf elles loſt lyf pryue woman aſſent ſhold aſſent ragges anone drawe tyme lawe bath ſhe reſt arrayed beſt craft combes brode myght • eſſe locke ſhode ſhe ne wold ſhore counſeyl therfore ſuche tyre tho vſed ordeynen excuſed ſo crafte lyche aboute noman myght ſeen hem oute whan ſhe fully arrayed tyre al aſſayed tho ſhe fouler vnto ſe yet may none wedded nyght wo begone neuer knyght maryage ſhe bygan playe rage ſayth wel ynough therof nothyng ne lough ſhe toke chere honde clepeth hym huſbonde ſayd lord go bed entent wedde thou ſhalt worldes bliſſe profereth hym kyſſe ſhe luſty lady body myght wel thought memorye hert purgatorye ſtrengthe matrimonye myght make none eſſonye mote algate plye gone bed companye whan abed naked withoute ſlepe awaked torneth ſyde wold eyen hyde lokyng foule wyght chamber ful lyght curteyne ſendal thynne newe bryd whiche lay withynne though nought acord armes ſhe beclypt hyr lord prayd torned hir fro wold hym torne ayeneward tho ſhe ſayd one lay ſtylle ony ſtone euer one ſhe ſpak praide bad hym thynke ſayde whan toke hyr honde herd vnderſtode bonde ſet penaūce man traunce torneth hym al ſodenly ſawe lady lay hym eyghtene wynter age whiche fayreſt vyſage euer al world ſyghe wold haue take hyr nyghe put hande loue beſought hym wold loue ſayth wynne leſe mote one two thynges cheſe wol haue ſuche nyght elles vpon dayes lyght ye ſhal haue bothe two bygan ſorowe tho many wyſe caſt thought al yet coude nought deuyſe hym ſelf whiche beſt ſhe wold hert reſt prayth ſhold cheſe algate tyl laſt long late ſayd ye lynes hele saye ye lyſt quarele anſuer ſhal yiue euer lyue wol ye mayſtreſſe ſelf geſſe whiche beſt vnto choys thus graunte yow myn hole voys cheſe v bothe yow praye euer ye ſaye ryght ye wol ſo wol lord ſhe ſayd graunte mercy word yt ye ſayn ye haue made ſouerayn deſtyne ouerpaſſed neuer ſhal laſſed beaute whiche haue tyl take graue nyght day ſhal alwey ſuche yow kynges doughter cecyle felle ſyth whyle fader late ſtepmoder hate whiche ward ſhe hath bygonne forſhope tylle wonne loue ſoueraynte knyght degre al paſſeth good name men ſeyn ye ſame dede proueth ſo thus youre euermo tho pleſaunce ioye inough echone playd lough lyue long wel ferde clerkes chaunce herde wryten euydence teche obedyence may wel fortune man loue ſet hym luſt aboue byfelle vnto knyght thy ſone yf yu ryght thou ſhalt vnto thy loue obeye folowe hyr wylle weye amans myn holy fader ſo wylle ye haue told ſuche ſkylle enſample fore ſhal euermo therfore myn obſeruaunce loue obeyſaunce better kepe ouer pryde yf ther ought elles wherof ſhryue ſhal thyng ſpecyal fadre axeth pray confeſſor leſt ſone ſhal ſaye yet ſurquedrye whiche ſtant pryde companye wherof thou ſhalt anone knowe yf thou haue gylt none vpon forme thou ſhalt vnderſtonde wel matere omnia ſcire putat ſed ſe preſumpci neſcit nec ſibi conſimile quem putat eſſe parem qui magi aſtutus reputat ſe vincere bellum laqueos veneris forcius ipſe cadit sepe cupido virum ſibi qui preſumit amātem fal lit vacuas ſpes redit ipſa vias h ic loquitur de tercia ſpecie ſuper bie que preſumpcio dicitur cuius naturam primo ſecundum vicium confeſſor ſimpliciter declarat ſ vrquedrye thylk vyce pryde ye third office hath court knowe trouthe til outhrowe vpon fortune grace cometh wyſt ful ofte place doth al thyng geſſe voydeth al ſykerneſſe none coūſeyll good hym ſemeth ſuche hym ſelf demeth ſuche wyſe compaſſeth wytte al paſſeth pryde ſo thurgh ſought al thre ſet nought weneth hym ſeluen ſo ſuche ther nomo thus wold bere pryce fayre ſo ſemely ſo wyſe abouen al nought thy ſayth one graunt mercy god whiche al grace ſendeth wyttes diſpendeth vpon hym ſelf though god whiche myght auayle al vpon owne wytte ſtant tyl falle pytte ferre may aryſe h ic tractat confeſſor cum amante ſuper illa ſaltem preſumpcione ex cuius ſuperbia ꝙ plures fatui amantes cum maioris certitudinis amore ſpē ſibi promittunt inexpediti cicius deſtituuntur nd ryght thus ſame wiſe vyce vpon cauſe loue proudely ſet hert aboue doth hym pleynly wene louen ony quene hath worthynes ſuffyſaunce ſo withoute purueannce ful ofte heueth vp ſo hyghe chyppes fallen eye eke fulofte weneth nought byloued loued al ther beſt ſone telleth ſo leſt haue told amans ha fader nought trowe ther noman leſſe ony maner worthyneſſe halt hym laſſe worthy byloued thy ſaye excuſyng al men loue fre certes may noman werne loue hym ſelf ſo derne luteth mannes herte ſhal aſterte wene worthy louen mercy ſyre ye wold mene ſhold otherwyſe wene byloued beknowe ca confeſſor good ſone telle amans leſt wol telle good fadre ful ofte hath byfalle thorugh hope certeyne wenyng hath ſet veyne truſte thyng helpe nouȝt onlyche myn owne thought ſemeth belle lyke wordes men telle anſueryth ryght ſo nomore ne leſſe yow fadre confeſſe suche wyl wytte hath euer ſet ſo hope behet ful many tyme wene ſothe fynally ſpede dothe thus may telle wenyng begyleth many man hath ryght wel wote yf man wol bote whiche withoute botome ro muſt nedes onerthrowe ryght ſo wenyng hath ferde whan wende next haue wenyng caſt fortheſt laſt foole bowe vnbende whan al fayled wende thy fadre wenyng hath gone amys touchend snrquedrye yeue penaunce dye yf ye wold ony forme • mater tale enforme whiche ayene vyce ſet ſhold fare wel bet hic ponit confeſſor exemplum cō tra illos qui ſuis viribus preſumē te debiliores efficiuntur et narrat qualiter ille capaneꝰ mile armis probatiſſimus de ſua preſumens audacia inuocacionem ad ſuperos tempore neceſſitatis ex vecordia tamen et non liter primitus proueniſſe aſſeruit vnde obſidione ciuitatis thebarum cū ipſe quodam die coram ſuis hoſtibus ad debellan dum ſe obtulit ignis de celo ſubito ſuperueniens ipſum armatum totaliter cineres conbuſſit ſone al maner wyſe surquedrye deſpyſe wherof fynde write thus proud knyght capaneꝰ ſuche surquedrye thorugh chyualrye vpon hym ſelf ſo mochel truſte goddes hym ne luſt quarelle beſeche ſayd ydel ſpeche whiche cauſe pure drede lak herte nede vpon ſuche preſumpcion held proud oppynyon tyl laſt▪vpon day aboute thebe lay whan ſyege beleyne knyght cromy que ſeyne al mannes ſyght whan proudeſt gere nothyng myght hym dere ful armed ſheld ſpere cyte wold aſſaylle god toke hym ſelf bataylle ayene pryde fro ſky fyry thonder ſodenly ſende poudre hym ſmote thus pryde whiche hote whan moſt ſtrengthe wende brent loſt withouten ende proueth wel therfore ſtrengthe man ſone lore yf wel gouerne ouer man may lerne eke ful oftyme greueth man hym ſelf beleueth though ſhold hym wel beſeme al men deme hath foryete owne vyce tale hem ſo nyce feynen hem ſelf wyſe ſhal telle ſuche wyſe wherof thou ſhalt enſample take thou ſuche thyng vndertake hic loquitur confeſſor contra illos qui de ſua ſciēcia preſumentes aliorum condicioues • udicantes indi ſcrete redarguūt et narrat exemplū de quodam principe regis hungarie germano qui cum featrem ſuum pau peribus publico vidit humiliatum ipſum redarguendo contrarium edocere preſumebat sed rex omni ſciencia prepollens ipſum ſic incaute preſumentem ad humilitatis memoriam ter ribili prouidencia micius caſtigauit fynde vpon surquedrye yt whilom hūgarye old dayes kyng wyſe honeſt al thyng ſo byfel vpon daye moneth maye thylk tyme vſance kyng noble purueannce hath hym ſelf chaar arrayed wheryn wold ryde amayed oute cyte playe lordes grete arraye luſty folk yonge ſomme pleyd ſomme ſonge ſomme gone ſom ryde ſomme pryke hors ſyde brydlen hem oute kyng eye caſt aboute tyll atte laſt ware ſawe comend ageyne chare two pylgryms ſo grete age lyche vnto drye ymage pale fade hewed buſſhe whiche beſnewed berdes hoore whyte ther kynde lyte ne ſemen fully dede come kyng bede somme good pur charyte grete humylyte oute chare grounde lepe hem bothe armes kepe kyſt hem bothe foote honde byfore lordes lond yaf hem good therto whan hath dede goth chare ageyne tho murmour tho dyſdeyne tho compleynt euery ſyde ſayden owne pryde echone oure kyng hath thynge amys abeſſe royalte euery man myght ſe humbled hym ſuche wyſe hem none empryſe thus ſpoken fro hem hym tho al pryuely behynde bak hym ſelf noman ſpak kynges broder preſence thylk tyme grete offence toke therof ſame abouen al moſt blame vpon lyege lord hath leyd hath vnto lordes ſeyd anone tyme fynde ſhal nothyng left behynde wol ſpeke vnto kyng felle vpon thyng mery fayr ynongh echone playd lough fellen tale newe freſſhe floures grewe grene leues ſpronge loue among yonge bygan hertes wake euery byrd hath choſe make thus may day thende lad home aye ne wende kyng ſo ſone come whan chambre nome broder ne redy brought tale vnto ere ſuche ſhame hyndeyng owne name hym ſelf wold dretche ſo vyle pouer wretche hym deyneth ſhewe ſuche ſympleſſe ageynſt ſtate nobleſſe ſayth ſhal vſe mote hym ſelf excuſe toward lordes euerychone kyng ſtode ſtylle onyſtone tale ere leyde thought ſeyde netheles herde wel curtoyſly anſuerde told ſhold amended thus yt tale ended al redy bord cloth kyng vnto ſouper goth among lordes halle ſouped alle leue forth go kyng bythought hym ſeluen tho hou broder may chaſtye thought ſurquedrye took vpon hond diſpreyſe humylyte whiche preyſe therupon yaf ſuche counſeylle toward kyng vnheyle wherof better lered hym thynketh make hym afered felle ſo thylke dawe ther ordeyned lawe trompe ſterne breth whiche cleped trompe deth court ye kyng certeyne man trompe bra hath kepyng therof ſerueth whan lord deth deſerueth ſhall dredefull trompe blowe fore gate make knowe jugement yeue deth whiche ſhal foryeue kyng nyght anone man aſſent bad hym gone trompen broders gate whiche mote done algate goth forth doth kynges heſte lord whiche herd tempeſte fore gate blewe tho wyſt lawe knewe ſekerlyche dede helpe wyſt rede ſende frendes alle told hem byfalle hym axe cauſe ſoth thy ne wyſt ther ſow tho ſtode thylk tyme ſo trompe ſuche ſentence ther ayene reſyſtence coude ordeyne weye ne mote algate deye yf ſo may purchace gete lyege lordes grace wyttes therupon caſt len appoynted laſt lord worthy lady vnto wyf whiche alſo drad lordes deth childre fyue bytwene hem two lyne yong tendre age ſtature vyſage ryght fayr luſty ſee tho caſten ſhe forth childre morowe full ſorowe al naked ſmok ſhyrte tendre kynges herte grace ſhold go ſeche pardon deth biſeche thus paſſen wofull nyght erly lyght gone hem forth ſuche wyſe thou fore haſt herd deuyſe naked hyr ſhyrtes one wepte made mochel mone hyr hanged aboute hyr eres ſobbyng ſory terys lord goth humble pa whylome proud noble wherof cyte ſore flyght hem ſawen ylke ſyght netheles al openly ſuche wepyng ſuche cry forth child wyf goth pray lyf vnto court whan thry come men therin hath hyed nome wyght yf hem ſyghe water myght kepe eye ſow maden tho kyng ſuppoſyth wo feyneth nought ne wyſt netheles vpryſt men told hym ferde whan wonder herde haſt goth halle al attones doune falle ony pyte may founde kyng ſeth hem fell groūde hath axed hem fere ye ſo diſpoylled broder ſayd lord mercy wote none cauſe nyght ful late trompe deth gate tokene ſhold dye thus come preye ye worldes deth reſpyte ha foole thou thou art wyte kyng vnto broder ſeyde thou art ſo lytel freyd trompes ſoune hath gone diſpoilled thorugh ye toune thou thy wyf ſuche manere forth thy child ben ſyght men aboute thou ſayſt thou art doute deth whiche ſtant vnder lawe man man may withdrawe may per chaunce faylle ſhalt thou thy meruaylle doune chare alyght behelde fore ſyght hem ſo grete age myn owne deth thorugh ymage god hath ſet lawe kynde wherof may bote fynde well wote ſuche ryght ſuche degre fleſſhe blood ſo ſhal deye thus though lawe obeye whiche kynges put vnder ought wel leſſe wonder thou whiche art withoute nede lawe lond ſuche drede whiche accompt iape thyng thou myȝt ouerſcape thy broder rede ſethyn ſo thou canſt drede man ſo ſore drede god al thyne hert al ſhal dye al ſhal paſſe wel lyon aſſe wel begger lord toward deth one acord ſhal ſtonde wyſe kyng wordes wyſe broder taught al foryeue confeſſor thy ſone yf thou lyue vertu thou muſt vyce eſchewe lowe hert hūbleſſe ſewe thou surquedous amans fadre amerous wherof wold beſeche ye enſample teche whiche myȝt loues cauſe ſtonde confeſſor ſene thou ſhalt vnderstonde loue thynges alle surquedrye falle may hym wel tyde whiche vſeth thylk vyce pryde whiche torneth wyſedome wenyng ſothfaſtneſſe leſyng though foule ymagynacyon thyn enformacyon thou thre vyce rede eſche ſhalt tale rede whiche felle whilome dayes olde clerk ouyde tolde hic ſpecyaali tractat confeſſor • amante contra illos qui de propri formoſitate preſumēte amorem mu hen dedignantur et narrat exemplum qualiter cuiuſdam principis filiꝰ nomine narcizus eſtiuo tempore cum ipſe venacionis cauſa quendam ceruū ſelue cū ſuis canibus exagitaret gra uem ſitim incurrens neceſſitate cōpulſus ad bibendum de quodam fonte pro mi inc • nauit vbi ipſe faciem ſuam pulchirrimam aqua percipiēs putabat ſe per hoc illam nimpham quam poete ekko woont flumine coram ſuis oculis conſpeyiſſe de cuius amore confestim laqucatus vt ipſe ad ſe de fente extra haberet pluri • ꝰ blandicijs ad • ſabatur ſed cum illud nullatenus perfi • ere poit pre nimio languore deficiens cōtra lapides ibidem adiacentre caput exuerferans cerebrū effudit • whilom lord sōne pride vice wō ne hath caught yt worthy lyche ſechen al ye worldes riche 〈◊〉 woman loue •• ghe ſet hym ſelf aboue ſtature beaute bothe hym thought al woman lothe comparyſon toward condycyon yong lord marcizus hyght ſtrengthe loue myght hert whiche vnafyled laſt begyled goddes purueaunce felle hym day per chaunce al proud fare vnto foreſt gan fare among ther hunte diſporte hym whan cam place wold make chace hoūdes within throwe vncoupled horne blowe grete hert anone founde ſwyfte foot ſet grounde ſpore hors ſyde hym haſteth faſt ryde tyl al men left behynde wod vnder lynde beſyde roche telle ſawe ſprong luſty welle day wonder hote alle ſuch thurſt hym falle muſt dye drynke doune lyeth brynke tyde hors vnto braunche leyd hym lowe ſtaunche thurſt caſt look welle heed took ſawe lyke vyſage wende ymage ſuche nymphe tho ſay wherof loue hert aſſay bygan ſene ſtoye made hym wene woman ſyghe welle cam nyghe ner cam ſhe hym ageyne wyſt neuer ſeyne whan wepte ſawe hyr wepe cryed toke good kepe ſame word ſhe cryed alſo thus bygan newe wo whilome hym ſo ſtraūge tho made hym loue herte eſchaunge ſet herte begynne thyng myght neuer wynne euer among gan loute praith ſhe hym come oute goth ferre whyle draweth nerre euer fond place wepeth cryeth axeth grace myght gete none ayene roche ſtone knewe none rede ſmote hym ſelf tyl deede wherof nymphes welles ther elles vnto wodes bylongend body whiche dede lyggend pure pyte haue vnder graue graue oute ſepulture ſprong anone parauenture floures ſuche wonder ſyght men enſample take myght vpon dedes whiche dede tho ſene ſtede wynter freſſh fayre floures ben whiche contrayre kynde ſo folye whiche felle ſurquedrye thus whiche loue diſdeyn werſt al byſeyn ſet pryce moſt hyghe leſt worthy loues eye moſt beiaped wyt wherof remembraunce yet thou myght enſample take eke al ſake amans fadre touchend vyce thynke flee whiche wenynge euer tro weth namlich thing groweth loues cauſe wel wo yet pryded neuer ſo wold grace ſende toward lady wende towardes hyr wene loue ſhold ſo byſene ther ſhold go pryde place fer fro thylk grace ſpeke tyme mote ſuffre praye yow ye wo • axe ſyde ther ony poynt pryde wherof nedeth ſhryue confeſſor ſone god foryeue yf thou haue thyng myſdoo touchend euermo ther another yet pryde whiche coude neuer wordes hyde ne wold hym ſelf auaunt may nothynge tonge daūt ne clappeth belle wherof yf thou wolt telle behouely thou myght thy tonge ſtere toward world ſtande grace whiche lakketh ofte many place hym ſytte ſtylle whiche elles ſhold haue wylle magnilo que propriā minuit iactancia lingue famā quam ſtabilem firmat honore alens ipſe ſui laudem meriti non percipit vnde se ſua per verba iactat orbe palam eſt que viri culpa iactancia que rubifactas muliere reas canſat habere genas hic loqitur de quarta ſpecie ſuper bie que iactancia dicitur ex cuiꝰ natura cauſatur vt homo de ſe ipſo teſti monium perhilens ſuarum vtrtutum merita de laude culpam tranſferre et ſuam famam cum extollere vellet illū proprio ore ſubuertit sed venus amoris cauſa de iſto vicio maculatos ſua curia ſuper omnes alios abhotrens expellit vt eorum multiloquiū verecundia deteſtatur vnde confeſſo amanti opponens materiam pleuius declarat vyce cleped auauntaūce pryde hath take acque intaūce owne pryce laſ ſeth ſuche meſure ouerpaſſeth owne herauld fyrſt wel amys thāk worthy blame thus worſhip name thorugh pryde auauntrye wineth vylonye vede pronde vyce hath thylk wynde offyce thorugh ye blaſtys yt b • weth man name ouerthro weth vertu whiche ſhold elles ſprynge vnto worldes knoulechynge fordeth al ſore ryght ſuche manere lore ther ben louers thy yf thou art one hem trlle ſay hou whan thou haſt take ony thyng loues ryght ouche ryng take vpon colde sōme goodly worde w • tolde frendly chere tokene letter wherof thyn hert better ſhe ſent gretyng haſt thou pryde thy lykyng made thyn auannt lyſt wold fadre ye wyſt conſeyence lyeth yet neuer ſuche matere wherof myght myn hert amende ſo moche ſhe ſende mouthe ſaid grete hym wele thus ther delo wherof make myn auaunt reſon accordaunt may neuer lye loue make auauntrye wote ſhold haue encheſon ſo ye haue ſayd many one fonde cauſe neuer none daūger whiche welny ſlough therof couthe telle ynough none auantaunce thus nedeth repentaunce axe fadre forther lyf thewf gyltyf confeſſor ſone wel payd al wyto wel ſpecyal loue vevay iuſtyce louen al ayene vyce al tymes moſt debateth al hert moſt hateth eke al maner wyſe auauntrye moſt deſpyſe ensample thou myght wyte whiche fynde bokes wryte hic ponit confeſſor exemplum contra illos qui de ſua armis probitate vel de ſuo amous cauſa de ſiderio completo ſe iactant et narrat qualiter albinus primus rex longo bardorum cum ipſe quendam alium rege nomine gurmundū bello morientem triumphaſſet teſtam capitio de functi au ferens aphum ex ea gemmis ouw circumligatum ſue victorie memoriam fabricari conſtituit inſuper ipſius gurmundi filiam roſemū dam vapiens maritali thoro coningē ſibi copilauit vnde ipſo albino poſtea coram regni ſui nobilibus ſuo regaſli con 〈…〉 ſedente dicti gurmūdi aphū infuſo bino ad ſe inter epulas ferri iuſſit quem ſumptum vxori ſue regiue porrexit dicens bibe cum patre tuo qd ipſa huiuſmodi operis ig nara feat quo facto rex ſtatim ſu • que per prius geſta fucrant cunctis au dientibus per ſingula ſe iactauit regina vero cum talia audiſſet animo celato factum abhorrens mordem dn̄i ſui regis circumſpecta induſeria conſpiraint ipſum que auxiliantibus glodeſida helmege brew ſubſecuto tempore inter fecit cuius mortem dux rauenenſis tam corpus regine quam ſuorum fautorum peſtea vindicauit hem lūbardes calle albinus firſt alle bare croun lūbardie grete chyualrye werre ageynſt dyuers kynges fell among thynges tyme werre gurmūd • geptees lad myghty kyng alſo netheles felle hym ſo albinus ſlough hym felde halpe hym notherſpere ne ſhelde ne ſmote heed wherof toke awey panne whiche ſayd wold make cuppe gurmundes ſake kepe drawe memorye bataylle vyctorye thus feld wōne lond anone ouer ronne ſeſed owne honde gurmundes doughter foūde whiche mayde roſamund hyght euery man ſyght fayre freſſh luſty one hert fylle hyr anone ſuche loue hyr caſt hyr wedded laſt tyme long reſte hyr dwelte beſte loue eche wondre wel ſhe kepeth ye blynde wheel venue moſt al hotteſt loue hyr whele ſhe torneth felle maner ſhal telle king ſtode al welth pee worſhip helth felt hym ſyde greued hath world acheued tho thought feſt wold make wyues ſake ſhe lordes feſte obeyſaunt heſte may knowe ſo therupon lete ordeyne ſent anon lettres meſſagyers warned al offycers euery thyng wel arayed grete ſtedes aſſayed iuſtyng tornement many perled garnement embrouded ageyne day lordes beſt aray comen tyme ſet one iuſteth wel another bet whyle torney thus caſt care awey toke luſtes vpon honde thou ſhalt vnderſtonde mete kynges halle comen beden alle ſet ſerued deſerued hem worthy knyghees ſeten pryce ſpoke youe oute among herawdes al aboute thus bynethe eke aboue al armes loue wherof aboute boordes men many ſondry wordes myrthe whiche made kyng hym ſelf bygan glade within hert took pryde ſawe cuppe ſtonde ſyde whiche made gurmūdes hede ye haue herd dede gold ryche ſtones beſet bounde none ſtood vpon foote hyghte borned gold grete ſleyghte werkemanſhyp bygraue suche werke ſhold haue polyſſhed eke ſo clene ſygne ſculle ſene grypes eye kyng bad bere cuppe aweye whiche ſtood byfore hym boord fette thylk vpon word ſculle fet wyn therin wherof bad wyf hegynne drynke thy fadre dame ſeyde ſhe byddyng obeyde toke ſculle lyſt drynketh ſhe nothyng wyſt cuppe al oute kyng audyence aboute hath told hyr fadres ſculle lordes knowe ſhulle vataylle ſoth wytneſſe made auaūt thorugh proweſſe hath wyues loue wonne whiche ſculle hath ſo bygonne tho pryde mochel alofte ſpeken aſ ſhe ſofte thynkend thylk vnkynde pryde hyr lord ſo nygh ſyde auaunath hym ſlayn pyked oute hyr fadres brayn ſculle hath made cuppe ſuffered tyll vppe tho ſhe hath ſekeneſſe feyned goth chābre hath cōpleyned vnto mayde whiche ſhe truſt none wyght wyſt mayde glodeſyde hote whome lady hath byhote sadyſhyp al ſhe • auenge hyr vpon man dyd hyr drynke ſuche pliȝt among hem al deſpyte hyr hyr fadre bothe wherof thoughtes ben ſo wrothe 〈…〉 ſayd ſhe ſhal glad 〈…〉 ſhe hym ſo hath beſtad • hat nomore glodeſyde loueth hote ſhe make hym aſſote loue graunted nyght ſhape gedre myght bedde mete done ſame nyght quene hyr ſelf nyght ſeconde went ſtede ſhe fonde chambre derke withoute lyght goth bedde knyght kepe obſeruaunce loue doth obeyſaunce weneth glodeſyde ſhe lay ſyde hym axeth hath ſhe ſhe told hym tho ſayd thy quene ſhal thy loue wel beſeen thou haſt thy wylle wrought ſhal ſore ben abought thou ſhalt worche ſaye yf thou wolt ſuche waye pleſaunce hold ſtylle euer ſhal ben thy wylle bothe al myn herytage anone wyld loue rage whiche noman hym gouerne hath made hym werne felle al hool aſſent thus whele al myſwent whiche fortune hath vpon honde euer ſtonde ſhope among hem ſuche wyle kyng dede within whyle ſlyly come aboute ne ben diſcouered oute thought hem beſt flee reſt thus treſour kyng tſxy truſſe moche thyng certeyne felauſhip fled went awey ſhip hel •• hyr cours thenne tyl come rauenne duke helpe ſought ſo hym beſought place graunteth duelle whan herd telle maner haue duk lete ſhape hem ſo poyſon whiche drunke hadden haue beſwūke al made auauut pryde good therfore man hyde owne pryce yf ſpeke may lyghtelyche thanke breke armes lyeth none auauntage hym thynketh name auaunce renomed dede alſo thynketh ſpede loue may hym auaunte man thylk vpce haunte purpoos ſhal ofte faylle armes wol trauaylle elles loues grace attryne loue tonge mote reſtreyne whiche beryth honoure keye thy ſone al weye take ryght good hede matere thanke yow fadre dere ſcole gentyl lore yf ther ought elles pryde whiche ſhal eſche axe forth wol ſhewe thyng ye wol enforme confeſſor ſone yet forme ther vyor prydes lore whiche lyche hawke wyl ſore fleeth vpon hygh delyces lykyng vyces wol nomans reſon knowe tyl doune falle ouerthro vyce veynglorye hote wherof ſone byhote trete ſpeke ſuche wyſe thou myght better auyſe gloria perpetuos pregnat munda na dolores qui tamen eſt vanus gaudia vana cupit eius amiciciam quem gloria tollit inanis non ſine blā dichis planus habehit homo merbis compoſitis qui ſit ſtagulare fauellum scandere ſellata iura valebit eques sic amore magi qui blanda ſubor nat ore merba per hoc bra •• um qd nequit alter halebit et tamen ornato • cantus varios que paratus let que corda ſuis legibus optat amor hic loquitur de quinta ſpecie ſuperbie que inanis gloria vocatur et eiuſdem vicij naturam primo delſcubens ſuper eodem moris cauſa confeſſor amanti conſequenter opponit proud vyce veinglorye remēbreth purgatorye worldes ioyes ſo grete hym thynketh heuen beyete lyues pompe al pe yet ſhal deye netheles therof thynketh lyte al luſt delyte newe thynges proud veyne ferforth may atteyne trowe yf myght make body newe wold take newe forme leue olde thyng may beholde whiche comon vſe ſtraunge anone old guyſe chaunge wol falle therupon lyche vnto myght falle blame pryde whiche worſt vyce alle wherof ſo byfalle tale thynke crony que telle yf may lyke thou myght humbleſſe ſewe eke vyce pryde eſchewe wherof glorye fals veyne god hym ſelf hath dyſdeyne though mounte athrowe ſhall falle doune ouerthrowe eſt virtꝰ humilis per quam deus altus ad yma sed tulit noſtre viſcera carnis habet sic humibis ſupereſt et •• ſibi ſubditur omnis cuius habet nulla ſorte ſuperbus opem odit eum tetra celum defecit et ipſum sedibus interm ſtat que receptus ibi hic narrat confeſſor exēplum contra ſuperbiam et dicit ꝙ nuper quidam rex famoſe prudencie cuidam militi ſuo ſuper queſtionibus vt inde certitudinis reſponſionē daret ſubpena capitalis ſeutencie terminum pre fixit primo quid minoris indigencie ab inhabitantibꝰ orbem auxilium maius obtinuit secundo quid maioris valencie meritum continens minoris expenſe repriſas exigūt tercio qid oīa bona diminuens ex ſui proprietate nichil penitus valuit quarum vero que ſtionnm quedam virgo dicti militis filia nomine patris ſolucionem aggredi en taliter regi reſpondit ad primā dixit quod terra nullius indiget quā tn̄ adiuuare cotidianis laboribꝰ omnes intendunt ad ſecundam dixit ꝙ humi litas omnibus virtutibus preualet q̄ tamen nullius prodegalitatis expenſis mēſuram excedit ad terciam dixit ꝙ ſuꝑbia omnia tam corporis qm̄ anime bona deuaſtans maiorum expenſarum exceſſus inducit aking
