concluſyon whiche ſhold confuſyon vnto knyght ſo name wyſedome hyghe fame ward hym ſelf wold wynne thus al wyt wynne kyng bygan ſtudy muſe ſtraunge mater myght vſe knyghtes wyttes confounde laſt hath founde knyght anone ſent ſhal telle ment vpon poyntes mater queſtions thou ſhalt fyrſt poynt al thre thyng al degre al world hath nede leſt yet men helpe alther meſt ſecond moſt worth coſtage leſt put forth thyrd whiche moſt coſte leſt worth goth loſte kyng theſe thre demaūdes axeth knyght lawe taxeth ſhal gone come ageyne thyrd weke telle hym pleyne euery poynt amounteth yf ſo myſcounteth make anſuere faylle ther ſhal none thyng faylle kyng ſayth ſhal dede leſe goodes hede knyght ſory thynge wold excuſe hym kyng ne wold hym forbere thus knyght anſuere goth home take auyfement entendement caſt wytte aboute therof ſtant doute tho wyſt wel kynges hert deth ne ſhold aſtert ſuche ſow hym take gladſhip hath forſake thought fyrſt vpon lyf vpon wyf vpon childee eke alſo whiche doughters two yongeſt hem age fourtene yere vyſage ryght fayre ſtature lyche heuenlyche fygure maner goodly ſpeche though men wold al londes ſeche ſhold haue founden lyke ſawe hir fadre ſorowe ſyke wyſt cauſe cam ſhe hym pryuely yt made mone within gardyn al hym one vpon hyr knee ſhe gan doune falle humble hert hym calle ſayd good fadre dere make ye thus heuy chere wote nothyng wel ye knowe fadre auenture yow felle ye myght ſaufly telle haue ofte herd ſayd ye ſuche truſt haue layd ſuſter ne brother al world ne none ye durſt haue told pryuete wel fadre thy fadre praye ne caſteth nought hert awaye ſhe wold kepe honour wepe hyr eye may forbore wyſſheth ben vnbore er fadre ſo myſtryſt tellen hyr wyſt euer among mercy ſhe cryede ne ſhold counſeylle hyde hyr ſo wold hym good ſo nyghe fleſſhe blood wepyng laſte chere vpon child caſte ſorowfully ſhe prayde told tale thus ſayde ſorowe doughter whiche make al ſake alle ſuche chaunce befalle ſhal thyrd day leſe al euer leſe may lyf al good therto therfore ſorowe ſo cauſe ala quod ſhe fadre ye ſholden deed deſtroyed ſuche wyſe bygan poyntes deuyſe whiche ye kyng told hym mouth ſayd hyr pleynly couth anſuere poynt ſhe hereth hyr counſeyl yafe ſayd tho fadre ſyn ſo ye none weye ye muſt nedes deye wold pray thyng late go yow kyng ye ſhal make hym vnderſtonde hou ye wyttes fonde haue leyd anſuere vpon telle hym ſuche degre vpon word ye wol abyde tho lyue deye ſo betyde yet per chaunce maye purchace ſom good word ye kynges grace lyf eke good ſaue ofte ſhal woman haue thyng yt man may areche fadre herd doughters ſpeche thought ther reſon ynne ſawe owne lyf wynne reuthe done hym ſelf cure better hym thought auenture put hym al good maner ſtood lyf certeyne leſe thus thynkend bygan cheſe counſeyll mayde eke purpoos whiche ſhe ſaide day come forth gone vnto court come anone kyng iugement ſet hath knyght aſent arrayed beſt wyſe mayden wordes wyſe hyr fadre led honde place fonde kyng whiche wolde kyng knelend tolde enformed fore prayth kyng therfore daughter wordes wol take ſayth wol vndertake vpon wordes ſtonde tho ther grete meritayl honde whiche ſoo wyſe knyȝt lyf vpon ſo yong wyght ſet wold ieopardye many helde folye laſt neuertheles kyng commaunded pee mayde caſt chere ſeyd wold hyr tale bad hyr ſpeke ſhe bygan lyege lord ſo quod ſhe poyntes whiche herde ſhal reſon anſuerde firſt vnderſtond thyng al world whiche men mooſt helpe leſt nede lyege lord wold rede erthe whiche euermo mannys labour vego wel wynter maye mannes honde maye helpe forth make ryche thy men delue dyche eren ſtrengthe plough hath hym ſelf ynough nede leſt euery man byrd beſt flour gras rote rynde euery thyng wey af kynde shal ſterue erthe ſhal bycome oute erthe nome ſhal erthe torne ageyne thus may reſon ſeyne therthe moſt nedeles moſt men helpe netheles lord touchand haue anſuerd poynt vnderſtood whiche moſt worth moſt good coſteth man leſt kepe lord yf ye wol take kepe ſay humylyte thorugh whiche hyghe trynyte deſerte trewe loue vnto mary aboue knewe humble entent owne ſone doune ſent aboue al hyr cheſe vertu whiche bedeth pee maye reſon calle humylyte moſt worthyeſt alle leſt coſteth mayntene al word ſene hath humbleſſe vn hende bryngeth wer • e londe deſyreth beſt ſet euery man reſt thus youre hyghe reuerence thynketh euydence poynt ſuffyſaunt touchend remenaunt whiche thyrd aſkynges leſt worth al thynges • oſteth moſt telle pryde whiche may heuene abyde luafer hym felle bar pryde hym helle ther pryde grete coſt whan pryde hath heuen loſt paradyſe adam pryde loſt pryce myddel erthe eke alſo pryde cauſe al al world may ſuffyſe ſtant pryde repryſe pryde heed al ſynne whiche waſteth may wynne pryde euery mys pryk pryde worſt al wyck coſteth moſt leſt worth place hath forth thus haue ſayd wol ſey myn anſuere yow prey myn lyege lord offyce ye ſhal grace ſuche iuſtyce ordeyne fadre men world therof may ſay good kyng whiche reſon vnderſtood hath al herd whiche ſhe hath ſaid inly glad ſo wel payd al wrath ouer go bygan loke tho vpon mayde face whiche founde ſo mochel grace al pryce • eyde audyence thus ſeyde fayre mayde wel ye thyne anſuere eke lyketh thou wylt foryeue thy fadre gylt yf thou ſuche lygnage thou parage thy fadre pere bachylere thou ſholdeſt wyf ſyker haue lyf ſay netheles wol ſhape thyn encrees worldes good thou wolt baue axe yeft yu ſhalt haue ſhe kynges wordes wyſe knelyng thanked wyſe lyege lord god mote yow quyte fader hath lyte waryſon wende al loſt amende ye may wel thorugh noble grace yt kyng ryght place none forth freſſh hete erldom whiche eſchete late falle honde vnto knyght rente londe hath youe chartre ſeſed thus al noyſe appeſed maide ſate vpon hir knee byfore kynges charytees comen deth ſayth euermore lyege lord ryght fore ye ſayde record yf fadre lord pere vnto theſe grete ye wolden elles lete ne ſhold wyf thus wote enery worthy lyf kynges word mote holden thy lord yf ye wolden grete charyte fulfylle god wote wel wylle whiche bachilere fadre made pere euer cam erles doughter yong kyng whiche pleſyd alle hyr beaute hyr wyt alle wae loue hente none therto yaf aſſente myght mayde aſterte ſhe ny lady herte took hyr wyfe holde whyle hath lyfe thus ye kyng toward knyȝt acordeth hym ryght ouer good wyte cronyes wryte noble kyng whome tolde spayne tho dayes olde kyngdome gouernaunce aud book maketh remembraūce alphons propre name knyght alſo yf ſhal name dom petro hyght men telle doughter wyſe petronelle cleped whiche ful grace ſene thylk place ſhe hyr fadre oute tene hath breuȝt made hyr ſelf quene ſhe hath ſo wel diſcloſed poyntes wherof ſhe oppoſed confeſſor lo ſone thou myght al thyng matere one take pryde whome grace may betyde heuene felle oute ſtede paradys hym forbede good men erthe hym hate helle mote algate euery vertu ſhal weyued aud euery vyce receyued humbleſſe al wyſe whiche mooſt worthy noo repryſe taketh ageyne ſofte fayre ony thyng ſtant contrayre humble ſpeche redreſſed thus yong mayd bleſſyd whiche spak fore fadre lyfe ſhe gat therfore wanne al kynges loue thy ſone yf thou wolt loue ſytt wel loue pryde take humbleſſe thy ſyde grace thou ſhalt gete amans fadre wol foryete yt ye haue told yf ony ſuche manere humble port may loue appaye afterward thenke aſſaye ouer beſeche ye ſhryfte ſeche confeſſor good ſone ſhal herkne lay ere tonchand pryde fayre al ferforth declare cauſe vyce cauſe loue thou haſt pleyne herd aboue nomore ſeye touchend weye touchend enuye thynk telle whiche hath propre kynde helle withoute cauſe myſdo toward hym ſelf mo afterward vnderſtonde thou ſhalt ſpyces ſtonde explicit liber primus liter ſecundus pryde ſecond ther many wo ful ſtoūd wardes beryth ā boute within hym ſelf withoute thought brenneth euer whan wote another leuer vertuous whiche paſſeth hym degre wherof taketh maladye vyce cleped hoote enuye thy ſone yf ſo ye art haſt ben one tho ſpeke loues ca yf euer yet thyn herte seke mennes hele god auannce quarele fadre ye thouſand ſythe whan haue ſene another blythe loue goodly chere ethna whiche brenneth yere byyere ſo hoote thylk whiche pryuely myn hertes thought within brenneth ſhip whiche wawe renneth forſtormed blowe payned athrowe whan ſe another whiche paſſeth fortune loues yefte fadre telle ſhryfte place ſeche fynde grace ſtede may nought greue ye may ryght wel byleue toward lady ſerue though wyſt ſterue myn hert ful ſuche folye ſelf may chaſtye whan court ſee cupyde approche vnto lady ſyde hem luſty ben freſſhe though auayle hem reſſhe ben ſpeche ſorowe ſeche whan rownen ere groweth al moſt fere namely whan talen long ſorowes ſo ſtrong ſe hem wel eaſe telle dyſeaſe ſyre lady ſelue though ſhe haue wowers x twelue myſtruſt haue hire greueth nonght certes ſyre trowe al world ſeche ny woman dede ſpeche wol better auyſe hyr ſhe doth ne better ſey ſoth kepe hyr honour al tyde yet gete hyr thank beſyde netheles knowe whan ſee ony throwe elles yf may ſhe make ony man good chere though therof haue done thought wol entermete ſone though ſelf ſtraunge enuye maketh myn hert chaunge ſorowfully ſtad ſe another glad hyr alle loue ſo may byfalle fayle ſpede therof take lytel hede haue ſayd fader alle poynt ſpecyal ferforthly haue wyſt axe fadre yow lyſt confeſſor ſone axe ony thynke ſomdele thy lore telle example mater touchend enuye thou ſhalt though houndes kynde wryte cyuyle fynde ete chaf yet wol werne oxe whiche cometh herne therof take ony fode thus vnderſtode ſtant loue many place oute loues grace wold another ſhold faylle may hym ſelf auaylle yf may put ony lettr deth al may lette wherof fynde thou ſhalt wyte purpoos tale wryte hic ponit confeſſor exemplum contra iſtos ſaltem qui amoris cauſa aliorum gaudijs inuidentes ne • ua quam per hoc ſibi ipſis proficiunt et narrat qualiter mundus mile noīe acis quem galathea numpha pulcherrima toto corde peramauit cum ipſi ſub quadam rupe iuxta litus mari colloquium ad inuicem habuerunt polophemus gigas concuſſa rupe mag nam inde partem ſuper caput acis ab alto percipiens ipſum per inuidiam terfecit et cum ipſe ſuper hoc dictam galatheam rapere voluiſſet neptunꝰ gigantem obſiſtens ipſam inuolutum ſalua cuſtodia preſeruauit sed et dij miſerti corpus acis defuncti fontē aque dulciſſime ſubito tranſmutarant ther ben ſuche mo xij able hem ſelue gete loue enuye vpon al aſpye hem lacketh wolde kepe none ſholde touchend loue cauſe ſpede wherof grete enſample rede whiche vnto mater acordeth ouyde book recordeth polyphemus whilome wrouȝt galathe byſought loue whiche may latche made hym waite watche al weyes ferde tyl laſt knewe herde another leue loue mote leue ſpeke ony ſpede knewe none rede wayten vpon alle tyl may ſee chaunce falle hyr myght greue whiche hym ſelf may acheue galathe ſeyth poete aboue al vnmete beaute men knewe luſty loue true bachyleer degre ryght ſuche another whome ſhe hath hyr hert ſet myght nought let yefte ne byheſt ſhe ne al heſt yong knyght acis hote whiche hyr ageynward alſo hote al loueth mo herof polyphemus wo thorugh pure enuye euer aſpyede wayteth vpon euery ſyde geder myght ſe yong acis galathe long wayteth fro tyl laſt founde hem two pryue place ſtood ſpeke haue wordes good place hem ſyghe vnder bank nyghe grete ſee aboue stood byhelde luſty loue whiche eche hem made goodly wordes glade al hert hath ſet fyre pure enuye fyre whiche flyeth oute myghty bowe awey fled throwe loue wood whan ſawe ſtood polypheme geaunt ſawe ſoth ca galathe hym hath forſaken acis loue taken hert may forbere ne roreth bere wylde beſte whome reſon myght areſte ran ethna helle aboute neuer yet fyre oute fulfylled ſorowe grete dyſeaſe ſawe acis wel eaſe tyl laſt hym bythought whiche al enuye ſought torneth banke ageyne galathe hath ſeyne acis whome thought greue though hym ſelf may releue geaunt rude myght part bank ſhoof doune right whiche euen vpon acis fylle fallyng hylle polyphemus acys ſlough wherof ſhe made ſorowe ynough ſhe fled lond neptunus toke hyr hond kepte hyr ſo faſt plac fro polypheme manace fals enuye ne myght atteyne hyr companye galathe whome ſpeke hyr ſelf may wreke withouten ony ſemblaunt feyned hath hyr loues deth compleyned hyr ſorowe hyr wo hath goddis moued ſo pyte grace haue acis ſame place lay deed vnto welle tranſformed bokes telle freſſh ſtremes clere whilome luſty chere freſſhe luſt queme rude polypheme enuye hate wrothe thus algate confeſſor ſone thou myght vnderſtonde yf thou wolt grace ſtonde loue thou muſt leue enuye thou wylt thy partye toward thy loue ſtonde fre muſt thou ſuffre another ſo byfalle vpon thy chaunce vnwyſe vengeaunce whiche none mannes lefe vnto hym ſelf grefe amans fader enſample good ſo euer ſtood polyphemus lone tho ſhal ſtonde ſo worchen ony felonye loue none ſuche enuye thy yf ther ought elles axe forth degre ſhal confeſſe ſhryfte vnto youre holyneſſe orta ſibi ſolito mentalia gaudia liuor dū videt alteriꝰ dampna doloris agit inuidus obridet hodie fletus aliorum fletus cui pro pri o craſtina fata parēt sic ī amore pare ſtat ſorte iocoſꝰ amā te cū vidit illuſos inuidus ille quaſi sic licet iuua • uum ſperet tn̄ ipſe leuamen alterius caſu lapſus ipſe ſimul hac •• quitur confeſſor de ſecunda ſpecie • die • que gaudium altr • u de • oris diatur et pumo eiuſdē vicij materiam tractans amantis conſciām ſuper codem vlterius inueſtigat good ſone yet ther • vyce reuers vnto • nuye taketh glad •• ſſe ſeeth heuyneſſe men welfare wot • another care another hath fall • thynketh hym ſelf aryſe alle suche gladship enuye worldes thyng partye ful oftymes eke alſo toues cauſe ſtant ryght ſo thou ſone haſt ioye thou another ſawe vnglad shryue thero fadre yi vysrno wen yo w theſe louers lotten ſtreyte fo poynt coucite ben purſuaunt • yere yere ſoues court may fxr • clymbe vpon whele wene al shal wele ben doune throwe laſt fed faſt laughe ſee hem loure thus that▪they brewe loure drynke ſwete wel • ſed wote ben dyſeſed whiche telle lady dere none knowe reheth ouerthrowe ne ſtonde loue vpryght ſquyer • nyght whiche lady ward purſueth leſeth ſeweth thynke wynne glad withynne wote hym ſorowe endute euer vpon ſuche auenture comfort men ſeyn ſee another peyn may compleyne hem ſo wo beſeyne ſelf may • auayle ſene another mannes trauayle ryght glad let though fare let hie ſow myn hert game whan knowe ſame whiche lady ſtant enclyned hath loue termyned ryght ioyeful thought ſuche enuye greueth nought • e knowe culpable ye wyſe reſonable fadre telle youre aduyſe confeſſor ſone enuye pryſe ſuche forme vnderſtonde ne myght reſon ſtonde enuye hath ſuche kynde wol ſet hym ſelf behynde hynder another wyght gladly leſe owne ryght make another leſe knowe▪ ſo tale lyche matere thenke telle yf thou wolt ſhewe propyrly vyce ennye malyce hic ponit confeſſor exemplum cō tra▪ illum qui ſponte ſui ipſius de trim • tum alterius penam maic • ein patitur et narrat ꝙ cum iupiter gelum ſuum forma hominis vt homi num condiaones exploraret ab exce •• terram miſit contigit ꝙ ipſe angelꝰ duo homines quorum vnus cupidꝰ alter inuidus erat itinevando ſpacio ſpacio quaſi vniꝰ di • committabatur et cum ſero factum eſſet angelus corum ſe ipſum tun • manifeſtans di • ꝙ quidquid alter e • rum ab ipſo dona ri ſibi pecierit▪ illud ſtatim obtinebit ꝙ ſocio ſuo ſecum comutanti affixmat duplicādū ſuper quo cupidus impeditꝰ auaricia ſperans ſibi diiucias carpere duplicatas primo petere recuſauit od cum inuidꝰ animiaduerteret naturam ſui vicij concernens ita vt ſocius ſuus vtro que lumine pr • uaretur ſe ipſum mo notulum fieri conſtanter primus ab angelo poſtulabat et ſic vnius inui • alteriu • auariciam maculauit iubitex thus find write whilō wold wite vpon pleynt herd among men yt ferd wrong condycyon iuſtyfycacyon cauſe doune ſent aungel whiche aboute went ſoth knowe may byfelle vpon day angel hym shold enforme clothed man forme ouertook vnderſtonde two men wenten ouer bonde thorugh whiche thought aſpye cauſe goth companye aungel wordes wyſe oppoſeth hem ſondry wyſe lowde wordes ſofte made hem deſputen ofte eche hem waſon thus tale hem lad good examynacyon tyl knewe condycyon men bothe two ſawe alſo wel laſt tho one hem coueyt • u fe lawe enuyous thus whan hath knowlechyng anone feyned departyng ſayd mote algate wende herken fell ende made hem vnderſtonde goddes ſonde ſayd kyndeſhip haue done hym felauſhip wold ſom grace ageyne bad one hem ſhold ſeyne thyng hym leueſt craue ſhal yefde haue ouer eke forth al ſayth haue ſhal double felawe axeth thus grace taxeth concytous wondre glad man ſeyth fyvſt ax • ſholde ſuppoſeth wolde make axyng worldes good knewe wel ſtood hym ſelf double wyght shal take thus ſleyght cauſe wolde wynne • ad felawe fyrſt begynne enuyous though late ſawe mot • algate make axynges fyrſt thought worſhip proufyte ſought ſhal double fere wold cheſe manere ſheweth toward enuye • vnto angel thus ſeyd yef • e thus preyd make hym blynde owne eye felawe thyng ſyghe word ſo ſone ſpoke owne eye loke▪ felawe forth alſo blynde eyen two tho glad ynough one wepte • ough ſet • tye coſt wherof two hath loſt thylke enſample whiche felle tho men telle ful ofte ſo world empeyreth comonly yet wote none cauſe acordeth nought kynde myn owne harme ſ • che fynde ſhal brother greue myght neuer wel acheue ſ • yſt thou ſone folye fadre yf ſhold ly • vpon poynt whiche ye haue ſayd yet myn hert neuer layd wyſe haue told ouermore yf ye wold ought elles ſhryft ſaye touchand enuye wold praye •••• die par eſt detractio p • ſſima peſtem qne magi infamein fla •• bue •• agit • ingua venenato ſermone reper • utit aures sic vt alteteris scandala f • volat morſibus • rge quos inficit ipſa fideles vulneris ignoti ſ • pe ſalute carent sed ge ne •• ſue amor •• nguam cōſeruat vt eiꝰ • erbum qd loquitur nulla ſiniſtra ge •• hic tractat confeſſor de tercia ſpe 〈◊〉 iuiudie que detractio dicitur 〈◊〉 ••• •• ſus viperos leſa qm̄ ſepe fama de • langit ton • hend enuyoꝰ brood wote one al good netheles ſuch yet ther one yt whiche • l • ped detractyon conferme actyon hath holde male bouche whoos tonge neuer croſſe ne crouche may ſo prouounce pleyne good word withoute froūce behynde man bak though pr • yſe fynt ſom lak whiche tale ay laſt al pryce ſhal ouer caſt though ther cauſe yet wol iangle thy yt hath yt herauldye hem vſen lye nettle whiche vp renneth freſſhe rede roſe brenneth maketh hym fade pale hewe ryght ſo fals enuyous hewe euery place duelleth fals wordes whiche telleth torneth preyſyng blame worſhip worldes ſhame ſuche leſynges compaſſeth ſo good ne paſſeth byt wene teth bakbyted thorugh fals tong endyted lyke sharnebyrdes kynde who nature fynde hoteſt day comen mery may ſpret wynge vp fleeth vnder al aboute ſeeth fayre luſty floures ſpryng therof hath lykyng ſeeth ony beſte filthe maketh feſte therupon wold alyghte lyketh hym none ſyghte ryght ſo iangler enuyous though man ſe vertuous ful good condycyon therof maketh mencyon elles ſo ly • e wherof may ſee wyte renneth open mouth behynde man maketh couth al vertu whiche wol hyde euery man openly vyce telle whiche ſcole helle taught foſtred vp • nuye houſhold companye hath propre offyce ſet euery man vyce ſo mouth comly word euermore ſyt wry ſeyth werſt may wyſe nowe day loues court man may ful ofte pleyne matere many enuyous tale ſtered may anſuered yet ful ofte byleued many worthy loue greued thorugh bakbytynge fals enuye thou haue made ſuche ianglarye loues court ſone hic amoris cauſa huins vicij •• men ad memoriam reducens cōfeſfeſſor amanti ſuper codem plenius opponit shryue therof fadre yi wyte ye openly priuely whan dere lady mete thynke mete vnto hyr hyghe worthyneſſe eſe ſee hyr beſyneſſe al yong buſty route whiche al day purſueth aboute eche tyme wayteth eche tale affayteth al deceyue innocent whiche wol aſſent men ſeyn vnknow • n vnkiſt hyr thombe ſhe helde hyr fiſt cloſe n • hyr owne hond may wynne noman lond leueth al ſhe hereth thus ful ofte hyr ſelf ſhe ſkereth al ware wyſt al myn herte aryſt theſe comon louers ſee wold holde hem thre welny louen oueral myn hert enuyous al euer adrad gyle aunter yf within ony whyle myght innocence enhaunte thy wordes ful ofte haunte behynden hem ſo dare wherof lady may ware ſay euer cometh mouth wers wold yf couth come vnto ſpeche al may enquere ſeche ſuche deceyte telle al ay worſt ſpecyal fayne wolde ſhe wyſt lytel ben tryſt wold mēt double encent thus toward hem wykked mene wykked word euer grene netheles ſoth telle certeyne yf ſo byfelle •• der treweſt man bore cheſe among thouſand ſcore whiche al fully tryſt lady loued wyſt yet rather ſhold ſpede wold ſuche tale ſprede lady yf myght wol al peyne vnryght therto wold al peyne certes though ſhold feyne telle neuer thought al world myght nought ſuffre another fully wynne yet begynne good bad wold none lady maketh fnlof • e aſpye vſen wordes enuye make bere blame thylk fame whiche vnto lady drawe euer renne gnawe hynder hem al euer may • ſothly ſaye lady ſelue celle nought twelue therof wol wel auyſe ſpeke iangle ony wyſe toucheth lady name wherof ſo euer myſpayd haue ye herd haue ſayd wol ye fadre ſone ſo euer kepe thy tonge ſtylle thou myȝt haue thy wille thou ſeyſt thy ſeluen lady ſuche manere wyſe ſo ware al thynges nedeth bakbytynges thou thy lady mys enforine ſhe knoweth al forme thy ſelf art enuyous thou ſhalt gracyous thou parauentur ſholdeſt elles ther wol man drynk welles whiche wote poyſon ynne aud ofte ſuche men begynne wardes ſuche fynde ſet hem ofte fer behynde wenen byfore good ſone thou therfore ware leue thy wycked ſpeche wherof hath fallen ofte wreche many man byfore tyme ſo wol handes tyme muſt vncleue many mote ſhal ſene wol elles eleue ſhold euery wyſe man fere ſo wol another blame ſekyth ofte owne ſhame whiche elles myght ryght ſtylle thy yf thy wylle ſtonde vpon amendement tale grete entendemêt thynke telle thy ſake wherof thou myght enſample take hic loqiutur confeſſor contra iſtos amoris cauſa detrahentes qui ſuis obliquijs aliena ſolacia perturbāt et nacrat exemplum de conſtancia tibe folowe ouer al gladly wold knowen al hold couert alway fulofte ye nay ne lyſt anſuere ony wyſe feynyng ſemblaunt wyſe herken tale tyl knowe lady louers al rowe haue wrought fare though herd nouȝt word nedes mote though loue al dyſcouer vnto lady dere good feyth haue myght hele fro ſwete wyght toucheth ony thyng wote wel heuen kyng ſythen fyrſt world bygan vnto none ſtrannge man ne feyned ſemblannt ne chere wyte axe matere though yt loueth x twelue nought lady ſelue yf wold axe ony rede al onlyche owne hede loue ferde tale myn eres herde myn hert cam nought ne ſanke depper thought bnt helde counſeylle bede told neuer ſtede lete paſſ • come fadre ſaye thy dome thou wolt yt peyned fals ſemblan̄t haue feyned ſone yf reſon wel peiſed may vertu vp reyſed ne vyce none ſet pryſe thy ſone yf thou wyſe vyſer vpon face whiche wol thyn hert embrace yf thou within throwe another man ſhal knowe myȝt thou lightely falle blame leſe grete part thy name netheles degre ful oftyme thou myght ſe ſuche men day vyce ſette aſſay ſpeke man blame warne thy ſhame ſone may talke euery place walke yf ſo none many dayes gone fyrſt herd telle fals ſemblaūt hath moſt comonly yere yere hem duelle among v ſuche lumbardes calle ſlyeſt alle men ſeyn towne aboute feyne ſhewe thyng withoute whiche reuers within wherof ofte wyn whan reſon ſhold leſe ben laſt yet chefe fyrſt yet behynde gone ſhuld fynde proufyte owne lond thus gone fre withoute bond done proufyte al large men bere al charge lumbardes vnto couyne whiche al londes conne engyne may fals ſemblaunt eſpecyal br lykened euer al thynken duelle among ſelf ſo telle fyrſt ben enformed lere craft whiche cleped faucrere yf faucrere come aboute afterward ſtant doute voyde ſubtyle honde beſt goodes lond brynge chaf take corn faucrere goth forn al wey fynt let • e none vſſher ſhet whiche hym lyſt take entre thus counſeyll moſt ſecre euery thyng faucrere knoweth whiche ſtraūge place bloweth whiche wote may moſt greue thus faucrere maketh byleue ful ofte hath deceyued er may ben apperceyued thus vyce drede theſe old bokes rede ſuche enſamples ar hym ought war al tho feynen chere wherof thou ſhalt tale hic ponit confeſſor exemplum contra iſtos q̄ ſub diſſimulate beniuolēcie ſpeculo alios amore defrau dant et narrat qualiter hercules c • ipſe quoddam fluuium cuiꝰ vad • non nouit cum deianyra tranſmeare propoſuit ſuperueniens neſſus gigas ob amiciciam herculis vt dixit deianyram vlnas ſu • ſuſcipiens trans ri pam ſaluo perduxit et ſtatim cum ad litus perueniſſet ꝙ cito currere pptuit ipſam tam quam propriam preiudicium herculis aſportare fugiens conabatur per qd non ſolum ipſi ſed eciam herculi mortis euentum fortuna poſt modum cauſauit fals ſemblaunt whiche beleued ful many worthy wyght greued long tyme bore ſone wyl therfore tale telle fals ſemblaunt whiche falſeth many couenaunt many fraude fals coūſeylle honged vpon ſeylle abouten gylteles bothe deyanyre hercules whiche grete dyſeſe felle thorugh fals ſemblaūt ſhal telle hercules within throwe al hath hert throwe vpon fayre deyanyre felle hym day deſyre vpon ryuer ſtood paſſe wold ouer flood withoute bote hym lede loue drede tendreneſſe ſwete wyght knewe forth aryght geaunt nyghe whiche neſſus hyght whan ſyghe hercules deianyre within hert gan conſpyre whiche thought trecherye hath hercules grete enuye whiche bare herte loke thought ſhal wroke ne durſt netheles ayene worthy hercules falle debate fyght feyned ſemblaunt al ſleyght frendſhip al good cometh ſtood maketh hem al chere ſayth owne man al redy thyng may fel ſo vpon ſemblaunt tryſt axeth hem yf wyſt thyng beſt done myghten ſauf ſont water paſſe ſhe whan neſſus pryuete knewe hert ment double entent made hem ryght glad vyſage herd paſſage hym hyr thought gyle feyneth ſemblaunt whyle thought al another wyſe done hem pleſaunce ſeruyce neſſus wordes ſlyghe yaf counſeylle fore eye whiche ſemed outward prouffytable within deceyuable bad hem ſtremes depe beware take kepe knowe compas helpe ſuche ca ſayth hym ſelf eaſe wold yf yt myght hem pleaſe paſſage water take lady vndertake bere hyr ſtronde ſauf ſet vpon londe hercules may alſo weye knowe ſhold go therto acorden alle ſhal byfalle wel payd hercules geaunt alſo glad toke lady vpon lofte ſet hyr ſhulder ſofte flood bygan wade whiche grutchyng made bare hyr oner ſauf ſoūde ſtood drye gronnd hercules ferre behynde ſet trouthe al oute mynde ſo ther lefe loth deianyre forth goth thought dyſſeuer companye hem euer hercules therof took hede faſt euer myght hym ſpede hyeth throwe hapneth bowe whiche al haſt bende wold arowe ſende whiche fore venymed hath ſo wel ſhot tymed hym thorugh body ſmet thus fals wyght let leſte ſuche felonye whan neſſus wyſt ſhold dye took deianyre ſhert blood hert thorugh oute deſteyned ouer al told ſhe ſo • kepe ſhal pryuely hir entent yf lord hert went loue ony place ſhyrt ſayth hath ſuche grace yf ſhe may ſo mochel make ſhyrte vpon hym take ſhal al lete veyn torne loue ageyn ſo glad deianyre hyr hert hyr thought fyre tyl cofer loke therof word ſpoke dayes gone yeres paſſe hertes waxen laſſe laſſe hem loue vntrewe hercules hert newe hert hath ſet eolen therof ſpeken al men eolen fayre mayde men thylk tyme ſayde kynges doughter euryce ſhe made hercules ſo nyce vpon loue ſo aſſote hym clotheth hyr cote ſhe clothed ofte thus febleſſe ſet alofte ſtrengthe put vnder fote man therof doo bo • e deianyre hath herd ſpeche ſorowe ſeche helpe wote ſhe none goth vnto hyr coufer anone wepeud eye woful herte took oute thylk vnhappy ſherte ſhe wend wel brought hyr werke aboute ſo hercules ſhert dede ſuche entent ſhe bede neſſus ſayd er therfore ſhe ye ner aud fortune may weyued fals ſemblaunt ſhe deceyued ſhe wende beſt haue wonne loſt al ſhe hath bygonne thylk ſhert vnto bone body ſet fyre anone cleueth ſo may twynne venym therynne wyld man vnto hyghe wode ran clerk ouyde telleth grete tree ground felleth ſtrengthe owne myght made hughe fyre vpryght lept hym ſelf therin one brente hym bothe fleſſhe bone whiche thyng cam thorugh fals ſēblāt fals neſſus geant made vnto hym wyf wherof hath loſt lyf ſhe alſo euermo thy ſone thou wo rede wel ware therfore ſo grete man lore ought yeue grete conceypt warne al ſuche deceypt graunt mercy fader ware fer dare fals ſemblaunt take acqueyntaūce rather wol penaunce haue feyned chere axe forth ſo ther • bylongeth ſhryfte ſone yet ther fyfte whiche conceyued enuye clepend ſupplantarye thorugh who compaſſement gyle ful many hath loſt whyle loue wel wyſe ſhal deuyſe inuidꝰ alte riu • ſupplātator hōris et tua quo vertat cultura ſubtꝰ arat eſt opꝰ occultū q̄i q̄ latrt āgīs ī herba qd facit ſubita ſorte nociuus adeſt sic ſubtilis amās aliū ſupplātat amāt • et capit occulte qd ne • ipſe palam sepe que ſupplātās plātā plātat amo • quod pntat proprijs alter ha bere bo • u hie tractat confeſſor de quinta ſpe cie inuidie que ſupplantacio dicitur cu ius cultor pr • uſ que percipiatur aliene dignitatis officij multociēs intruſor exiſtens vyce supplantacyon many fals collacyon cōſpirethal vnknowe ful oftyme hath ouerthrowe worſhip another man wel lyf awayte ayene ſleyght caſt purpoos laſt ne hath withſet mooſt al herte ſet court vpon theſe grete offyces dygnytees benefyces thus goth ſleyghte hyndre ſhoue another ſtonden ſlyghe compas ſeede another ſo ſet hym ſelf ynne r • ebeth ſo wynne another man ſhal l • ſe thus ful ofte chalk chefe chaungeth ful lytel coſt wherof another hath loſt proufyt ſhal receyue fortune receyue chaunge vpon whele woo men wele another man auayleth aſtate thus vp hayleth taketh byrd beyete men buſſhes bete ſone ſame wyſe louers ſuche empryſe ſhapen hem relyeued wrong achyeued man ryght whiche hath take day nyght ty kepe owne ſtore toward hym ſelf euermore propre lawe whiche thynge axeth felawe worchen ſupplauut take part thylk plant whiche hath hym ſelf ſet ſo fulofte al vnknet ſom man weneth ryght faſt ſupplaunt ſly caſt ful ofte happeneth mowe thyng another man hath • owe maketh comon propyrte ſleyghte ſubtylte men may ſeen yere yere thus cleymeth boot ſtere whiche another mayſter thy ſone yf thou haſt ben ſuche profeſſyon dyſcouer thy confeſſyon haſt thou ſupplanted ony man ought yow telle myn holy fadre dede withouten ony drede gilteles thought cenſcyence excuſe nought wrong ryght lacketh thyng myght ne wold longe man loue • wy wey supplantacyon haue made appropryacyon hold neuer bought though another man forthought al ſpeke one whome lete al gone may ouerpaſſe ne mote alwey compaſſe • e rought queynty • e myght ony wyſe fro ſuche lady ſerue hert make ſwerue withoute ony part loue thegoddes al aboue wold myght ſo byfalle alone ſhold hem alle supplante welde hyr wylle yt thyng may nought fnlfylle yf ſhold ſtrengthe make dar vndertake thongh alyſander therof myght ryſe ſklaunder certes ſhal neuer good feyth yet lener ony ſympleſſe dye worche ſuche ſupplantarye wyſe wol ſay yf fond ſyker way wold concluſyon worche ſupplantacyon hyghe loue wynne fadre yf ſynne al redy redreſſe gylt whiche confeſſe ſone ſupplant dar drede tant ne quant thyng haue herd thou haſt myſferd thynkend lyketh nought god beholt man thought yf thou vnderſtood ſoth loues cauſe doth man ſupplantour thou woldeſt thyn honour double way take kepe fyrſt thyn owne eſtate kepe thy ſelf ſo wel thought thou ſupplanted nought eke worſhip thy name towardes ſame ſuffre euery man haue netheles wayte al aſſayes supplant loue wayes leef ful ofte leuer forſaketh hath done euer enſample fynde therupon qualiter agamenō de amore brexeide achillē diomedes de amore cri ſeide troilum ſupplanta • ut troye agamenon supplanted worthy knyghte achilles ſwete wyghte whiche named brexeyda alſo cryſeyda whome troylus loue ches supplanted hath diomedes qualiter amphitriun ſocium ſuam geta qui almaenam peramauit ſeipſum loco alterius cauteloſa ſupplanta cione ſubſtituit geta amphitryone whilome one frendſhip companye rede ſupplantarye loue betyd tho begyled hath one hem two geta whome mene whome luſty fayr almene aſſured wey loue beſt wende aboue ſykereſt cupido ſo cauſe lad whyle oute weye amphytryon haſt next weye hath take forme hath wrouȝ nyght vnto chambre ſought ſhe lay within whyle counterfeted dyde fyle voys geet ſuche wyſe made hyr hyr bed aryſe wenend lete hym gyder bed armes faſt geta cam laſt vndo dore ſayd vndo ſhe anſuerd bad hym goo ſayd bedde al warme hyr lyef lay naked hyr arme wende ſoth lo ſupplaunt loue doth get • forth beiaped went yet ne wyſt ment amphitryon hym hath ſupplanted ſleyghtr loue enchaūtrd thus put euery man oute ſhip loue hath loſt rother reſon ſtere fo ſkepe matere touchend loue supplaunt tal • whiche acordaunt vnto thyn ere thynke enforme herken men ye noble rome calle er ſet cryſtes feith crony que ſeyth emperour whiche ladde pee werres hadde thyng dyſobeyſaunt whiche was▪ rome appertenaunt al torned reſt ſom thought beſt ſom thought thyng ſo vnto tho who herte ſtood vpon knyghthode mooſt al manhode worthy ſone emperour whiche wold ben werryour chyualrous worldes fame deſyrous bygan fadre beſeche werres myght ſeche ſtraunge march ryde fadre ſayd ſhold abyde wold graunte hym leue whiche wold byleue knyght whiche tryſt ryght euen thought lyſt toke told hym courage purpoſyth vyage fortune hym ſtonde ſeyd wold fonde grete ſee paſſe vnknowe abyde throwe vpon werres • auayle poynt withoute fayle knyȝt hath herd lord ſwore ſtant acord bothe yong preny counſeyl ben aſſented wende therupon make ende treſour ynough hem token whan tyme beſt loken ſodenlyche galey fro rome lond wente▪ wey londed vpon ſyde world felle ſo ylke tyde whiche euer happes hath dyuerſe grete soldan perſe ayene calyphe egypt werre whiche hym beclypt hath marche coſteraunt whiche purſyuaunt worſhip armes atteyne romayn anone lete ordeyne redy euery dele arrayed wele euery thyng hym bylongeth strauȝt vnto kayre wey fong geth sowdan fond axeth within lond myght hym werre ſerue whiche wol thank deſerue soldan ryght glad wel ſpecyall wyſt romayn elles incertayn myghte wyte wey thus knyght whome ſey toward soldan left march eft dedely werres wrought ſuche knyghthode euery man ſpak hym good thylke tyme ſo ſtood myghty soldan wyf doughter hath lyf men ſayd none ſo feyr ſhold hyr fadres heyr yeres rype ynough hyr beaute many herte drongh bowe ylke lawe fro lyf may withdra loue who nature set lyf deth noo meſure hem knyghthode vndertake luſty peyne hath ouertake h • rte romayn ſo ſore knyghthode pro weſſe auaunteth courage lyche lyon rage fro whome al beſtes fbe suche knyght degre armed felde ther durſt none abyde ſhelde grete pryce vpon werres ſhe whiche al chaunce lad fortune ſhope march ſo thaſſent bothe two soldan calyphe eke batayll vpon day ſeke whiche ſuche awey ſet lenger ſhold let made hem ſtrong euery ſyde drough toward tyde bataylle ſhold soldan grete prynete goldryng doughter toke made hyr ſwere vpon book eke vpon goddes alle yf fortune ſo byfalle bataylle dye ſhe ſhal thylk man obeye take hym houſbonde whiche thylk ſame ryng honde hyr ſhold brynge deth hath ſhe ſwore forth geth al power lond vnto march fond enemy ful enbataylled soldan hath feld aſſaylled ben hardy ſone aſſemblen wherof dredeful hertes tremblen one ſleeth ſterueth abouen pryce deſerueth knyght romayn rode dedely ſwerd man abode ayene defence egypt fled preſence perſe vpon chace pursuen grace byfelle arowe oute bowe al ſodenly ylke throwe soldan ſmote lay chaas left thylke day bore tent souldan ſyghe went ſholde algate dy • knyaht romanye hym moſt tryſt doughter rynge anone twyſt took hym told hym al ca vpon othe token ſhe ſhold ben wyf ſayd hertes lyf souldan departed ſone therupon done dede body wel fayre carye tyl come kayre worthelyche bygraue lordes whiche wolden ſaue regne whiche deſolate brynge good eſtate parlement ſet anone herkne fel therupon yong lord worthy knyght rome vpon ſame nyght morowe trete ſhold vnto bachyler told counſeyll ryng • lle ſheweth thurgh whiche yt ſhall ſeyth kynges doughter wedde ſoo rynge leyd wedde told hyr fadre honde man ſhe fonde ſhold • ym toke vnto lord thus ſeyth ſtant record man wote hath ring bachyler vpon thyng ere entent l • yde thought ſeyde feyneth • fals vyſage glad courage ſ • another wyſe theſe old philoſophr • wyſe wryten vpon thylk whyle may beſt man begyle whome man hath moſt credence byfelle euydence toward yong lord rome bachyler whiche nome lord nyght ſlepte ryng whiche mayſter kepte oute purs awere dede put another ſtede morow court ſet yong lady forth fet whome lordes done homage maryage treten axen wylle ſhe whiche thought fulfylle fadre heſt mater sayd openly men may charge whiche hyr fadre bad tho lord rome glad droughe toward purs anone al nought gone bachyler hath forth drawe axeth therupon lawe ſhe hym hold couenaunt tokne ſo ſuffyſaunt myght forſake netheles lord hath take quarelle ayene owne man thynge euer myght nought herd clayme vnanſuerd hath purpos fayled bachiler ſoo counſayled wedded thylk empyre crouned lord ſyre al lond hym hath receyued wherof lord whiche deceyued ſekenes thyrd morowe conceyued hath dedely ſorowe lay vppon deth ther whyle hym laſteth ſpeche breth ſende worthyeſt al londe eke beſt told hem al ſoth tho ſone heyre alſo themperour grete rome gyder come knyght ryght told hem al pleyne ca counſeyll tolde al wolde hath fayled mede good taketh none hede ſayth loue whiche wende haue aboue therupon letter wryte doth fadre wyte al mater ſtood bertely mood vnto lordes beſought telle lady bought hyr loue whiche another gladeth aud word hewe fadeth ſayd dieu lady ſwete lyf hath loſt kyndely hete lay dede ony ſtone wherof ſory many one none al ſo ſhe fals knyght degre areſted put hold openly told treſon whiche falle thorugh oute lond ſayden alle ſoth men ſuppoſe owne vntrouth hym ſhal depoſe ſeche euydence honour grete reuerence wherof myghten knowe ende themperour anone ſende letter whiche ſone wrote ſoth wote telle ſorow endeles yet haſt netheles vpon tale whiche herde ſtyward perſe ferde worthy romayns eke lyege traytor ſeke thyder come knyght hym hath confeſſid falſely hath hym bore wherof worthy lord lore tho ſayden ſom ſhold deye yet haue foūden ſuche weye ſhal dede perſe thus ſkyles dyuerſe cauſe coroned lond habandoned hym al though werr vnryght peyne hym dyght poynt ende graūten wel yt ſhal wende romayns rome ageyne thus acorded ful playne quyk body dede leue take forth lede ſupplaunt hath iuyſe wherof thou myght auyſe vpon informacyon touchend ſupplantacion thou ſone ſo take hede alſo ſupplaūt doth halue man fynde ſalue pleynly hele ſuche ſore hath ſhal euermore pryde enuye ioynt ſuffreth man good poynt may honoure let therupon yf ſhal ſet enſample holy chirche fynde ſupplaunt behynde god wote yf ſo crony que tyme go fynde tale concordable ſupplaunt whiche fable maner ſhal telle whylome thynges felle • ponit confeſſor exemplum contra iſtos cauſa dignitatis adquirende ſupplantatores et narrat qualiter papa bonefacius predeceſſorē ſuū celeſtinū papatu contractata circumuencione fraudulenter ſupplantauit sed qui potentes ſede deponit hu iuſmodi ſupplātacōm fraudem non ſuſ tinens ipſum ſic ſublime exaltatum poſtea profundi carceris miſeriam proici fame que ſiti cruciari nec nō ab hu ius vite gaudijs doloroſa morte ſupplantari permiſit rome hath ofte falle vyker generall alle hem yt lyeuen criſtes feyth iſts al whiche none ſeyth hath ſhett worldes eye who name yf ſhal ſpecyfye hyght pope nycholas thus paſſed cardynals wold ſaue forme lawe conclaue gone cheſe newe pope couthe agrope hath eche hem ſayd entent tyl laſt aſſent vpon holy good recluſe whiche ful goſtely vertuſe pacyence ſympleſſe hath ſet hym hyghe nobleſſe thus pope canonyſed grete honour intronyced vpon channce falle name celeſtyn men calle whiche notyfyed bulle holy chirche fulle al londes magnyfyed euery worſhip enuyed thylk tyme ſen • pope whome mene choſe ſet ſyde cardynal thylk tyde whiche papate hath long deſyred therupon gretely hath conſpyred ſyghe fortune fayled whiche long tyme trauayled ylke fyre whiche ethna brēneth thorugh woful hert renneth whiche reſembled enuye wherof supplaunt trecherye engendred netheles feyneth loue feyneth pe outward doth reuerence al within conſeyence thorugh fals ymagynacyon thought supplantacyon therupon wonder wyle wrought thylke whyle fel ſo lygnage clergyon yonge age whome chamber affaited cardynal tyme hath waited wordes ſly queynt whiche couth lyghtely peynt ſhope clerk whiche telle toward pope duelle within chambre nyght lay preuy wyght toward pope nyghtes tyde may man flee ſhal tyde cardynal whiche thought gyle vpon day whan whyle yong clerk hym took made hym ſwere vpon book told hym wylle forth al trompe bra hath hym take bad hym ſhal ſaye tyme awayte take ryght good kepe pope faſt ſlepe none man ny thou ſo ſly thorugh oute trompe ere fro heuen though voys ſowne ſuche prolacyon medytacyon therof may make vnderſtonde though goddes ſonde wyſe thou ſhalt ſex thylk eſtate awey pope whiche ſtant honoured ſhal ſoule ſocoured thylk worſhip laſt heuen whiche ſhal euer laſt clerk hath herd forme ho pope ſhold enforme toke cardynal leue goth hym home tyl eue pryuely trompe hedde tyl pope bedde mydnyght knew pope ſlepte blew within trompe thurgh yt wal told maner ſhal papacye leue take fyrſt eſtate thus awake holy pope hath made thryes wherof dyuers fantaſyes vpon grete holyneſſe within hert gan impreſſe pope ful innocence conceyueth conſcyence goddes wyl ceſe wyſe may releſe hye eſtate wote nought thus within hym ſelf thouȝt ſtylle memorye tyl cam conſiſtorye preſence hem alle axeth yf ſo byfalle ony pope chefe ſholde lawe ſuffre wolde ſeten al ſtylle herde none whiche poynt anſuerde purpoos ment man knewe entent whiche ſhope gyle cardyual ſame whyle al openly wo • de pleyne seyth yf pope wol ordeyne ſuche lawe wrought myght cheſe elles nought ſayd done pope anone vpon ca papal auctoryte hath made youe decre lawe confermed due forme al affermed innocent whiche deceyued papacye anone hath weyued reuounced reſygned eke thyng ſeke vndernethe ſuche iape hath hym ſelf ſo ſhape hou euer hym ſeme myter dyademe hath thorugh ſupplantacyon confyrmacyon vpon fortune grace name cleped boneface vnder vyſer enuye lo hyd trecherye whiche hath begyled many one ſuche counſeyll ther may non whiche treſon conſpyred ny lyke ſpark fyred vp roofe whiche throwe lyeth hyd tyl whan yt wyndes blowe blaſeth oute euery ſyde boneface whiche hyde trecherye ſupplaunt hath openly made auannt papacye hath wonne thyng wrong gonne may neuer ſtonde wel ende pryde ſhal bowe bende ſheteth ful ofte oute weye thus pope whome ſeye ſtode hyghe whele ſuffre hym ſelf wele enuye whiche loueles pryde whiche lawebes ſuche tempeſtes made hym erre charyte goth herre vpon myſgouernaunce agaynſt lowys kyng fraunce toke quarel oultrage ſayd ſhold done homage vnto chirche bodely wyſt thyng ſhold doo ſo grete ſeruyce world ſuche wyſe withſtood wrong demaūd nought pope may commaund kyng wol pope obeye pope tho al weye may worche vyolence hath ſent bulle ſentence curſyng enterdyt kyng vpon wrongful plyȝt kepe regne fro ſeruage counſeyled baronage myght ſhal withſtōde thus cauſe take honde ſayden papacye honoure magnyfye al euer ſpyrytual pryde temporal boneface perſone ayene ylke wrong allone wolden ſtonde debate thus man nought ſtate frenſſhe ſhopen myght greue fel ther knyght syre gwilliam de langaret whiche vpon cauſe ſet therupon took route men armes rood oute long awayte laye aſpyede vpon daye pope auynyon ſholde ryde oute toun vnto ponniforge whiche caſtel prouynce vpon weye rood knyght whiche houed abood embuyſſhed vpon horſbak al ſodenlyche vpon hym brak hath hym brydel ſeſed ſayde thou whiche haſt dyſeſed courte fraunce thy wrong thou ſhalt ſynge another ſong thyn enterdyte thy ſentence ayene thyn owne conſeyence afcer thou ſhalt fele grope pleyne nought ageyne pope thylk name honourable thou whiche haſt deceyuable trecherours al thy werke thou boneface thou proude clerke myſl • der papacye thy fals body ſhal abye ſuffre hath deſerued lo thus ſupplātour ſerued hym lad fraunce ſetcen hym penaunce within toure hard bondes honger hondes ece dyed god wote whome wrytyng yet regyſtred man maye whiche ſpeketh ſayth manere thy entre lyke foxe ſlyghe thy regne alſo pryde hyghe lyche lyon rage laſt thy paſſage thy deth houndes lyke suche letter cronyke proclamed court rome wherof wyſe enſample nome yet ferforth dare rede af men beware loke wel algate none owne eſtate tranſlate holy chirche degre frāude ne ſubtylyte thylk aaron honour took shal none receyue ſeyth book becleped ſhal thynken ca day whiche may reſon bothe nature helpe euery man cure kepe symon fro folde nota de prophecia ioachim quanti meranarij ſunt ouile dei tuas aures mei narracionibus fedare nolo ioachym thylk abbot tolde ſuche dayes ſholden falle comonlyche place alle chapman ſuche mercery fraude ſupplantary many ſholden bye ſelle ne may ſhame teſte foule ſynne man • god forbede ſo oure dayes ſeyth yf clerk ware feyth chapmanhode ſuche feyre remenaunt mote nedes empeyre al world bylongeth whan holy chirche wrongeth thyng ſhal netheles mannes owne eye enuye preferred hath conſcyence ſo dyfferred man loketh vyce whiche modre malyce thylk fals enuye whiche cauſeth many trecherye may another ſee gracious ſhal ſtonden myght yf hynder ſuche wyght wel nyghe oueral vyce ſo general qualiter ioab princeps milicie dauid inuidie cauſa abner ſubdole inter fecit et qualit achitofell ab hoc qd cuſy conſilio abſolon preferebatur attenſo inuidia laqueo ſe ſuſpēdit enuye thylk vnhap drough ioab deceypt ſlough abnet drede ſhold kyng dauyd ſuche ennye alſo felle thylk fals achitofelle counſeylle ach • ued ſawe cuſy byleued abſolon hym forſake henge hym ſelf vpon ſtake senec wytneſſeth openly enuye propyrly court comon wenche halt tauerne ſhence drynke whiche maketh hert brēne doth wytt rēne euery wey compaſſe myght al paſſe whiche thorugh vnkyndeſhyp enuyeth euery falauſhip thou myght wel knowe ſee vyce ſuche fyrſt toward god abhomynable mankynde vuprofytable ben worth fewe ſhal reſon proue ſhewe inuidie ſtumilus ſine cauſa ledit abortus nam ſine temptante crimine crimen habet non eſt huius opus tempture cupdinis archum dum que facies veneris ethnica flamina vorat abſ que rubore gene palles quies fuſtus obū brat frigida nature c •• mēbra docēt hic deſcribit confeſſor naturain inuidie tam amore quam aliter ſecundum proprietatem vicij enuye yf ſhal deſeryue ſhapely wyue erthe among woman hym matere wherof myght pleſaunce fyrſt heuy contenaunce ſemeth euer vnglad able eke brenneth withynne kynde may proufyte wynne wherof ſhold loue pleaſe thylk blode ſhold haue eaſe regne among moyſt veynes drye thylk vnkyndely peynes thorugh whiche enuye fyred ay thus reſon proue may toward loue enuye nought wyſe yf beſought vpon ſyde euer falle werſt vyce alle whiche hym ſelf hath moſt malyce vnderſtonde euery vyce som cauſe hath wherof groweth enuye man knoweth fro whens cam oute helle thus wyſe clerkes telle ſpyryt malyce wey kynde vyce tempted ſuche waye enuye hath kynde put waye malyce hath ſturyng wherof maketh bakbytyng hym ſelf therof dyſeaſed may ther kynde pleaſed ay enuyeth ayene hym ſelf plenyeth thus ſtant enuyt good eſpeyr ben hym ſelf deuels heyr whiche next lyche fortheſt heuen ryche may neuer wone thy good dere ſone thou wold fynde ſyker weye lone put enuye aweye myn holy fadre reſon wolde vyce eſche ſhold yet ſtrengthe courage ye wold auauntage therof ſet recouere grete deſyre vyce myght flee vnderſtonde ſone ſee phyſyk ſeke vertues vyces eke vyces wold eſche mote reſon ſewe vertues thylk weye may vyces done aweye gydre maye duelle water welle fyre abateth malyce ryght ſo vertu fordoth vyce ayene enuye charyte whiche • modre pyte maketh man hert tendre may malyce engendre hym incline therin courage tempred ſo though myght hym ſelf releue yet wold another greue rather pleſaunce bereth hym ſelf greuaunce fayne wold another caſe wherof ſone thyn eaſe • • ne tale whiche rede vnderſtond wel rede hic ponit confoſſor exemplum de virtute cartatis centrum inuidi et narrat de conſtantino e lene filio ſuo qiu cum imperij romani dig nitatem obtinuerat morbo lepre • fectus medici pro ſanitate recuperanda ipſum ſanguine • puerorum moſeulorum balneare prepe ſuerant ſed cum numera multitudo matrum cum filijs huiuſmodi medicine cauſa circuitu palacij affuiſſet imperator que corum gemitus clamores percepiſſet caritate motus ingemiſcens ſic agit vere ipſe eſt dominus qui ſe facit ſeruum pietatis et dictis ſtatum ſuum cuncti potentis medele commuttens ſui ipſiꝰ morbum pocius quam infancium mor tem benignus elegit vnde ipſe quo • paganꝰ lepreſus extiterat ex vnda baptiſmatis renatꝰ vtrinſ que materie tā corporis que anime diuine miraculo conſecutus eſt ſalutem imong bokes latyn fynde wryte cōſtātyn worthy emperour rome suche infortunes hym come luſty age lepre caught vyſage ſo forth ouer al aboute myght ryden oute left ſhelde ſpere myght hym beſtere holde hym chambre cloſe thorugh al world fame aroſe grete clerkes ben aſſent come commaaundement trete vpon lordes hele long geder dele vpon medycyne appoynten hem determyne maner ſtood wold hym bathe childes blode within ſeuen yere age ſayen ſhold ſuage lepre al vyolence whiche knewe accidence wey kynde falle therto acorden alle fynal concluſyon tolden oppynyon themperour anone counſeyl toke therupone letter ſeales oute ſend euery lond aboute yong child ſeche whoos blood ſayd ſhold leche themperours maladye ynough wepe crye among modres herd wofully cauſe ferd netheles mote bowe thus woman ther come ynowe child ſoukend theyr tete many teres lete hem lyef hem lothe woman child bothe paleys forth brought many ſory hertes thought hem whiche body bore child ſo forlore within whyle ſhold ſee modres wepe degre many hem ſwoune falle yong babyes cryeden alle noyſe aroſe lord herde loked oute ferde ſawe ſayd abrayd oute ſlepe thus ſayd thou dyuyne purueaunce whiche euery man balaunce kynde haſt formed lyche pore bore ryche dyeth ſame wyſe vpon fool vpon wyſe seken eſſe hele enter comune may eſchewe fortune whiche kynde hath lawe ſett ſtrengthe beaute ben ſet euery man lyche fre ſhe profereth degre dyſpoſycyon bodely complexyon eke ſoule reſonable pore child bore able vertu kynges ſone euery man owne wone luſte aſſaye vyce vertue chefe maye thus ſtand al men fraunchyſed eſtate deuyſed ſomme worſhyp rycheſſe ſome pouerte dyſtreſſe one lordeth another ſerueth yet euery man deſerueth world yeueth yeftes certes hath grete matere good condycyon whiche hath ſubiectyon men ben ſemblaunce eke toke remembraunce made lawe kynde wolde euery man lawe bynde bad man ſuche wold toward hym ſelf ryght ſuche ſhold toward another done alſo thus worthy lord al tho set balaunce owne eſtate hym ſelf ſtood debate thought good ſee ſo mochel man blood ſpylt cauſe hym alone ſawe alſo grete mone moders vnglade wo childre made wherof hert tendreth ſuche pyte within engendreth hym leuer cheſe owne body leſe ſee ſo grete mordre wrought vpon blood gylteth nought thus pyte whiche toke al lech forſoke put hym oute auenture al goddes cure ſayth wol mayſter mote ſeruaunt pyte ferforth ouercome charyte hath nome counſeyll offycers bad vnto treſorers treſour al aboute departe among pouer route wymmen chyldren bothe wherof myght hem fede clothe ſothly borne home ageyne withoute loſſe ony greyne thorugh charyte thus dyſpendeth good wherof amendeth pouer peple countreuayleth harme hem ſo trauayleth thus woful nyghtes ſorow ioye torned morowe al thankyng āl blyſſyng whiche erſt wepyng curſyng theſe woman gone home glad ynough echone ioye lough preyd lordes hele whiche hath releſed quarele hath owne wyl forſake charyte goddes ſake thou ſhalt god hath wrouȝt matere doth al equyte hym wrought charyte ayeneward charytous pyte pytous neuer knowe yet charyte geth vnaquit nyght leyd ſlepe hyghe god wold hym kepe seynt peter ſeynt poule hym ſende whome wold lepre amende two hym ſlepend appere fro god ſayd manere conſtantyn thou haſt ſerued pyte thou haſt pyte deſerued thy thou ſhalt ſuche pyte haue god thorugh pyte wol ſane thou ſhalt ſo double hele fynde fyrſt bodelyche kynde • nd thy woful ſoule alſo thou ſhalt hole two thou ſhalt deſpeyre thy lepre ſhal empeyre tyl thou wylt ſende therupon vnto mount celyon sylueſtre clergye gyder duellen companye drede whiche many day haſt ben foo cryſtes lay haſt deſtroyed mochel ſhame prechours holy name thou haſt ſomdele appeſed thy god good dede pleſed thou thy pyte haſt bywaryd vpon blood whiche yu haſt ſpared thy thy ſaluacyon thou ſhalt haue informacyon suche sylueſtre ſhal teche nedeth none leche emperour whiche al herd graunt mercy lord anſuerd wol ye ſay one thyng wold pray ſhal telle vnto sylueſtre youre name eſtre hym told hyght forth al oute offhis ſyght paſſen vp heuen awoke oute ſweuen clepeth men come anone told dreme therupone ſuche wyſe hem telleth mount sylueſtre duelleth haue haſt ſought foūdē hem brouȝt themperour whiche told ſweuen elles wold silueſtre hath herd ye king ryght ioyeful thyng • hym bygan al wyt techen vpon holy wryt fyrſt mankynde • ore hyghegod therfore ſone ſend aboue whiche born mannes loue owne choys toke deth vpon croys ḡraue byloke hath helle broke toke hem yt lyeue make v ful byloue veray goddes ſone ayene kynde mannes wone fro deth roſe thyrd day wold wel may ſtyghe vp fadres euene fleſſhe blood heuene ryght ſo ſame forme fleſſhe blood ſhal reforme tyme cometh quyk dede thylk woful day drede euery man ſhal take dome well mayſter groome myghty kynges retenue day maye ſtonde value worldly ſtrengthe defende euery man mote entende ſtonde vpon owne dedes leue mennes nedes day may counſeyl auayle pledour ple ſhal fayle ſentence ylke daye maye none appele ſet delaye may gold iuge plye ne ſhal ſoth trye fetten euery man vp ryght wel plow man knyght leud man grete clerk shal ſtonde vpon owne werk ſuche fonnde tho suche ſhal euermo may peyue releſed may ioye encreſed endeles haue • ſhal receyue one two thus sylueſter ſawe ground al newe lawe grete deuocyon precheth fro poynt poynt techeth vnto emperour ſayth hyghe creatour hath vnder fonge charyte wrought ſuche pyte child honde thus lord hath vnderſtōde al thyng ferde vnto sylueſtre anſuerde al hool hert ſeyth redy feyth ſo veſſel whiche blood made sylueſtre ſtood clene water welle al haſt lete felle ſet conſtantyn therynne al naked vp chynne whyle begonne lyght though ſonne fro heuen place come took cryſtendome euer among holy tale lyke fyſſhes ſcales fellen hym efte tyl ther thyng lefte al grete maladye wold hym puryfye hyghe god hath made hym clene left thyng ſene hath hym cleuſed two body ſoule alſo tho knewe emperour dede cryſtes feyth drede ſende anone lettres oute lete cryen al aboute vpon peyne deth mā weyue baptyſme ne receyue moder quene eleyne ſend ſo bytwene hem tweyne treten cyte al cryſtned ſhe forth al emperour whiche hele hath foūd within rome anone lete found two chirches whiche dyd make peter poule ſake whome vyſyon yaf therto poſſeſſion lordſhip worldly good ſo wylle good toward pope franchyſe yet hath proued wyſe ſee worchyng dede crony que thus rede anone hath made yefte voys herd hyghe lefte whiche al rome adrad ſayd day venym ſhad holy chirche temporal whiche medleth ſpyrytal ſtant degre yet may man ſoth ſee god maye amende wylle therto none ſkylle go ther̄ bygan charyte may helpe man bothe worldes haue ſayd yf thou haue ere layd ſone thou myght vnderſtonde charyte take honde▪ • foloweth mochel grace thy yf thou wolt purchace thou enuye fle acqueynte charyte whiche vertu ſouerayne fadre ſhal peyne e • ſample whiche ye told al myn hert haue withold ſhal euermore eſchewe enuye wel haue myſdo ye • e penaunce go ouer matere ſhryfte whyle ye ſytten pryuete betwene v tweye axe ther preye confeſſor good ſone thy lore wol telle thou ſhalt ſo vyces knowe ful knowe thou myȝt hem wel better eſchewe cauſe thynke ſewe forme matere ſewend thou ſhalt whiche vyce ſtant next whan thou woſt thou ſhalt deuyſe thou myght thy ſelf better auyſe explicit liber ſecundus incipit liber tercius ira ſuis paribus eſt par fu rijs acherontis quo furo • ad tempus nil pi • tati habet ira melācolicos ani mo perturbat vt equo • ure ſui pondus nulla ſtatera tenet omnibus cauſis grauat ira inter amantes illa magi facili ſorte grauamen agit eſi vbi vir diſcors leuiter que repugnat amori sepe loco ludi fletus ad os venit hic • ercio libro tractat ſuper quin que ſpeciebus ire quarum prima melancoli •• dicitur cuius confeſſor primo deſcribens amanti ſuper eodem conſequenter opponit thou vyces leſt knowe ſone hath vnknowe fro fyrſte men theyr ſwerdes groūde ther none vpon ye groūde vyce foreyn fro ye lawe wherof many good felawe hath dyſtraught ſodeyn chaū •• yet kynde pleſaunce doth moſt acheueth pur •• o moſt kynde greueth whiche outr conſcyence enemy vnto pacyence name one ſeuene whiche ofte hath ſet world vneuent cleped cruel ire whoos herte euermore fyre ſpeke amys bothe ſeruauntes ben euer wrothe good fadre telle thyng ire sone oure englyſſhe wrath hote whiche hath wordes ay ſo hote al man pacyence fyred vyolence hym hath euer fyue seruauntes helpen hym ſeryue fyrſt hem melancolye cleped whiche companye honderd tymes oure wol angry beſt loure man wote cauſe ſone ſhryue thy haſt thou malencolyen fadre ye ſeynt iulyen vntrewe wordes vſe may therof excuſe al maketh loue wel wote whiche myn hert euer hote brenne doth glede wrath may ſpede thus ful ofte day nought sauf onlyche myn owne thought ſo ſeluen wrothe ſo game gothe men glade wel vnglade men game torneth pure grame thus ſelf oppreſſed thought whiche haue impreſſed al wakyng dreme mete hyr alone mete prayd ▪ hyr ſom good anſuere wol gladly ſwere ſeyth nay withouten oth thus waxe within wroth outward al affrayed ſo dyſtempered ſo eſ •• ayed thousand tymes day ſowneth myn eres nay whiche ſhe ſayd fore thus wyttes forlore namely whan begynne rekne ſelf within many yeres ben agone syth haue truly loued one neuer took hyr hede euer lyche ſpede fole hyr dele hap al hele thynketh ay lenger ferre bringeth gladſhip erre wherof wyttes ben empryred ſayth al diſpeyred fynally muſe thynk ſhe wol refuſe • anger ſo beſtad al world myght glad laſteth al vp ſo doune ioye caſteth • forther ne may lady ſe redy wrathe fo touchyng lathe tornyng ſere wode doth wylde ſee ſo melancolyous ther ny ſeruaunt myn hous ne none tho aboute eche hem ne ſtant doute wene wold raue anger ſee haue ſo wondre laſſe ſeen ouerpaſſe▪ fadre yf ſo betyde approche ony tyde place lady hyr lyketh wy ſpeke goodly word vntome al gold rome ne couth wroth al myn anger ouer goth glad preſence hyr al offence foryete though nought ouer glad thought and▪ netheles ſoth telle • ene word yf ſoo byfelle thylk tyme ſyghe ſhe myſcaſt hyr eye ſhe lyſt nought loke therof good hede toke anone fyrſt eſtate torne alſo mate euer aſyche wycke thus myn hond ayen prycke hurte haue many day go ſo forth goo may fulofte bytyng lyppe make vnto ſelf whyppe whiche many chele •• woful hert ſo bete al wyttes ben vnſofte wroth ofte al melancolye whiche groweth fantaſye loue wol loute bere forth angry ſno wte ful many tymes yere fadre ye ſytten loues ſtede yow byſeche ſom enſample ye teche wherof may ſelf appeſe confeſſor sone thyn hertes eſe ſhal fulfylle thy prayer thou myght better ler • meſchyef vyce ſtereth whiche angre forbereth wherof hym thynketh ſobre hym thynketh vpon foly dede poynt tale rede hic ponit confeſſor exemplum cō tra iſtos qcū vires amoris nō sūt realiter experti contra al • o amantes malen • ol ••• ſ • ueritate neuer chyd telle forth yf ther touchyng vnto wrathes lore demoui • eſt odium quaſi ſcrib • cui dabit ira • teriam ſcripti cordis ad antrum ſui non laxa • amor odij que frena reſtringunt nec ſecreta ſui iuris adire ſciuit hic tractat confeſſor de tercia ſpecie ire que odium dicitur cuius natura om̄s ire inimicicias ad mentem reducēs illas vſ que ad tempꝰ vindicte velut scriba demonis cordis witholde • yet ought ye tolde fadre good feyth ſone yi fadre nay ye leue leſt ſone thou ſhalt ha •• wrath ſhewend loug tyme gaderend duelleth hert loken tyl ſee tyme wroken ſheweth tempeſt ſodeyn wylde beſt whiche wote thyng mercy ſone art thou knowen good fadee wene wote ſonidele ye mene dare ſaufly make othe lady neuer loth wol ſwere netheles hate gylteles lady plye fro day day mercy crye ſhe mercy leyth ſhrote wordes ſeyth though lady loue algate tho wordes mote nedes hate wold al dyſpent fer oute londe went hereafter ſhold hem yet loue lady dere thus hate ye may ſee bytwene lady word word hate hyr loue ſo ſhal betyde loue forthermore wol ſhryue haue hated al lyue ianglers whiche enuye ben euer redy lye fals compaſſement ful often haue made ſhent hyndred ful oftyme canſe wyſte • yme onlyche hyr owne thought thus ful ofte haue bought lye dranke wyn wold happe ſuche myn ſo ſhryue ne may foryeue tyl ſee debate loue myn eſtate myghten owne deme loke wel ſhold hem queme hyndre man ſhold alle abyde hym ſelf wold thyder ryde cam fore tonne hath tale thus bygonne al heyl ſeyth man art thou quod ſuche one thou ſeeſt kynge whiche wordes wyſe age wold deſpyſe ſayth fadre praye thou wolt cauſe ſaye thy man man syre kyng quod yf thou wylt yes ſeyth kyng quod ſoth thyng syth fyrſt reaſon vnderſtood knewe euyll good wyl whiche body moueth who werkes god reproueth haue reſtreyned conqueroure worldes good whiche may laſt thou hygheſt euer lyche faſt thou reaſon haſt wynne thus thy wylle cauſe ſynne thy lord whome thou ſerueſt wherof thou lytel thank deſerueſt kyng yt thus anſuerd thyng wroth herd hyghe wordes whiche ſayde gooodly wordes thus prayde hym wold telle name quod thylk ſame whiche men dyogenes calle tho ye kyng ryght glad alle herd ofte fore man ſo therfore ſayde wyſe dyogene ſhal thy grete wyt ſene thou ſhalt yefte haue worldes good yu wolt craue quod houe ſonne lete ſhyne tonne thou bynemeſt thylk yifte lyeth thy myȝt ſhyfte none good nedeth kyng whome euery coūtrey dredeth lo thus enformed wherof ſone thou myght lere thy wylle ſhal beleued wyt releued thou haſt ſayd thy ſelf thy wyl thy mayſter thorugh whiche thyn hertes thought within euer contak werre helpeth ryde couetyſe worldes pryde ſlee worldes men aboute beſtes whiche gone ther oute ony lyf whiche reſon ought wel▪ knowe man ne ſhold thorugh tyrannye lyche beſtes dye tyl kynde wold hym paſſe oue • grete ſee werre ſlee saraȝyn lawe sone myn preche ſuffre feyth haue herd goſpel ſeyth ſlee nought cryſt owne deth hath bought al men made hem fre tokne parfyte charyte taught hym ſelue dede theſe twelue apoſtles went aboute holy feyth preche oute wherof deth ſondry place ſuffre ſo god grace feyth cryſt hath made aryſe yf wold wyſe werre haue bought creaūce yet ſtonde balaunce may prouen dede man cronykes rede fyrſt holy chirche hath weyued preche hath ſwerd receyued wherof werres begonne grete partye wonne cryſtes feyth ſtant myſwent god doo therof amendement wote beſt ſone yf thou wylt lyue reſt conſcyence wel aſſyſed er thou ſlee wel auyſed man tellen v clerkes hath god aboue al erthely werkes ordeyned pryncypal eke ſoule ſpecyal made lyche godhede ſyt wel taken hede loke euery ſyde er thou falle homycyde whiche ſynne ſo general wel nye ſtant oueral holy chirche elles al whyle ſo wdorl mote nede fare amys the▪ whele pyte thorugh couetyſe worldes good defouled ſhedyng blo • remenaunt folk aboute vnnethe ſtonden ony doute werre eche ſlee al worth ſtre charyte wherof prechen thyng techen thus blynde conſcyence pe •• hath loſt thylk euydence whiche cryſt vpon erthe taught may mē ſee mordre manſlauȝt lyche dayes olde whan men ſynnes bought ſolde grece afore cryſtes feyth rede cronyke ſeyth touchend af mater thus thylk tyme peleus owne broder phocus ſlough gold ynough ſynne dyſpenſed gold wherof compenſed achaſtꝰ whiche venus pryeſt aſſoylled ca al repentaunce bokes make remembraūce tellyth med • e alſo ſhe ſlough ſones two egeus ſame plyte hath made hyr hyr ſynne quyte ſone eke amphyoras who ryght name almeus moder ſlough eryphele achylo preſt bokes recorden certayne ſomme gold acorden thylk horryble ſynful dede aſſoylled thus mede worldes goode fallyth ofte homycyde ſet alofte lyf ſhal knowe hem ſuche thynges wyrche alſo holy chirche lete ſuche ſynnes paſſe quyte wol hem acquyte dedely werres make wold enſample take lawe whiche naturel weye kynde weth wel homycyde degre whiche werreth ayene charyte among men ſhold duelle foer bokes telle ſ • che al world ryche men ſhal fynde one lyche beſt wyl take preye ſyth kynde hath ſuche weye wondre man whiche kynde hath reſon wol eyther laſſe kynde reſon ouerpaſſe ſlee hym ſemblable man reſonable kynde honeſte worſe beſte nota ſecundum solinum contra ho •• iadium de natura cuiuſdam aius faci • ad ſimilitudinem humanam habentis qiu cum de preda ſua hominem myta flauium occident▪ vident que aqua ſunile ſibi occiſum ſtatim pro delo 〈◊〉 moritur among bokes finde solinꝰ ſpeketh wōdre kinde whiche wol drynke take whiche viſage ſeeth make hath ſlayne anone thynketh myſdede forthynketh gretely pure ſorowe lyueth tyl morowe enſample may wel ſe men ſhal homycyde eſchewe euer mercy good take yf lawe hath forſake iuſtyce ageyne fnl oftyme haue herd ſeyne amonges werres hadden ſom whyle cauſe ladden mercy myȝt haue ſlayn wherof fayn ſone yf thou wolt recorde vertu myſerycorde thou ſyghe neuer thylk place vſed lak grace euery lawe euery kynde mannes wyt mercy bynde namely worthy knyghtes ſtonde mooſt vpryghtes ben moſt myghty greue ſholden thenne moſt releue hym whome myȝten ouerthrowe enſample may men knowe hic ponit confeſſor exemplum de pietate contra homicidium et narrat qualiter achilles vna cum thephalo filio ſuo contra regem meſee qui tunc theucer vocabatur bellum regni ſui heredem libera volū tate conſtituit may faylen mede hath mercy rede cronyke fynd thus whan achilles telaphus ſone ward troye fel hem come ayene thoucer kyng meſe make warre leſe lond wolde regne theucer pnt oute regne thus march aſſaylle theucer yaf hem bata ylle foughten bothe ſydes faſte ſo happeth laſte worthy greke achilles kyng among al ches cruel felle ſwerd hond hym felle ſmote hym dethes woūde vnhorced fel grounde achilles vpon hym alyght wold anone wel myght haue ſlayn hym place thephalus fadre grace hym beſought pyte prayth wold late hym caſt ſheld bytwene hem two achilles axeth hym ſo thephalus cauſe tolde ſeyth mochel holde whylome theucer ſtede grete grace ſocour hym dede ſayth hym wold acquyte prayth fadre reſpyte achilles tho withdrough hond al power lond yt ſawe hyr kyng thus take fled hath f • ld forſake grekes vnto chaas falle mooſt part alle countre lordes grete took wonne grete beyete anone vyctorye kyng whiche memorye vpon grete mercy thought laphus toward hym wrouȝt preſence al londe took hym fayre honde wyſe gan ſeye ſone mote double weye loue deſyre thyn encrees fyrſt thy fadre achilles whylome ful many day ſhold fare amys reſcouſe dyd quarele kepte al myn eſtate hele ſo ther falle dyſtaunce among v yet remembraunce haue mercy whiche dede than▪ thou ſtede gentylnes frauncheſſe haſt mercy ſame geſſe wol ony tyme loſt thou haſt byme ſo fortune falle yet ſtant truſt abouen alle mercy whiche fynde thou wolt • e kynde ſuche myn eſpeyr ſone myn yre receyue al lond yeue ſeſe thyn honde wyſe accorde cauſe myſerycorde lordes obeyſaunce thelaphus purueaunce made ſo coroned thus mercy reguerdoned whiche theucer dyde fore loo enſample made therfore thou myght take remembraunce ſone thou ſeeſt chaunce men paſſyon take pyte compaſſyon lete thynge leef whiche another man greef yf thou deſyre ſtonde ayene vyce ire counſeyl pacyence take thy conſcyence mercy thy gouernour ſhalt thou • fynde rancour wherof thyn herte ſhal debate homycyde ne hate cheſte melancolye thou ſhalt ſofte companye withoute conteck foolhaſt elles myght thou long waſt thy tyme thou haue thy wylle loue wedyr ſtylle men preyſe blame tempeſtes fadre wol heſtes poynt ye haue tauȝt toward ſelf better ſaught thenke bewayle whyle lyne moche ſhryne wrathe al circumſtaunce yeue ye lyſt penaunce axe forther lyf yf wyſe gyltyf ony thyng toucheth ſynne ſone hym longeth fadre tho poyntes longeth wyte pleynly mene maye ſhryue clene herkne ſhal ye pointes deuyſe vnderſtonde wel myn appryſe ſhryfte ſtant value hym wol hym vertue leue vyces folye wynd word moyſes thorugh enchauntynge somtyme ethyope made tharbys wedded hade whiche ryng bare oblyuyon name reſon fynger ſate anone loue ſo forya • e neuer knowe ſo fel ylke throwe tharbys hond knowlechyng within caſtel ſtronde demophon cam vp londe • hylles ſhe hyght yong age bothe ſtature • yſage al hyr beſt veſemeth demophon ryȝt wel quemeth come ſhe made hym chere ſuche manere luſty knyght ne myght aſterte ne ſ • hyr herte within day twoo thought euer go wold aſſaye fortune gan quene comune goooly wordes ere put hyr oute fere ſwore hath trouthe plyght euer hyr owne knyght thus hyr ſtylle abode whyle ſhyp anker rood bad ynough tyme ſpace ſpeke loue ſeke grace lady herd al ſayde ſwore prayde whiche enchauntement innocent though trouthe feyth leueth al euer ſeyth fortune ſholde graunteth hym al wolde thus tyme ioye tyl ſhold go • • e tho ſhe made mochel ſorowe trouth leyd ſorowe come yf lyue may ageyne within moneth day therupon kyſten bothe hym leef hym loth ſhyp goth forth went troye eftſone forſate ſhe whiche myght ſo tyde awayteth euermo caſt hyr eye vpon ſe • somtyme nay ſomtyme ye somtyme cam ſomtyme nought thus ſhe dyſputeth thought wote ſhe thynke may faſtend al long day derk nyght tho ſhe hath ſet vp lyght lanterne hyghe 〈◊〉 vpon toure ſhe goth ofte hope comyng ſhold ſee lyght brennyng wherof myght weyes ryght come ſhe nyght al nonght ſhe deceyued venus hath hyr hope weyued ſhewed hyr vpon ſky day faſt within lytel throwe dayes lyght ſhe myght knowe tho ſhe byhelde ſee large ſhe ſaw ther barge • e ſhyp 〈◊〉 fer ſhe may kenne doune fro tour ſhe gan renne herber al hyr one many wōder woful mone made lyf wyſt ſhe whiche al ioye myſt ſhe ſwouneth ſhe pleyneth face ſhe dyſt • yneth teres whiche welle ſtremes eyen felle ſhe myght euer one cleped vpon demephon ſayd cleped yerd yet demophon ſhame daye bereth name woful chaunce ferde anone demephon herde euery man ſpeche ſorowe tho ſeche gan ſlouthe banne al late thanne lo thus ſone myght thou wyte ayene vyde hou wryte man may harmes geſſe fallen thurgh foryetylneſſe wherof thy ſhryft haue herd yet ſlouthe hou hath ferd wyſe thenke oppoſe thou haue gylt suppoſe dum plantare licet cultor qui n • cli git ortum si deſint feuctus imputat ipſe ſibi preterit iſta dy bona nec valebit illa ſecunda hoc caret exemplo lentus amore ſuo hic tractat confeſſor de vicijs necligencie cuius condicio •• idiam amplectens exēplair ther yet one ſecretayr cleped necligence whiche wol loke euydence wherof may beware fore hath cauſe lore wyſe hond helpe may maner bond fyrſt wold bynde thus euermore ſtant behynde thyng may amende ware ſeyth ende wold god knowe wherof beiaped mowe goth grete ſtede ſtole taketh hede maketh ſtable dore faſt thus euer pleyth caſt al ſhal ſaye hath maner • ke alſo hym lyſt lerne wyſe le ſett vertu pryſe hym lyketh whyle fayleth ful ofte gyle weneth ſeker ſtonde thus thou myght wel vnderſtōde ſone yf thou art ſuche loue thou myght come thyn aboue thou woldeſt wel acheue▪ amans myn holy fadre leue may wel ſauf conſcyence eycuſe neglygence towardes loue al wiſe though • e none wyſe truly amerous euer curyous hem beſt enforme knowen wyten al forme falleth vnto loues craft yet ne fond nought haft whiche myght vnto blade acorde neuer herd man recorde thyng myght auayle wynne loue withoute fayle yet ſo ferforth couthe neuer fynde man reſon ne kynde conthe teche ſuche arte ne fayled parte toward myn owne wyt contryue couthe neuer yet fynde ony ſe • yrneſſe myght leſſe loue make ſpede leueth wel withouten drede yf ther ſuche weye certaynly ſhal deye lerned long go wote wel none ſo netheles may wel ſoo rude degre eke wyttes ben ſoo dul ne may nought ful atteyne vnto ſo hyghe lo • e dar ſeye ouermore al though wyt ſtrong wyl along •• ſy nyght day lerne al lern emay hou myght loue wynne yet begynne wold make ende hou ſhal wende mooſt ſorowe dare take god borowe myn entendemēt none wyſe neclygent ſaye haue thy pur ſeynt charyte telle fadre yow ſemeth confeſſor good feyth ſone wel quemeth thou thy ſelf haſt thus acquyte toward vyce whiche noo wyte byde may houre loſt al may laboure long yere ſoo men ſeyne euer doth veyne thorugh ſlouthe neclygēce neuer ſuche ſcyence ne vertue whiche bodely ny deſtroyed loſt therby enſample hath ſoo bokes fynde wryte alſo hic contra vicium necligencie ponit confeſſor exemplum et narrat ꝙ cum pheton filius ſolis currum pa •• ſui per 〈◊〉 regere debuerat ad monitus patre vt equos ne deuiarent equa manu diligēciꝰ 〈◊〉 ipſe cōſ • liū pris ſua necligēcia pret •• ēs equos curru nimis baſſe errare permiſit vn de non ſolum incendio orbem inflammauit ſed ipſum de curru cadendem quoddam fluuium demergi ad inte •• tum cauſauit phebꝰ whiche ye ſōne hote ſhyneth vpon erthe hote cauſeth euery lyues helthe ſone al welthe whiche pheton hyght deſyreth modre conſpyreth whiche cleped clemene helpe counſeyl ſo fadre cart lede myght vpon fayre dayes lyght thyng prayde vnto fadre ſayde wold wel forth al thre poyntes bad ſpecyal vnto ſone al wyſe hym ſhold wel auyſe take weye lore firſt hors ſore ne pryk told reynes faſt hold alſo ryght ware maner ledeth chare myſtake gate vp auyſement algate ſhold bere ſyker weye lowe ne heye cart dryue ony throwe drede leſt ſhold ouerthrowe thus phebus ordynaunce toke pheton goueruaunce ſonnes cart whiche lad b • ſuche veyn glory ſet vpon hygh owne eſtate ne ſygh thorugh neglygence took none hede myght wel long ſpede hors withouten lawe cart lete aboute drawe hym lyketh wantonly laſt ſodenly reſon wold knowe fyry cart droue lowe fyreth al world aboute wherof al doute god helpe cryden ſuche vnhappes betyden phebus whyche ſawe neglygence pheton ayene defence chare hath dryue oute weye ordeyneth fel weye oute cart flood drowned lo ſtood hym ſo neglygent fro hyghe fyrmament wold goo lowe anone doune ouerthrowe hyghe eſtate vyce goo lowe ſeruyce greueth goo hyghe wherof tale • eeſye exemplum ſuper eodem de icharo filio didali carcere minotau • exiſtente cui dedalus vt inde eu • faret ala componens firmite • imunxit ne nimis alte propter ſolis ardorem aſcen deret▪ quod icharus ſua ngligēcia poſt ponens cum alcius ſublimatus f •• ſſet ſubito ad terram corruens expira •• fynde whylome dedalꝰ whiche ſone icharus hyght though hym thought loth ſuche pryſon mynotaurus aboute myghten nowher wenden oute bygonnen ſhape pryſon myght eſcape dedalus whiche fro youthe taught many craftes couthe fethers thynges hath made flee dyuers wynges hym ſone alſo whome yafe charge tho bad hym thynke therupon wynges ſet wax yf took flyght hyghe al ſodenlyche myght make melte ſonne thus al ydel neuer yett ne neuer ſhal whyle may goo ſone telle ſo haſt thou done beſyſhyp loue ladyſhyp hyr whiche thy lady fadre euer yet euery place euery ſtede ſo lady hath bede al myn herte obedyent reule forth cupyde myght meruayle ſuche wyght whiche tho luſty age deſyreth nouther maryage ne yet loue peramours whiche euer hath ben comon cours among hem luſty ſhewed hye hertes loweth fyry dart whiche throweth cupyde whiche loue god chaſtyſynge hath made rod dryue awey wantonneſſe soo within whyle geſſe ſuche chaunce ſporned al moo • ouertorned whiche fyrſte ſhe ſlowe manere fel thou ſhalt come moneth may wold walke vpon day ſonne aryſt woman fewe wyſt forthe ſhe went pryuely vnto park faſt al ſoft walkend vpon gras tyl ſhe cam ther laūde thorugh ran grete riuer thought hyr fayr ſayd wol abyde vnder ſhawe badde hyr woman withdrawe ſhe ſtood alone ſtylle thynke wylle ſawe ſwete floures ſpryng herd gladde foules ſynge ſawe beſtes kynde buk doo hert hynde male go femele ſo bygan quarele bytwene loue hyr owne hert whiche ſhe couthe aſtert ſhe caſt hyr eye aboute ſawe clad one ſute route ladyes come ryde long vnder wode ſyde fayre ambulend hors ſete al whyte fat grete echone ryde ſyde ſadeles ſuche pryde perles gold ſo wel begone ryche ſawe ſhe neuer none kyrtels cope ryche clothed al alyche departed euen whyte blewe al luſtes ſhe knewe embroudred oueral bodyes long ſmal beaute fayr vpon hyr face none erthely thyng may deface corownes theyr hedes bere eche hem quene al gold creſus halle leſt coronal hem alle myȝt haue bought worth thus come rydend forth kynges doughter ſawe yt tide pure abaſſhede drewe hyr aſyde held hyr cloos vnder abough lete hem ſtylle ryde inough thought auyce hem ſuche pryce worthy axe fro come bnt leuer worldes good wold haue wyſt ſtood put hyr hede lytel oute ſhe loked hyr aboute ſawe comend vnder lynde woman vpon hors behynde hors ſhe rood blak al • ene galled vpon back halted enc • oyed wherof woman annoyed thus hors ſory plyght al ſterre lyght amyddes front ſhe ſadel este wonder bad whiche woful woman ſat netheles ther ryche brydel none gold precious ſtones cote ſomdele tore aboute myddel tweuty ſcore hors halter wel mo ther hangen tyme tho thus ſhe cam lady nyghe thenne ſhe took better hede ſyghe woman fayr vylage freſſhe luſty yong tendre age ſo lady ſhe ſtood bethought hyr wel vnderſtood whiche come rydend tho tydynges couthe telle tho whiche ſhe ſawe fore ryde put hyr forth prayd hyr abide ſayd ſuſter lete ben ryden ben ſo rychely arrayed woman ſo cam eſmáyed auſuerde ful ſofte ſpeche ſayd madame ſhal teche theſe ar tho whylome seruauntes loue trouthe bere theyr hertes ſett fare wel may let madame go ſeruyor muſt haſt al wyſe thy madame yeue leue may long leue good ſuſter yet preye telle ye ſo beſeye theſe haltres thus begone madame whilome one fadre kyng ſlowe thyng lyſt loue obeye ful ſore obeye lome loue hors feble bad al tore myn array euery yere freſſhe may theſe luſty ladyes ryde aboute muſt nedes ſewe route maner ye ſee truſſe hyr haltres forth hors knaue none offyce ne haue hem thynketh worthy ſlowe loues lore able lere wold tale hem couthe loue teche trſſe byſeche fore ryche brydel ſerueth awey chere ſhe ſwerueth gan wepe thus ſhe told ryche brydel whiche ye behold ryche vpon myn hors hede madame afore dede luſty lyf felle myn herte ſtryf loue whiche ouercome therof lady ſyght tho fore hyr hert aflyght ſayd hyr ſelf allas ryght ſame caas lyue daye ſhal amende yf maye thus homeward lady went chaunged al hyr fyrſt entent within hyr hert gan ſ • bere ſhe haltres bondes thouȝt wold oute hōdes ſleyghte ſom maner eſcape ās couthe hym ſelf ſhape lykeneſſe adder ſlypt • oute hond forth ſkypte efte fyght wole borneth hym bole gan belwe ſuche ſoune though ye world ſlepe waken euer ſhold dyſſeuer fro hyr whome al lyght curſe alſo nyght al wylle courage ſaye awey thou black ymage whiche thy derck cloudy face maketh al worldes lyght deface cauſeth vnto ſlepe awey whiche mote gone aweye oute lady companye ſlepy nyght defye wold thou lay preſſe proſerpyne goddeſſe pluto helle kyng tyl ſee day ſpryng ſet ſlepe ryſſhe word ſyghe wyſſhe ſey ne day yet lady may beholde though efte thynke forthermore ſomme man hou nyght doth eaſe hath thyng yt may hym pleaſe long nyghtes ſyde fayle goo beſyde ſlepe wherof ſerueth whiche noman thank deſerueth gete hem loue ony place hynderer grace maketh hem dede throw ryght ſtok ouerthrowe ſo fadre wyſe ſlepy nyghtes deſpyſe euer myddes tale thynke vpon nyghtyngale whiche ſlepeth wey kynde loue bokes fynde thus laſt goo bedde yet myn hert lyeth wedde ſ • r • bere cam fro though departe w • l ſo bock may ſhet hym oute hym nedeth nought gone aboute perce may hard wal thus • e oueral hyr • ef hyr bed myn herte goth ſoftely taketh hyr arme feleth hou ſhe warme wyſſheth also body tho fele felyth thus ſelf tormente tyl dede ſlepe hente thouſand ſcore wel fore tormented ſlepe dreme ſhepe ne thynk wulle dretched fulle loue haue take kepe laugh wepe leſe wynne ende begynne otherwhyle dreme • te alone mete daunger left behynde ſlepe ſuche ioye fynde ne bede neuer awake heede take shal aryſe vpon morowe al
