proficiſcens •• ar • lō giue patria dimerſus fucrat • uno mitten • ridem nunciam ſuam partes chimerie ad domum ſompni iuſſit ꝙ ipſe alceone dicti regis vxori huiꝰ rei euentum per ſompnia certificaret quo facto al •• ona rem perſcrutans corpus mariti suij vbi ſuper fluctus mortuꝰ iactabatur inuenit que pro lore auguſtiata cupiens corpus amplec tere altum mare super ipsum proſi •• vnde dij miserti amborum corpus aues que ad huc alceones dicte ſunt ſubito conuerterunt fynde wryten poeſie ceyx kyng trocenye alceon wyfe whiche owne hertes lyfe hym loueth hath alſo broder whiche cleped tho dedalyon goddes fynde grace broders hele purchace myght reformed hath ben tranſformed purpos ende kyng redy wende whiche wold go ſhyp done hym felauſhyp wyf vnto ſee hym brought al hyr herte hym beſought tyme wold ſeyn thought come ageyne within ſayth two monethis day thus al haſt may took leue forth ſayleth wepend ſhe hyr self bewayleth torneth ther ſhe cam fro monethes ago whiche ſet comyng ſhe herd tydyng care ſeche wherof goddes byſeche tho ſhe bygan many wyſe iuno ſacryfyce aboue al moſt ſhe dede lord ſhe hath ſo bede wyte knowe hou ferd iuno goddes herde anone vpon matere irys bad h • r meſſagyer ſlepes hous ſhe ſhold wende byd hym make ende ſweuene ſhewen al caas lady hou irys fro hyghe ſtage whiche vndertake hath meſſage reyny cope dede vpon whiche wonderly begone colour dyners hewe honderd mo men knewe heuene lyche vnto bowe bende ſhe cam donne lowe god ſlepe ſhe fond ſtraunge lond whiche marcheth vpon chymery • ſeyth poeſye god ſlepe hath made hous whiche entaylle meruaylous vnder hylle ther caue whiche ſonne may haue yt man may knowe ary • poynt bytwene day nyght fyre ſpark dore whiche may chark wherof eye ſhold vnſhet inward let ſpeke withoute ſtant grete tre nyhe aboute wheron ther myght crowe pye lyght clepe crye coſt crowe day ne beſt none whiche noyſe may hylle al aboute round growend vpon ground popy whiche bereth ſeed ſlepe herbes ſuche hepe ſtylle water none rennend vpon ſmal ſtones whiche hyght • ethes ryuer vnder hylle ſuche maner whiche yeueth grete appetyte ſlepe thus ful delyte slepe hath hous couche within chambre yf ſhal touche hebenus ſlepy tre boordes al aboute ſhold ſlepe ſofte vpon fether bed alofte lyeth many pylwe doun chambre ſtrowed vp doun ſweuenes many thouſand fold thus come irys hold bed whiche blak goth therwith ſlepe ſhe ſpak wyſe ſhe bede meſſage iuno ſhe dede ful •• wordes ſhe reherſeth er ſhe ſlepy eres perſeth moche woo laſt ſlomerend eyen vpcaſt ſayd hyr ſhal bedoo wherof among thouſand tho within hous ſlepy ſpecyal cheſe oute thre whiche ſhold dede fyrſt hem ſo rede morpheus who nature take fygure perſone hym lyketh wherof therof entryketh lyf whiche ſlepe ſhal nyght ithecus hyght whiche hath voys euery ſoune theyr chere theyr condycyoun euery lyf ſo thyrd ſewend pantafas may tranſforme euery thynge ryght forme chaunge another kynde •• hem thre fynde ſweuenes ſtant al thapparence whiche otherwhyle euydence whyle iape netheles ſo ſhape morpheus nyght allone wereth vnto alceone lykeneſſe huſbond al naked dede vpon ſtronde hou dreynt ſpecyal theſe two ſhe wen ſhal tempeſt blak clowde wode ſee wyndes loude met ſhe ſawe hym dyen wherof ſhe bygan cryen slepend bedde ſhe laye noyſe hyr affraye woman ſtert vp aboute whiche doute axen hou ſhe ferde ſhe ryght ſhe ſawe herde ſweuen hath told hem euery dele halſen al wele ſeyn tokne good tyl ſhe wyſt hou ſtood hath comfort hyr herte vpon morowe vp ſhe ſterte ſee ſhe met body lay withoute let drough whan ſhe cam nygh stark dede armes ſprad ſhe ſyghe lord fletend vpon wawe wherof wyttes withdrawe ſhe whiche toke deth kepe anone forth lepte depe wold haue cauȝt hym hir arm infortune double harme goddes heuen aboue beheld trouthe loue whiche worthy lady stood haue vpon ſalt flood hyr dreynt lord hyr alſo fro deth lyf torned ſoo ſhapen byrdes swymmēd vpon wawe amyddes ſhe ſawe hyr lord lyuend lykeneſſe byrd ſwymmend ſhe ſame ſort ſhe myght dyſport vpon ioye whiche ſhe wynges anone ſhe ſprad hym bothe ſo ſhe may ſuffyſe • lypte kyſt ſuche wyſe ſhe whylome wonte doo wynges byr armes tho took lyppes ſofte hyr hard bylle ſoo ful ofte fondeth hyr byrdes forme ſhe myght hyr ſelf conforme pleſaunce wyf ſhe dyde lyf though ſhe hyr power lore hyr wylle ſtood fore ſerueth ſo ſhe may wherof ylk day geder vpon ſee wone many doughter ſone bryngen forth byrdes kynde men ſholde take mynde alceon trewe quene byrdes ſene alceon name bere lo thus may ſtere ſweuenes take kepe oftyme man ſlepe may ſee ſhal betyde thy helpeth ſom tyde man ſlepe belongeth ſlouthe noo lyf vnderfongeth whiche loue appertenaunt fader vpon couenaunt dare wel make auo al lyf nowe ferforth vnderſtonde yet took neuer ſlepe honde tyme wake though myn eye wold take myn herde euer ageyne neuertheles ſpeke pleyne al haue ſayd wakyng ye may toucheth lady ſwete otherwyſe byhete ſtraunge place go lyſt thyng wake ſoo woman lyſt playe ſee waye whome ſhold myrthe take lyſt longe wake yf pure ſhame wold eſhewe name ne ſhold haue cauſe none ſeye loo ſuche one hath forlore contenaunce thus among ſynge daunce feyne luſt none fulofte ſyth fete thought whiche myn hert falleth nyght myn hert appallyth ſee hyr nought whiche waker thought thus tymelyche may ful ofte brood day take al theſe heue goo wey byleue ſeen pe • caas loues goo forth nought ne vnto bed ſo alone may ther lygge ſyghe grone wyſſhen al long nyght tyl ſee dayes lyght yf ſompnolence vpon youre conſcyence myn holy fader demeth ye ſone wel payd ſhepe thou ſluggardye nyght loues companye eſche weſt haſt thy peyne thy loue dare pleyne loue vpon luſt wakend euer wolde none ende therof long nyghte ſet wherof thou ware bett telle tale bethought loue ſlepe acorden nought hic dicit ꝙ vigilia amantibus non ſompnolencia laudanda eſt et ponit exemplum de cephal • filio phebi qui nocturno ſilencio auroram amicam ſuam diligencius amplectens ſolem lunam interpellabat ▪ videlicet ꝙ ſol circulo ab oriēte diſtanciori currum cum luce ſua retardaret et ꝙ luna ſpera ſua longiſſima orbem circuiens noctem continuaret ita vt ipſum cephalum amplexibus amore volutum priuſ quam illa dy illuceſceret ſuis deliciis adquieſcere diucius permittere dignarentur loue lyſt wake nyȝt may enſāyle take cephalus yt lay aurora ſwete may armes al longe nyght toward lyght his▪ herte ſye day whiche morowe nyhe anone vnto ſonne preyde luſt loue thus ſeyde phebus whiche dayes lyght gouerneth tyl nyght gladeſt euery creature lawe thy nature netheles ther thyng whiche onlyche thy knoulechyngr belongeth pryuete loue dute whiche oxeth ben part ſylence couert deſyreth ſhadyd thus lyȝt faded veſper ſhe weth hym alofte nyght long ſofte vnder clowdes derſte ſtylle hath thyng moſt wylle fo • thy vnto thy myghtos hyghe thou whiche art dayes eye loue myght counſeyl hyde vpon derk nyghtes tyde al myn herte byſeche pleſaunce myght ſeche hyr whiche ſyeth myn armes withdrawe baner thyn armes ſete thy lyghtas ben vnborne ſygne caprycorne hous appropred saturne preye thou wolt ſoiourne ben nyghtes derk longe loue haue vnderfonge whiche lyeth ſyde naked whiche wold ben waked lyſt thyng ſlepe good take kepe tyme prayer lyke ſtere fyry cart ſo ordeyne thou thy ſwyft hors reſtreyne lowe vnder erthe occydent toward thorrent ſcr • le go long eke dyane preye whiche cleped art thy nobleſſe nyghtes mone goddeſſe thou gracyous • eo thyn owne hous ayene phebus oppoſyte stond al tyme delyte byholde venus glad eye vpon aſtronomye due couſtellacyon thou makeſte profyfycacyon doſt child begete whiche yf myght gete al myn herte wolſerue nyght thy vygylle obſerue loo thus luſty sephalus prayd vnto phebe phebus nyght lengthe drawe soo myght lawe thylk poynt loues heſte whiche cleped nyghtes feſte withouten ſlepe ſluggardye whiche venus oute companye hath put awey thylk ſame whiche luſtles fer game chambre doth ful oft woo bedde falleth ſo loue ſhold awayted ſlouthe whiche euyl affayted ſlepe hath made retenue thynge loue due al dette payeth none wote hou nyght gone ne hou daye come aboute ſlepe route tyl hyghe mydday aryſe sephalus dyd otherwyſe thou ſonne hoſt herd aboue amans fader hath loue bedde naked ſyde wolde eyen hyde ſlepe man certes touchend felle neuer yet whyle ſo may catche ſlepe honde lyggend alone fonde dreme mery ſweuene day yf▪ ſo falle may thought ſuch ſweuen pleſe thynſt ſomdele eſe none comfort haue soo nedeth nought ſhal craue ſonnes carte tarye ne yet mone ſhe carye cours long vpon heuene nought huene worldes good degre ſlepe yet ſee sōwhat ſweuene lyketh whiche afterward myn hert enteyketh fynde otherwyſe wote ſeruyce ſompnolence man doth ſone certes thou ſayſt ſoth helpeth kynde somtyme phyſyk fynde whan take meſure whiche ſlepe meſure vpon reule belongeth ful oft ſodeyne chaunce fongeth suche infortune hym greueth theſe old bokes leueth sompnolence hou wryte maye man ſothe wyte wold enſample take whyle good wake w •• rof tale poeſye thynke ſpecyfye hic loquitur amoris cauſa cō tra iſtos qiu ſōpnolencie dediti ca que ſeruare tenentur amittunt et narrat • cum yo puella pulcherrima iunone vaccam tranſformata argi cuſtodiam ſic depoſita fuiſſet ſuperuemens mercurius argum dormientem occidit vt ipſam vaccam paſtura rapiens quo voluit ſecum perduxit ovyde thus telleth ſawes hou iupiter olde dayes lay mayde whiche y cleped wherof iuno wyf wrothe goddeſſe yo torned lykeneſſe cowe goo ther oute large feldes al aboute gete hyr mete vpon grene therupon hyghe quene betook hyr argus kepe ſeldon wonte ſlepe yet honderd eyen al alyche wel ſym herkne hou begyled mercurye whiche al affyled cowe ſtele cam deſguyſed pype wel deuyſed vpon note muſyke wherof myght eres lyke ouer affayted luſty tale awayted tyme thus felde cam argus beheld yo whiche beſyde hym went pype anone hent gan pype manere thyng whiche ſlepy pypyng euer among told hym ſuche luſty ſong fool hath brought ſlepe none eye myght kepe hede whiche mercurye ſmote forth al anone fote hote ſtal cowe argus kept al fel ſlept enſample many mo mochel ſlepe doth ofte wo tyme wake yf man vyce take ſompnolonce hym delyte men ſhold vpon dore wryte epytaphe vpon graue ſpylle nought ſaue ſhaped though dede thymy ſone hold vp thyn heds lete ſlepe thyne eye englue reaſon due fader touchend ryght ſo told ofte bedde ſholde maye ſlepe though wolde loue euer faſt byme whiche taketh none hede due▪ tyme ſhal myn eye cloſe none hert wol oppoſe hold ſcole ſuche wyſe tyl day aryſe ſelde ſlepe thus fro ſompnolence kepe myn eye thy yf ther ought elles degre axe forth ſone yi ſlouthe whiche moder forth drawer▪ noryce man many dredeful vyce hath yet another laſt alle whiche many mā hath made falle myght neuer aryſe wherof thou ſhalt auyſe er thou ſo thy ſelf myſfare vyce wol declare nil fortuna iuuat vbi deſperacid •• dit quo deſiccat humor non virideſat humus magnanimus ſed amor ſ • em ponit inde ſalutem▪ cōſequitur • 〈◊〉 proſpera fata fauent hic loquitur ſuper vltima ſpecie acadie que triſticia ſiue deſperacio dicitur auus olſtinata condicio tocius con ſolacionis ſpem deponens alicuius remed • quo kberari poterit fortunam ſib • euenire impoſſible credit whan ſlouthe doth al yt may dryue forth long day tyl bycome nede laſt vpon dede laketh hou tyme lore ſo woo begone therfore within thought conceyueth tryſteſſe ſo hym ſelf deceyueth wanhope bryngeth inne comfort begynne euery ioye hym dylayed within herte affrayeth thouſand tyme one breth wepend wyſſheth deth fortune fynt aduerſe wol happe reheree though world al forlore ſayth allas lore ſhal lyue ſhal doo fortune foo wote wel god wol helpe ſhold ioye yelpe ther bote care ouer caſt al welfare ſhapen al ſtryf allas neuer lyf fullyche ouertake thus wol ſorowe make god hym myght auayle yet ne wol trauayle helpe hym ſuche nede ſlouteth vnder ſuche drede whiche affermed hert ryght myght nought aſterte worldes woo whiche inne alſo falle ſynne hym thynketh ſo fer culpable god wol mercyable soo grete ſynne foryeue thus leueth ſhryue yf man thylk throwe wold hym coūſeyle wol knowe ſoth though • man fynde tryſteſſe ſuche kynde mayntene fely hath hym obſtynacy whiche within ſuche ſlouthe forſlaketh al trouthe wol reſon bo yet alowe owne ſkylle hede thus dwyneth tyl dede hyndryng owne eſtate man obſtynate whan hope foloweth laſt whiche may longe laſt tyl ſlouthe make hym ende god wote whether ſhal wende ſone ryght ſuche manere louers heuy chere ſorowen nede whan torned theyr ſpede ſelf rede leſen hope ſpede ſtynten loue purſewe thus faden hyde hewe luſtles hertes waxe herof wold axe thou ſone art one tho good fadre ſoo take poynt knowe elles ouerthrowe al euer ye haue ſeyd ſorowe euermore vnteyd ſecheth oueral veynes counſeylle peynes bote doo therto thus withouten hope goo soo • wyttes ben empeyred ſayd deſpeyred wynne loue thylke ſwete withoute whome behete myn herte ſo beſtad ryght may neuer glad trouthe ſhal lye pure ſorowe whiche drye ſhe ſayth ſhe wol nought dretchyng myn owne thoughe ſuche wanhope falle ne vnnethes calle ſpeke ony grace lady grace purchace yet ſay nought al myn defaulte neuer yet ſtede tyme bede ne ſayde dorſt tolde neuer fonde ſhe wolde ought ſhe knewe myn entent ſpeke goodly word aſſent netheles dar ſeys yf ſynful wold prey god foryeueneſſe half ſo grete beſyneſſe haue lady lak axyng mercy ſholde neuer come helle aud thus may ſothly telle sauf ceye byd tryſteſſe al amydde fulfylled dyſperaunce therfor yeue penaunce myn holy fader lyketh ſone thy herte ſyketh ſorowe myght thou amende tyl loue grace wol ſende thou thyne owne cauſe empeyreſe tyme yt thou thy ſelf dyſpeyreſt uot thyng auayleth hope herte fayleth ſuche ſoor ina • rable eke goddes ben vengeable man may ryght wel feede theſe old bokes ſo rede thyng whiche hath byfalle enſample hic narrat qualiter iphis gi theucri filius ob amore cuuiſdā puelle nomine araxarathen quam ne que donis aut precibus vincere potuit deſ perans ante patris ipſiꝰ ianuas noctanter ſe ſuſpendit vnde dij comoti dic tam puellam lapidem duriſſuuam tranſmutarunt quam rex theucer vna cum filio ſuo apud ciuitatem sala minam templo veneris pro perpetua memoria ſepeliri locari fecit whylome old dayes fer meſe ye kyng theucer knyȝt ſon iphis loue • e ſoo maſtred hath ſet al courage regard lygnage vpon mayde lowe aſtate though poteſtate worldes good ſubgett loue put ſuche plyte excedeth meſure reson hym ſelf aſſure nought prayd laſſe loue hym ſhe layd loue vn wiſe cōſtreyned ſhe reson ſtreyned luſtes herte ſeweth ſhe drede ſhame eſche weth ſhe ſhold toke hede ſaue kepe hyr womanhede thyng ſtood debate bytwene lust eſtate yaue ſend ſpak mouth yet ought euer couth vnto ſpede fond weye cast hope aweye within hert gan dyſpeyre fro day day ſo • empeyre hath loſt al delyte luſt ſlepe appetyte thurgh ſtrength ſone laſſeth wyt reſon ouer paſſeth whiche lyf ne tought deth vpon hym ſelf ſought nyght weye nam wyſt none bycam nyght derk mone ſhone fore gate cam ſone yong mayde woful word allas dedely pleyntes bygan ſtylle noman herde ſayde thus thou cupyde thou venus fortuned whoos ordenaunce loue euery man chaunce ye knowen al myn hole hert ne may hondes aſterte euer crye yet deyneth plye ne toward ere enclyne thus ſee noo medycyne make ende quarele deth ſhal ſtede hele ha thou woful lady dere whiche duelleſt thy fadre ſlepeſt thy bed eſe thou woteſt thyng dyſeſe thou vnmete lord ſweuene ſhalt thou mete dremes haſt thou hond thou ſlepeſt ſtond though deth deſerue ſhal thy loue ſterue ſhal kynges ſone▪ deye loue felonye whether thou therof haue ioye ſorow ſhalt thou ſee dede morowe hard hert abouen alle deth whiche ſhal falle thou wolt grace ſhal told many place dede loue trouthe thy defaulte thy ſlouthe thy daunger ſhal many mo enſample euermo woful deth recorde word took corde whiche vpon gate tre henge hym ſelf pyte morowe cam nyght gone men come oute ſyghe anone yonge lord dede hous withoute dede noman knewe cauſe wepyng ther cry mayden ſhe herde ſawe thyng hou myſferd auone ſhe wyſt mente al cauſe hou wente al world ſhe told oute preyth hem aboute take wngeaunce ſhe cauſe thylk chaunce kynges ſone ſpy • taketh vpon hyr ſelf gylt al redy peyne whiche ony man hyr wol ordeyne yf ony wold ſayth hyr ſelf ſhe ſhold doo wreche hyr owne hond thorugh oute world in▪ euery lōd euery lyf therof ſhal ſpeke hou ſhe hyr ſelf ſhold wreke wepeth ſhe cryeth ſhe ſwouneth oft caſt hyr eyen vp alofte ſayd among ful pytouſly god thou woſt wel iphis thus byſeyn ordeyne ſo many may ſeyn thouſand wynter hou ſuche mayden dyd amys ſo dyde ne dyde noo pyte hym whiche loue lore doo pyte therfore word ſhe felle groſid ſwoune ſhe lay aſtound goddes whiche pleyntes herde ſawe hou wofully ſhe ferde lyf awey took anone ſhopen ſtone forme hyr ymage body bothe vyſage meruaylle thyng vnto place cam kyng eke quene many mo wyſten foo haue told aboue hou iphys dede loue refuſed helden al men excuſed wondren vpon vengeaunce kepe remembraunce fayre ymage mayden lyche companye noble ryche torch grete ſolempnyte salamyne cyte lede carye forth dede corp ſeyn ſhall beſyde thylk image haue ſepulture begraue corp image thus cyte venus goddeſſe temple geder bothe forth lad thylke image myracle ſette vpon hyghe pynacle al myght knowe vnder maden lowe tombe ryche none marble eke iaſpre ſtones wheryn iphys byloken euermore ſhal ſpoken men ſhal ſothe wyte haue epytaphe wryte thyng whiche ſhold abyde ſtable lettres granen table marble ſayd thys lyeth ſlouȝ hym ſelf iphis loue araxarathen euſample tho woman ſuffren men dyen ſoo forme man may ſeen alſo hou torned fleſſhe bone fygure ſtone neſſhe ſhe hard beware thy afterward ye men woman bothe two enſampleth tho loo thus ſone ſeye greueth dyuers weye deſpeyr man falle whiche laſt braunche alle ſlouthe thou haſt herd deuyſe wherof thou thy ſelf auyſe good thou deceyued wherof hope grace weyued fadre hou ſo ſtonde nou haue pleynly vnderſtonde ſlouthes court propyrte wherof touchend degre euer thynk ware ouer ſo dare al myn hert yow byſeche ye wold enforme teche youre apryſe loue al wel wyſe may clene ſhryue confeſſor ſonne whyle thou art alyue haſt alſo thy ful mynde among vyces whiche fynde yet one ſuche ſeuene whiche al world hath ſet vneuene cauſeth many tymes wrong cauſe hath vnderfong wherof thou ſhalt forme matere expliat liber quartus incipit liber quintus • ſtat auaricia nature legibus et que largue amor poſcit ſtrict •• e illa vetat omne ꝙ eſt nimium vi c • oſum dicitur aurū vellera sicut oues ſeruat auarus opes non decet vt ſoli ſer • abitur o ſed amori debet homo ſo lam ſolus habere ſuam firſt hyghe god begā world kynde man falle grete encrees worldes good tho prees al ſet comune ſpeken fortune leſe wynne tyl auaryce brought inne yt ye world woye man hore ſhepe oxe men knewen money tho went pee oute weye werre came euery ſyde whiche al loue leyd aſyde comon propre made ſtede ſhouel ſpade ſharp take honde wyſe cam londe wherof men made dyches depe hyghe walles kepe gold whiche auaryce encloſeth al lytel hym ſuppoſeth though myȝt al world purchace thyng may embrace gold catel lond lete neuer oute hond gete hym halt faſt though world ſholde euer laſt lyche vnto helle theſe bokes telle cometh ther laſſe ſhal departe neuermore thus hath cofer loken ſhal ben vnſtoken hym lyſt haue ſyght gold hou ſhyneth bryght theron may loke muſe wyſe dare vſe take part leſſe power euermore hym lakketh hath inough oxe draweth plough hym ſelf hath profyte ſhepe ryght ſame plyte wulle bereth vpon day another taketh flees aweye thus hath yt nought ne hath therof part ne tath ſeye hou ſuche man hath good ſo reſon vnderſtood inproperlyche ſayd good hath hym halt hym taid ne gladeth nought alle vnto good thralle ſubget thus ſerueth ſhold mayſter suche kyng thauarous ſone thou art amerous telle yf thou fareſt loue ſoo fadre ſemeth auarous yet neuer ye ſetten caas ye tolden aboue ful poſſeſſyon loue yet neuer fore soo thynketh wel therfore may excuſe wel dede wylle withoute drede yf treſour myght gete ſhold neuer foryete ne wold faſte holde tyl god loue hym ſelue wolde deth v ſhold departe two leueth wel loue ſo euen myn owne lyf ſwete luſty wyf myght one welden wylle wold holde hyr ſtylle wyſe taketh kepe wold kepe yet frydaye wold faſt though kepte holde faſt fy bagges kyſt ynough yf kyſt certes yf ſhe myn leuer myn gold al worlde ryche ne myght make ſo ryche ſhe ſo inly good ſet nought good myght gete ſuche thynge treſour kynge though wold faſte holde therto mochel byholde myȝt pype laſſe ſuffre ouerpaſſe wyll thus wold ben auarous yf ſhold fadre herd ſey hou auarous hath yet ſomme wey wherof may glad may hym lyſt treſour ſe grope fele al aboute ful ofte ſhet ther oute worthy treſour lyf lyche vnto tolden fore hou oxe yok hath bore thyng ſhold hym auayle wyſe trauayle euer hath welfare wote wel haue care ſayth loues knaue nought ne haue deme owne thought yf auaryce nought ſone haue wonder thongh thou ſerue put vnder loue whiche kynde acordeth ſoo euery book recordeth kynde pleſaunce man aboue ſuſtenaunce vnto gold ſhal ſerue bowe may reaſon auowe auaryce netheles may geten encrees gold wold ſerue kepe taketh nought elles kepe fylle bagges large al hym charge ne parteth nought al kepeth ſeruaunt ſhal thus though multyplye gold withoute treſorye 〈◊〉 man nought amended gold yf dyſpended man vse wherof rede tale take therof manere wh • ſe yt hym lyketh duelleth al bachus telleth cam hym ageyne bachus herd ſeyn hou myde hath done curteſye hym thynketh • vylony • reward hym dede myght godhede vnto kyng god appereth clepeth hereth god myde thanketh fayre ſoo debonayre toward preſt bad hym ſey • thyng wold preye ſhold haue worldly good kyng glad ſtylle ſtood axyng doute al world casteth aboute thyng beſt • ſtate hym ſelf ſtood debate vpon thre poyntes whiche fynde ben leueſt vnto mannes kynde fyrst hem delyte two ben worſhyp profyte thought yf craue delyte though delyte may haue delyte ſhal paſſen age ſyker auauntage euery ioye bodely shal ende woo delyte thy wol cheſe yf worſhyp axe world lordſhyp occupacyon proude imagynacyon whiche maketh hert veyn within certeyne wynne lorde knaue al one weye bore deye yf profyte axe wolde maner ſholde worldes good haue ſykerneſſe euery theef vpon rycheſſe wayteth robbe ſtele suche •• ood cauſe harmes fele also though man one al world within wones treſour myght haue euery deele yet one man dele toward hym ſelf ſo thynke clothynge mete drynke oute take vanyte hath lord degre thus vpon poyntes dyuerſe dyuerſly gan reherce poynt hym thought beſt pleynly gete hym reſt ſyker weye caſt netheles yet laſt felle vpon couetyſe gold ſondry wyſe thought haue ſayd fore treſour may ſone forlore inly grete deſyre touchend ſuche recouer hou myght cause auayle gete hym gold withoute fayle within hert thus preyſeth gold ſayth hou peyſeth aboue al metal moſt gold ſayth may lede hooſt make werre ayene kyng gold put vnder al thyng ſet whome hym lyſt aboue gold make hate loue werre pee ryght wrong long ſhort ſhort long withoute gold may feſt gold lorde man beſte may hem bye ſelle soo man may ſothely telle al world gold obeyeth thy kyng bachus preyth graunte hym gold excedeth meſure hym nedeth men tellen maladye whiche callyd ioropeſy • resembled vyce weye kynde auaryce idropeſye drynketh thyrſteth hym thynketh may drynke fylle soo may thyng fulfylle luſtes appetyte ryght ſuche maner plyte stant euer auaryce euer ſtood hath worsdes good wolde kepe ſtreyte euer coueyte ryght ſuche condicyon wythoute good diſcrecyon kyng auaryce ſmete al worlde myght wete bachus preyd wherupon honde leid ſholde thorugh touche anone become gold therupon god hym graunteth bad tho kyng fryge glad put aſſaye al haſt maye toucheth toucheth hond al gold stone tre leef gras floure fruyte al gold thus toucheth may laſt hongre att laſt hym took ſoo mote nede wey kynde hongre fede clothe leyd boord ſet alle forth byfore hym ſet diſſh drink cuppe meet wold drynk ete mouth anone cam nyghe al gold ſyghe auayrce folye bygnne crye preyde bachus foryeue gylt ſuffre hym lyue ſuche fore soo nought forlore god whiche greuaunce herd toke routhe vpon repentaūce bad hym goo forth redyly vnto flood faſt whiche paceole hyght whiche ſone euer myght ſholde hym waſſhe oueral ſaid hym ſhal recouere hys fyrſt aſtate ageyn kyng right herd ſeyn flood goth fro lond weſſhe hym bothe fote hond ſo forth al remenaunt hym ſet •• uendunt ſawe meruayles ſtraūge flood coloure gan chaunge grauel ſmal ſtones gold torne al attones quyte thus fortune chaunge lad ſawe touche gone goth hym home ryght forth ſoone lyueth forth dyde er put al auaryce fer ryches gold deſpyſeth ſeyth mete clothe ſuffyſeth thus hath kyng experyence hou fooles done reuerence gold whiche owne kynde laſſe worth rynde ſuſtenaunce man fode made lawes goode al thyng ſet vpon ſkylle lede people tylle l • nd lyue vnder lawe alſo ſhold forth drawe beſtayl ſeche none encrees • f gold whiche breche pee man may fynde wryte fere tyme gold ſmyte coygne men floren knewe wel nyhe noman vntrewe nother ſhelde ne ſpere ne dedely wepen bere • toune withoute walle whiche cloſed ouer alle tho bro •• ge lond whiche taketh euery cauſe hōd may yt man knowe hou floreyn moder fyrſt malengyn brynger alle werre wherof world stant oute herre thorugh counſeyl auary •• whiche owne propre vyce whiche helle wonderful may neuermore ful euer cometh therynne awey ne may neuer wynne ſone myn thou ſo late al ſuche auaryce go take thy part thou haſt byd thou waſt hold largeſſe meſure yf thou ſee creature whiche thorugh pouert falle nede yeue hym ſomme good rede hym wol yeuen peyne ſhal haue elles peyne among al bynethe helle whiche men calle woful peyne tantaly whiche ſhal redely deuyſe hou theryn men ſtond helle thou ſhalt vnderſt • nd flood thylk offyce whiche ſerueth al auaryce man ſtonde ſhal therin ſtant vp euen chynne aboue hede alſo hougeth fruyt whiche peyne longeth fruyt toucheth euer one ouerlyppe therupon suche thyrſt honger hym aſſayleth neuer appetyte ne fayleth wende hongar fede fruyt withdraweth hym nede though haue hede hyghe fruyt euer alyche nyghe honger wel also though hym thurſt ſore water bowe adoune flood ſuche condycyon aualeth drynke areche may loo whiche wreche mete drynk hym ſo couthe yet ther comth none mouth lyche peynes flood stant auaryce worldes good hath inough yet hym nedeth ſcarcenes hym forbedeth euer honger trauayleth hym alyche ſore peyned oueral thy thy goodes oueral ſone loke thou dyſpende wherof thou myght thy ſelf amende bothe eke place alſo yf thou wolt purchace loued thou muſt vſe largeſſe yf thou refuſe yeue thy loues ſake reſon thou take loue thou woldeſt craue thy yf thou wolt grace haue gracyous largeſſe auaryce ſekeneſſe eſche aboue al thyng take enſample myde kyng flood helle alſo inough al wo though matere fynden men ought auaryce eſche man thylk vyce ſewe gete hym ſelf lytel reſt though ſo body reſt hert vpon gold trauayleth whome many nyȝt • drede aſſaileth though lygge bed naked herte euermore awaked dremeth lyeth ſlepe hon beſy kepe treſour noo theef ſtele thus hath woful wele ryght ſo ſame wyſe thou thy ſelf wolt wel auyse louers ſuche inough wol vnto reaſon bough • e come aboue mayſtres loue ſholden moſt glad loue ben mooſt beſtad fayn wolden holden hir herte hir eye ouerall wenen euery man theef ſtele awey hem leef thus thorugh owne fantaſye fallen ielouſye hath ſhyp broke cable euery wynde meuable amans fader ye telle haue herde oftyme telle ielouſye yet vnderstond neuer wherfore wold byſeche ye wold enforme teche maner thyng myght ſone hard netheles haue herd herkne thou ſhalt anſuerd nota de ielouſia cuius fantaſtica ſuſpicio amorem quentuis fideliſſimū mul • ciens ſine cauſa corruptum imagina tur among men lak manhod maryage vpon wyſhode maketh man hym ſelf deceyueth wherof yt conceyueth ylke vneſy maladye whiche cleped ielouſye whiche yf propyrte shal telle nyorte worcheth man feuer cotydyan whiche euery day wol come aboute ſo man oute home yf man wol wone feuer comon wone mooſt greuous man eye maketh hym tote prye ſo loue euer go ſhal hyr lytel myſteppe ſeeth al eye walkend oueral ſhe ſynge ſhe daūce ſeeth leſt countenaunce ſhe loke man ſyde hym rowne ony tyde ſhe laugh ſhe • oure eye euery houre draweth nyght ſhe ſoo withoute lyght anone al game ſhente ſet parlement ſpeke cometh bedde ſayth yf wedde wold neuermore haue wyf ſo torneth ſtryf luſt loues dute al vpon dyuerſyte ſhe freſſhe wel arayed ſayth baner dyſplayed cle • e geſtes fro weye yf ſhe wel beſeye hyr lyſt glad beryth hond ſhe mad loueth huſbond ſayth may wel vnderſtond yf ſhe wold companye ſhold afore eye al pleſaunce ſhe myȝt daye ne nyght thyng beſt lyueth wel oute al reſt euer hym lyſt ſeyn dare ſpeke one word ageyn wepeth hold hyr lyppes cloos may wel wryte saunce •• poos wyf whiche ſuche one maryed al woman waryed feuer jelouſye eche dayes fantaſye ſoro euer alyche grene loue ſene whyle hym lyſt home abyde ſo wol oute ryde ••• hath redy • ſpye abydyng companye jangler euyl mouthed one ſhe ne may •• ther gone ne ſpeke one word ne one loke ne wol wende croke torne owne entent though ſhe thyng honour ment lord comth home ageyn jangler muſt ſomwhat ſeyn withoute withynne feuer euer begynne cometh ende tyl deth hym hath made ende though ſo ne ne ſee wyte manere al honoure womanhede therof ielous taketh none • ede man loue vnkynde caſt ſtaf doth blynde fynt defaulte none ſo dremeth ſtone hou leyd groneth ofte lyeth pylowe ſofte ther nought ſtryf cheſt loue ſhold make reſt grete thyng yf kyſſe thuo hath ſhe loſte nyghtes blyſſe ſuche tyme grutcheth euer beryth hond ther leuer ſhe wold another ſtede hym abedde tho wordes mo jelouſye torneth fro lyeth vpon ſyde ſhe draweth hyr aſyde ther ſhe wepeth al nyght peyne ſhe dyght▪ thought hath ſo beſet bonde whiche may vnknet wote tyme ofte curſed euer gold vnpurſed whiche leyd vpon book al ſhe forſook loue hym al late pleyneth algate mo • e forbere hym • owe though ne wold allowe man lord thylk feyre may woman empeyre ſhe ſpeke ought ageyne thy wylle thus ſhe beryth peyne ſtylle yf feuer woman • ke ſhal wel harde ſha •• yf ſhe bothe ſee fynde matere dare ſelf pleyne thus ſhe ſuffreth double peyne loo thus ſone haue • ryt • thou myght jelouſye wyte feuer condycyon whiche fal ſuſpectyon wherof feuer groweth ſo theſe olde bokes weth may fynde hou v teche telle hou feuer jelouſye somdele groweth ſotye loue ſomdele vntruſt ſekeman left luſt may ſauoure gete hateth owne mete ryght ſo feuerous maladye whiche cauſed fantaſye maketh jelous feble plyght leue loue appetyt thorugh feyned informacyon imagynacyon fynally taken heede men may wel make lykelyhede bytwene hym whiche auarou • gold hym ir •• u loue one degre ſtonde bothe ſemeth one wold haue bagges ſtyl nought departen wyll dare theues ſlepe fayne wold treſour kepe maye wel glad euermore adrad theſe louers gone aboute aunter yf put hym oute haue bothe lytel ioye wel loue moneye haſt thou ſone techyng ielouſye knowlechyng thou myght vnderſtonde fro cometh eke whome lyke beware thy thou ſyke thylk feuer haue ſpoke wol hym ſelf wroke loue hateth thyng men may fynde lore hem whylome wy •• hou ſpeke many wyſe fader ſothe ye ſeyn loke ageyn byfore tyme hou falle wherof myght enſample falle ſuche men ben ielous maner greuous ryght fayn wold enſample good ſone thy prayere ſuche enſamples fynde soo comen mynde vpon poynt tyme gone thynke tellen one hic ponit confeſſor exemplum contra iſtos maritos quos ielouſia •• la •• et narrat qualiter vul canus cuins vxor venus extitit ſuſpicionem inter ipſam martem concipiēs eorum geſtus diligencius explorabat vnde contigit ꝙ cum ipſe quadam vice ambo inter ſe pariter amplexantes lecto nudo inuenit et ſtature • othly malgracyous yet hath within hous lykyng lyf fayre venus wyf mar whiche bataylles god eye vnto whiche chyualrous felle hym ben amerous thought grete pyte ſee ſoo luſty one ſhe coupled ſo hard wyght peyne day nyght dyd yf wynne myght ſhe good inſyght toward ſo noble knyghtly lord loue fel acord lakketh nouȝt tyme place ny • ſyker grace two hertes fallen one wyſe wayte neuer none ſomtyme ne mete thus fayre luſty ſwete mar hath ofte companye thylk vnkynde ielouſye whiche euermore herte oppoſeth maketh vulcanus ſuppoſeth wel ouerall hym ſelf ſayde ſhal ſ • • better yf may ſo felle vpon day thyng ſo ſlyghly ledde fond hem bothe • edde al warme echone naked craft al redy maked ſtrong cheynes hath hem bounde geder hem founde lefte hem bothe lygge ſo gan crye tho vnto goddes al aboute aſſembled route come al one ſee none amendes bat rebuked hem loues frendes ſayd blame yf ther felle hym ony ſhame thorugh myſgouernaūce thus loſt contenaunce god lete cauſe falle ſcorne •• owen ••• e lo • en mar oute hondes wherof theſe erthely huſbondes euer myght enſample take ſuche chaunce hem ouertake vulcanus wyf bewrayd blame vpon hym ſelf ho layd • wherof ſhame whiche ought lore euery man leueth reulen hym matere though ſuche hap loue aſterte yet ſhold apoynte herte ielouſye wrought feyne though wyſt nouȝt yf • ete ouerpaſſe ſklaunder ſhal wel laſſe eſe ſtonde thou myght wel vnderſtonde man ſhal nedes le •• laſſe harme cheſe ielouſye vntryſt maketh ful many harme aryſt whiche elles ſhold aryſe yf man wold hym auyſe byfelle▪ vulcanus hym ought reſon thynke thus ſyth god therof ſhamed wel ſhold erthely man blamed take vpon hym ſuch • vyce thy ſone thyne offyce beware thou nought ielous whiche oftyme hath ſhent hous fadre enſample bard hou ſuche thyng heuen ward among goddes myght falle one god alle whiche lord heuene •• helle yf lyke telle hou ſuche goddes come place ye myght mochel thank purchace ſhal wel taught alle confeſſor ſonne ſoo ouerall • hem ſtonden hym al ryght inne hyghe god whiche wold wynne people vnto owne feyth abraham ground leyth made hym multyplye ſo grete progenye egypte al ouer ſprad pharao wrong hem lad ſeruytude ayene pee tyl god lete ſende moyſes make delyueraunce peple grete vengeannce took whiche wonder kyng ſlayn ye lōd put vnder god bad reed ſee deuyde whiche ſtood vpryght euery ſyde yafe vnto people weye foote paſſed dreye gone ſo forth deſert kepe hem couert dayes ſonne brent large cloude hem ouer went wyſſen hem nyght fyry pyler hem alyght hongre pleyn myghty god began reyne manna fro heuen doune grounde wherof eche hem hath fonnde fode ſuche ryght hym lyſt ſhold vpon hym tryſt right ſet tonne broche perced hard roche ſpronge oute water al wille man beſte hath bronke wyll afterward yafe lawe moyſes hem withdrawe ſhold fro bad wyſe lad tyl took poſſeſſyon lond promyſſyon caleph ioſue march vpon ſuche degre departen lygnage eche hem herytage pourpartye hath vnderfonge thus ſtood byleue longe whiche prophetes gouerned eke peple lerned grete honour ſholde hem falle mooſt nede alle fayleden cryſt bore hou feyth haue lore nedeth nought tellen al mater ſoo general luafer beſt heuene ought mooſt haue ſtond euene towardes god took debate obſtynate wold nought trouthe enclyne fel euer ruyne adam eke paradys ſtood mooſt al prys̄ ſtate innocence ayene god brake defence fell hye place wey ryght ſuche maner weye iewes beſt plyght ſhold mooſt parfyght haue ſtonde vpon prophecye tho fellen mooſt folye hym whiche frō heuen come mayde fleſſhe hath nome amonge hem born fed men wold nought ſped goddes ſone one voys henge ſlough vpon croys wherof parfyte lawe fro forth forth drawe ſtonde meryte bnt truage folk ſubgect withoute propyrte place lyuen oute goddes grace dyſpers al londes oute thus feyth come • whylome iewes ſtood whiche nonght parfytely good ſpeke falle feyth abouen alle trouthe comprehended wherof ben al amended de fide criſtiana qua perfecte le gi complementum ſummi • iſterij ſacramentum noſtre que ſaluacionis fundamentum infallibiliter conſiſtere credimus hyghe almyghty mageſte ryght wyſenes pyte ſynne whiche adam wrouȝt ſawe tyme ſouȝt ſende ſone fro ye heuene ſette man ſoule euene whiche ſo forfalle vpon poynt whiche ſo byfalle ne myght hym ſelf aryſe gregorye ſayth apryſe helpeth nought man bore goddes ſone vnbore thurgh fyrſt ſynne whilom adam brouȝt v inne ſholden al men loſt cryſt reſtoreth thylk loſt bought fleſſhe blood yf thynken hou ſtood thylk raunſon whiche payd ſeynt gregorye wrote ſayd al behouely man wherof woo bygan cauſe al welthe whiche welle helthe hyghe creatour lyf vpon nede ſuche ſtryf wold creature take hym ſelf forfeture ſuffre man ſake thus may reſon wel forſake ilke ſynne orygynal ne cauſe ſpecyal man worſhyp laſt whiche ſhal withouten ende laſt cauſe godhede aſſembled manhede vyrgyne nome oure fleſſhe man become bodely fraternyte wherof man degre stondeth worthy haue told dyd erſt thouſand fold thorugh baptyſme newe lawe whiche criſt lord felawe thus hyghe goddes myght whiche vyrgyne alyght man ſoule hath reconſyled whiche long ben exyled ſtant feyth vpon byleue withoute whiche may man acheue gete hym paradys ageyn byleue ſo certeyn ful grace vertu man clepeth iheſu clene lyf forth good dede may faylen heuen mede soo ſtonde vppon byleue euery man may wel acheue whiche taken hath ryght feyth elles goſpel ſeyth saluacyon ther maye none preche therupone thus cryſt bad apoſtles alle who power falle v holy chirche good dedes wirche feyth ſuffyſeth nought good dede alſo wrought good thou thy whiche thorugh baptyſme propyrly art vnto cryſtes feyth profeſſed wa • e thou oppreſſed antecryſtes lollardye iewes prophecye ſet god auauntage ryght ſo newe tapynage lollardye goth aboute ſette cryſtes feyth doute ſayntes v fore whome feyth firſt vp bore holy chirche ſtood releued oughten better byleued theſe whiche men knowe holy though feyne blowe lollardye mannes ere yf thou wylt lyue oute fere suche newe lore rede eſchewe hold forth ryght weye ſewe thyn aunceſtres dyde thou byleue nought amys cryſt wrought fyrſt taught soo dede word araught yafe enſample perſone wordes haue alone lyke tree leues grene foſſum talentum pro nichi •• computabitur wold enſample take gregorye vpon omelye ageyne ſlouthe prelacye compleyneth hym thus ſeyth peter fader feyth domeſday ſhal hym bryng iudeam whiche thorugh ſpyrytual whiche oure charge ſpecyal thyng may amounte vpon thylk ende oure acompte cryſt hym ſelf audytour taketh none hede wyn honour offyce chauncellery kynges treſorye ne wryt ne wyll warant may auayle world ſo wel • row shal make v mowe soo paſſe withoute mede none otherwyſe ſpede rede ſpedde whiche • • de beſauntes dde therupon gat none en • rees tyme netheles man thanke deſerue world ſo luſty ſerue hym ben al acorded wyſt wel recorded thorugh oute erthe al londes late knyȝ • e wynne hondes oure tonges ſhal ſtylle ſtonde vpon fleſſhes wylle trauayl preche feyth cryſt teche folk paynem wol euery prelate holde ſee al ſuche may gete luſty drynk luſty mete wherof body fatt ful vnto goſtely labour dull ſlough handel thylk plough elles ſwyft inough toward worldes auaryce ſacryfyce whiche apoſtel ſeyth openly ayene feyth vnto idoles youe graunted netheles haunted vertu chaunged vyce largeſſe auaryce who chapytre mowe trete fader mater bete fer euer whyle lyue ſhal bet heed yeue vnto caſt soo whyle thylk myrrour laſt ther lond whiche myȝt acheue werre rome greue▪ wherof grete enuye tho felle thylk tyme ſoo rome werres ſtrong ageyne cartage ſtonde long two cytees vpon debate cartage ſawe ſtronge aſtate rome thylk myrroure ſtonde thought al pryuely fonde ouerthrowe ſomme wyle hanybal thylk whyle prynce leder cartage whiche ſet al courage vpon knyghthode ſuche wyſe worthy wyſe none counſeyled wherof world yet merueyled mayſtryes wrought vpon march whiche ſought fel thylke tyme alſo kyng puyle whiche tho thought ayene rome rebelle thus take quarelle hou deſtroye emperour rome tho gouernour craſſus whiche ſo couetous euer deſyrous golde gete pyllage wherof puyle eke cartage philoſophres wyſe grete begynne▪of mater trete laſt degre philoſophres thre doo thys thyng whiche vndertake therupon ▪ hem toke grete treſour gold cofres rome thus theſe philoſophres gedre companye went noman wyſe ment rome come pryuely duelt thoughten deceyne none myȝt hem perceyue tyl ſondry ſtedes haue gold vnder erthe begraue treſours holde ſheld ſeme gold ſo forth thenne vpon day al openly good array▪ themperour preſente tolden entente duelle vnder ſeruyſe hem axeth wyſe hym told ſuche plyte eche hem ſpyryt whiche ſle • end nyght appereth hem ſondry dremes lereth world hath betyd vnder ground yf ought hyd olde treſour ony throwe ſhal ſweuene knowe vpon condycyon they▪ſeyn gold vnder toun hyd rome wol fynde ſhal nought left behynde ſoo haluen dele hem graunteth aſſenteth wele thus cam ſleyghte duelle couetyſe telle emperour bad redyly lodged faſt owne bodye lay morow day one hem ſayth mette whele gold hoord ſhold fette wherof emperour glad therupon anone •• nours goo myne hym ſelf couyne goth forth al hond treſour redy fond ſayd ſhold glad vpon day ſecond haue another gold hoord found whiche ſecond mayſter took vpon ſweuene vndertook thus ſothe •• peryence themperour yafe ſuche credence al truſt al feyth ſekyrlyc • e hem leyth fond hym ſo releued parfytely beleued though goddes thre herkne ſubtylyte thyrd mayſter ſhold mete whiche ſaiden ſhold mete aboue hem al couthe mooſt withoute noyſe boſt al pryuelycho ſo wolde vpon morowe ſweuene tolde themperour ryght ere ſaid hym wiſt treſour ſoo plentyuous gold eke ſo precious iewelles ryche ſtones vnto al hors one charge ſuffiſaunt lord vpon couenaunt glade axeth maiſter ſaide vnder glas told hym eke myne wolde ordeyne ſuche engyne werk ſhold vnderſett timbre withoute lett men maye treſour ſauely delue soo myrrour hym ſelue withoute empeirement ſhal ſtonde thus maiſter vpon honde hath vndertake al weye lord whiche wit alweye couetiſe blent anone therto yafe aſſent thus myne forth • tymbre ſette vp oueral wherof pyler ſtood vp ryght til byfelle vpon nyght theſe clerkes whan ware hou tymbre bare piler myrroure ſtood ſleight man vnderſtood go nyght vnto myne pitche ſulphir •• ſyne cyte ſlepe wylde fyre depe caſt among tymbre werk ſo forth whyle nyght derk deſguyſed pouer array paſſeden towne day comen vpon helle ſawen hou myrrour felle wherof made ioye ynough eche hem lough ſayd loo couetyſe may hem wyſe proued afterward euery lond rome ward whiche ſubgett fore myrrour forlore wonder herd ſeye anone begonne dyſobeye werres vpon euery ſyde thus hath rome loſt pryde defouled oueral fynde hanybal romayns day hem oute away grete multytude ſlough gold rynges whiche drouȝ gentyle handes ben dede buſſhellys ful thre rede feld made brydge alſo myght ouer tyber goo vpon corp thāt dede romayns whiche ſlouȝ ſpeke iuyſe whiche couetyſe take vpon emperour deſtroyed myrrour wonder romayns made chayere ſet emperour therin ſayden wold wynne gold ſuperfluyte gold ſhold plente receyue tyl ſayde ho gold whiche tho boylend hote within panne mouthe poure thanne thus ye thirst gold queint gold whiche ben atteynt wherof ſone thou myght couetyſe hath loſt ſtere reſonable gouernaunce falleth ofte grete greuaunce may werſe thyng couetyſe aboute kyng perſone doth aduerſyte yf in▪his counſeyl ſtond bryngeth al day meſchyef hond comon harme yf▪it growe within court wol knowe ſhal kyng be▪pyled man whiche hath lond tyled awayteth nought redyly herueſt gredely ne maken thenne warde watche profyte myȝten catche yett ful ofte falleth ſoo men may ſeen among hem tho whiche mooſt coueyteth faſt hath leſt auauntage laſt fortune ther ageyne though coueyte veyne happes ben nought al alyche one made pouer another ryche court ſom doth profyte ſom ben euer one plyte yet alyche ſore coueyte fortune vnto one part fauourable though nought reſonable thyng may man ſeen al day wherof telle may enſample remembraunce hou euery man maye take chaūce rycheſſe pouerte hou ſo ſtonde deſerte nought▪euery thyng aguyte ofte man may ſee yet beſt doth leſt ſhal haue helpeth nought worlde craue whiche oute reule meſure hath euer ſtand auenture wel court elles hou al dayes ſtood ſo thynges felle thynke tale telle ic ponit • xhemplum contra illos qui domibns regum ſeruientes pro eo quam ipſi ſecundum eorum cupidita tem promoti non exiſtunt de regio ſer uicio puis e •• nm defectu indiſerete murmurant cronyke rede aboute kyng muſt nede therof knyghtes ſquyers grete route eke offycers som long tyme hym ſeruyd ano thouȝten haue deſeruid auauncement gone withoute ſom also ben route comen whyle agone auaunced anone theſe old men vpon thyng durſt ageyn kyng among hem ſelf compleynen ofte thynge ſayd ſo ſofte ne cometh oute laſt kyng wyſt al faſt whiche hyghe prudence ſhope therfore euydence hem pleynen ca knowe who defaute al within owne entent noman wyſt ment anone bete two cofres make one ſemblaunce one make lyche lyf thylk throwe one may fro knowe chambre brought noman wote brouȝt netheles kyng hath bede ſet pryue ſtede yt wyſedome ſly therto tyme ſygh al pryuelyche none wyſt owne hondes one kyſt fyn gold fyne perrye whiche oute treſorye take anone feld ful cofre ſtrawe mull ſtones meuyd feld alſo thus ful bothe twoo erlyche vpon day bad within lay ſhold fore bed boord vp ſet fayre spred lete cofres fette vpon boord dyde hem ſette knewe name wel tho whiche ayene hym grutched ſo bothe chambre halle anone ſente hem alle ſayd hem wyſe ſhal man hym deſpyſe wote wel ye haue long ſerued god wote ye haue deſerued yf long ye bnauaunced elles yf long yow ſoth ſhal preued ſtoppe euyl word loo two cofres boord theſe whiche lyſt bothe two wyteth wel one tho troſour ſo ful bygone yf ye happe therupone ye ſhal ryche men euer cheſe take whiche leuer wel ware ye take one vndertake maner good therin wherof ye myghten profyte wynne goth gyder one aſſent maketh youre auyſement day auaunce ſtant vpon youre owne chaunce al defaulte grace ſhal ſhewed place vpon alle wel ofyne defaute ſhal myn knelen al one voys kyng thanken choys vp aryſe gone aſyde hem auyſe laſt acorde wherof tale recorde yſſu befalle knyght ſhal ſpeke hem alle kneleth doune kyng ſayth vpon thyng wynne leſe ben al auyſed cheſe tho toke knyhht yerd hond goth cofres ſtond thaſſent eueryehone leyd yard vpon one ſeyth kyng hou thylk ſame cheſe reguerden name preyth hym yt myȝt haue kyng whiche wold honour ſaue hath herd comon voys hath graunteth hem owne choys toke hem therupon keye wold ſeye good haue ſuppoſe bad anone cofre vncloſe fulfilled ſtraw ſtones thus ſerued al one thyng ſame ſtede anone cofre vndede ſawen grete rycheſſe wel couthen geſſe loo ſerth kyng maye ye ſee defaute thy ſelf wol acquyte bereth ye owne wyte fortune hath refuſed thus wyſe kyng excuſed left cuyl ſpeche mercy kyng byſeche nota hic de diuiciarum accidencia vbi narrat qualiter fredericus imperator romanorum duo pauperrs auditut litigantes quorum vnus dixit bene poteſt ditari quem rex vult ditare et alius dixit quem deus vult ditare diues erit que rex cum ad experimentum poſtea probata fuiſſet ille qui deum inuocabat paſtellum auro plenum ſortitus eſt alius vero caponis paſtellum ſorte preelegit ſomdele mater lyke fynde tale hou frederyk rome tyme emperour herde wente grete clamour twoo beggers vpon weye one hem bygan ſeye lord wel may man ryche whome kyng lyſt ryche ſayd thyng ſoo ryche wel begoo whome god wol ſende wele thus maden wordes fele wherof lord hath hede nome dyde hem come paleys ſhal ete bad ordeyne mete two paſteyes whiche lete make capon one bake wynne floreyns al that▪ may within lete put grete rycheſſe euen lyche myght geſſe outward bothe two begger commaunded tho whiche held hym kyng fyrſt cheſe vpon thyng ſaw hem felt hem nought soo vpon owne thought cheſe capon forſoke whiche felawe toke wyſt hou ferde ſeyth aloude men herde certaynly conceyued may lyghtly deceyued tryſteth vnto man helpe wel hym god wol helpe ſtant ſyker ſyde whiche elles ſhold goo beſyde ſee felawe wel recouer mote duelle ſtylle pouer thus ſpak begger entent pouer cam pouer went hath rycheſſe ſought infortuue wold nought soo may ſhewe ſondry wyſe betwene fortune couetyſe chaunce caſt vpon dee yet man may ful ofte ſee inowe ſuche netheles whiche put hem ſelf euer pres gete hem good yet faile ſpeke entayle touchend loue thy matere good ſone thon myght ryght tho men ſtood infortune worldes good thou haſt herd telle aboue ryght ſo ful ofte ſtant loue though thou coueyte euermore thou ſhalt haue noo dele whiche ſhape remenaunt iape netheles nowe tho ben coueyte ſoo woman ſee ye ten twelue though ther loue ſo vnauyſed beaute ſtant aſſyſed mannes herte anone rouneth tale ere ſeyth loueth ſtreyte thus ſette hym coueyte honderd though ſawe day ſholde may grete couetyſe ſotye fool empryſe eche hem fynt ſomwhat pleſeth hym one ſhe whyte kyn one ſhe noble kyn one ſhe hath rody cheke one ſhe ſemeth meke one ſhe hath eyen greye one ſhe laugh pleye one ſhe long ſmal one ſhe lyte tal one ſhe pale bleche one ſhe ſofte ſpeche one ſhe camuſed one ſhe hath vſed one ſhe dauuce ſynge ſome thyng lykyuge fynt though fele ſhe hath lytel hele inough therfore hyr loue thus honderd ſcore whyle newe wold whome forſaketh ſhe ſhal bad blynde man colour demeth al one ryght hym ſemeth soo hath luſt iugement couetyſe loue blent hym thynketh couetyſe al world ne may ſuffyſe wylle wold haue alle myght ſo byfalle soo comon ſtrete ſet nought beyete ſone haſt thou ſuche couetyſe nay fader ſuche loue deſpyſe whyle lyue ſhal done euer good feyth yet leuer coueyte ſuche weye ben euer tyl deye poure iob loueles taken one haules thankes noman lyue man ſhold al vnthryue ought wyſeman coueyte lawe ſet ſo ſtreyte thy ſelf al ſaue suche one ther wold haue noue al theſe mo ſone thou woldeſt ſoo nought wroth bnt ouer wol telle hou men whiche otherwyſe ryght ouly couetyſe ſee woman ryche wol al hyr loue affyche nonght beaute face ne yet vertu ne grace whiche ſhe hath elles ryght inough park plough thynges whiche therto lō geth none otherwyſe ther longeth loue yf profyt fynde yf profyte behynde hyr loue euer leſſe leſſe ſhe hath rycheſſe loue proporcyon thou haſt ſuche condycyon ſone telle ryght myn holy fader nay iwys condycyon ſuche haue none truly fader loue one well al myn hertes thouḡht certes though ſhe nought poure medea whiche exyled creuſa wold hyr nought leſſe loue ne though ſhe hyr aboue ryche quene canda • e whiche deſerue loue grace alyſander kyng yofe many worthy ryche thyng elles pantaſylee whiche quene femyne grete rycheſſe hyr nam ſhe loue hector cam troye reſcous toune ſuche condycyon though lady hyr ſelue alſo ryche ſuche twelue couthe though ſo better loue hyr loue ſo pleyne wyſe ſpeke couetyſe pouerte rycheſſe loue nouther ne leſſe good feyth tro couetous man lady ſyghe thorugh lokyng eye ne ſholde haue ſuche ſtroke withyn gold myght wyn ſhold nought hyr loue aſterte yf lefte herte ſo ſuche man coutheſkylle woman men ſo rude ſome among woman come gone vnder protectyon loue affectyon ne ſhal take hem ſleue ben oute byleue hem luſteth lady cheere euer thynkend gold cofte wol none loue profre ſo wote loue amoūteth reſon trulyche acompteth may knowe taken hede al luſt womanhede whiche may ben lady face lady hath eke grace men ſhold yeuen apryſe maye wel ſeye hou ſhe wyſe ſobre ſymple contenaunce al good gouernaunce belongeth worthy wyght hath pleynly thylk nyght ſhe bore none nature ſet hyr al one beaute bounte ſo byſeyn maye wel afferme ſeyn ſawe yet neuer creature comlyheede feture ony kynges regyon lyche hyr comparyſon therto haue told yet hath ſhe thouſand fold bounte ſhortely telle pure heede welle myrroure enſample good ſo hyr vertues vnderſtood thynketh ought ynough ſuffyſe withouten couetyſe loue ſuche one ſerue whiche hyr chere deſerue byloued better ywys ſhe par ca rycheſt hath gold mylyon suche hath myn opynyon euer ſhal neuertheles ſaye nought ſhe haueles ſhe ny ryche wel eſe hath inough pleſe worldes good whome hyr lyſt one thyng wold wel ye wyſt neuer worldes good myn hert vnto hyr ward ſtood ryght purr loue wote hyghe god aboue fader ye ſay therto confeſſor ſone ſaye wel doo take ryght good byleue man wol hym ſelf releue loue ony wyſe ſhal wel fynde couetyſe shal ſore greue hym laſt ſuche loue may laſt men ſeyn oure dayes men taken fewe aſſayes yf cauſe rycheſſe thy loue wel leſſe wold enſamples telle old dayes felle myght man wel vnderſtond suche loue may long ſtonde herkne ſone thou ſhalt grete enſample matere hic ponit exemplum contra iſtos qui non propter amorem ſed propter diuicias ſponſalia ſumunt et narrat de quodam regis apubic seneſcalla qui non ſolum propter pecuniam vxorem duxit ſed eciam pecunie come • ci vxorem ſibi deſponſatam vendidit trete vpon ca loue soo tolden aboue fynde wryte wōder thyng puyle whyſome kyng man hyghe complexyon yong affectyon nature age yet falle courage luſt woman knowe soo betyd vpon throwe lord felle grete ſekenes phiſyk hath done heſynes ſondry cure many one make hym hoole therupon worthy mayſter whiche ther yafe hym counſeyl vpon ca yf wold haue parfyte heele ſhold woman dele freſſhe yong luſty wyght done hym compauye nyght ſayd hym redely ſhal al hole ther otherwyſe knewe cure kyng ſtode auenture lyf deth medycyne aſſented couyne ſtyward whome truſteth wel took told hym euery del hou mayſter hath ſeyd therupon hath hym prayd charged vpon lygeaunce make purueaunce ſuche one couenable pleſaunce delytable bad hym hou euer ſtood ſhal ſpare good wylle ryght wel paye ſtyward ſeyd wold aſſaye bnt thou ſhalt wyte fynde bokes wryte couetyſe loue doth ſtyward telle ſoth amonges al men lyue luſty lady hath wyue whiche netheles gold took nouȝt loue ſeyth book ryche marchaunt lond hyr fader hyr fond worthely ſuche rycheſſe worldes good ſuche largeſſe hyr yafe maryage thylk auauntage gold ſtyward hath hyr take lucre nought loues ſake ſtiward wel ſene herkne wol mene ſtyward owne herte sowe lord may aſterte maladye haue luſty woman hym ſaue though wold yeue inough treſour wherof drough grete couetyſe mynde ſet honour fer behynde thus whome gold hath ouerſet trapped owne net gold hath made wyttes lame soo ſechend owne ſhame rouneth kynges ere ſeyd wyſte gentyl luſty one tho thyder wolde gone mote yiue yeftes grete yf thurgh grete beyete gold ſeyd ſhold ſpede kyng hym bad vpon nede take honderd pound ſhold yeue wolde ſo worthy place thus ſtonde loues grace king gold hath habandouned tale ful rouned styward toke gold went within hert many went couetyſe caſt wherof purpoos laſt ayene loue ayene ryght toke ſayd hou thylk nyght wyf ſhal lygge kynḡ goth thynkend vpon thyng toward inne tyl ca home chambre nome wyf told hyr al ca ſhe whiche rede ſhame hyr handes hath hym praid • enelend wyſe ſayd ſhe reſon ſkylle thyng bydde wylle redy done heſte thyng honeſt gold ſhold ſelle tho wordes felle forth gaſtely contenaunce seyth ſhe ſhal done obeyſaunce folowe wylle euery place thus thurgh ſtrengthe nace innocence ouerlad wherof ſhe ſo ſore adrad ſhe wylle mote nede obeye therupon ſhape weye owne wyf nyghte hath oute al mennes ſyght pryuely none wiſt brouȝt kyng hym liſt may doo hyr wolde ſhe ſhe ſholde hym bedde vnder cloth ſtyward took leue goth chambre faſt hou ſlepte wote ſawe cauſe ielouſye whiche hath companye ſuche luſty one ſhe hym thought degre noman ſo wel eſe doth al ſhe may pleſe soo al hert ſhe thus kyng ioye lad tyl nyhe vpon day styward ſhe lay cam bedde wyſe hath bede ſhe ſhold aryſe kyng ſayd nay ſhe ſhold go ſtyward ſayd ageyne nought ſoo ſhe mote gone er knowe ſo ſwore ylke throwe fette kyng tale wold ſeyth hou hath hir bouȝt thy ſhe ſhal departe nought tyl bryght day holde armes gan hyr folde whiche lyſt pleye bad ſtyward gone aweye ſoo dyd ayene wylle thus wyf bedde ſtylle lay king long nyght tyl hyghe ſonne lyght ſhe knewe thyng tho cam ſtyward kyng prayd hym withoute ſhame ſauyng owne name myght leden home ayene lady told hym pleyne hou owne wyf kyng ere vnto ſtryf hath leyd herde wel nyhe oute wyt ferde ſayd caytyf mooſt al euer byfalle ony coward wyſe betoke wyf conetyſe thou haſt hyr begyled eke thyne owne eſtate reuyled wherof buxome vnto ſhal ſhe neuer auowe god make day yf take thou ſhalt honged drawe loke anone thou withdrawe soo ſee neuer styward drad hym ſore al haſt may fled awey ſame day exyled oute lond loo nyce hyſbond whiche thus wif hath loſt euer netheles ſhe leuer kyng hyr weddeth honoureth wherof hyr name ſhe ſecoureth whiche erſt loſt thurgh couetyſe hym lad hyr wyſe hath hym ſelf alſo forlore ſone thou ware therfore thou ſhalt loue ony place thou couetyſe embrace whiche loues kynde al man may fynde tyme thylk rage ful grete dyſeſe maryage venym medleth ſucrē maryage made lucre luſt hele man ſhal dele may fayle repente fader ſuche myn entente netheles good haue good may oftyme ſaue loue whiche ſhold elles ſpylle god wote hertes wille dar wel take wytneſſe yet neuer rycheſſe ſett maryage none al myn herte vpon one frely perſone stant al worldes ioye alone axe nother park ne plough hyr inough hyr loue ſhold ſuffyſe withouten couetyſe loo fader touchend ryght ſhryfte knowe pleyn yf yr wol ought elles ſeyn couetyſe yf ther loue agropeth oute ſore fallere cum nequeat propria vir fraude ſubornat teſtes ſic que eis vera retorta fides sicut agros cupidus dū querit amans mulieres vult teſtes falſos falſus habere ſuos non ſine vi dictum periurus abibit eis viſu qui cordis intima cuncta videt fallere per iuro non eſt laudanda puella glori ſet falſo condicionis opus hic tractat ſuper illis auaricie ſpeciebus que falſum teſtimonium et periurum nūcupantur quorum fraudulenta circumuencio tam cupiditatis que amoris cauſa ſui deſiderij propoſitum quam ſepe fallaciter attingit ſone thou ſhalt vnderſtonde hou couetyſe hath yet hōde ſpecyal two coūſeyllours ben alſo procurours fyrſt hem fals wytneſſe whiche euer redy wytneſſe thyng maiſter wol hym hote periure ſecond hote whiche ſpareth nought ſwere oth though fals god wroth one ſhal fals wytnes bere ſhal thyng ſwere charged booke hepe croke make mayſter ofte wynne wol know ſinne couetyſe thus men ſeyn make many fals barḡeyn may trewe quarel aryſe thylk queſte thylk aſſyſe two people enforme kepe euer one maner forme vpon gold conſcyence founde take euydence thus fals wytnes othes wynne hem mete drynk clothe • ryght ſo hem knewe theſe louers ful many vntrewe may woman fynde ynowe eche hem ſhal wowe anone wold hand doune leyn vpon book ſwere ſeyn wol feyth trouthe bere thus profereth hym ſwe • e • ſe • uen euer tyl deye al trecherye ſoth hym ſelf tryeth ſw • reth lyeth feyth maketh al ther • ſt may woman truſte hym leſt tyl may wylle acheue l • nger leue thus trouthe loue exyled • • good woman begyled eke ſpeke fals wytneſſe ſuche many g • ſſe lyche vnto prouyſours make hem preuy procura tour telle hou ſuche man whiche worthy loue al good man ſholde conne soo leſyng hath bygōne cauſe whiche wol procede alſo ſyker crede make knowen fals thus ful ofte aboute hals loue fals men embraced loue whiche ſo purchaced come afterward lytel pryſe thy ſone yf thou wyſe thou haſt herd euydence thou myght thyne owne conſcyence oppoſe yf thou haſt ſuche one nay god wote fader none ne neuer men ſeyth man ſhal make feyth herte tonge muſt acorde yf ſo dyſcorde fals elles nought dare ſay thought loue dyſcordable vnto word • ordablo wyſe fader may ryght wel ſwere ſaufly lady loue wel acordeth euery del nedeth nought ſoth ſawe wytneſſe ſhold drawe day neuer yett ne myght ſynke wyt counſeyl ſhold ſeye ony wyght bewreye ſechen helpe ſuche manere lady dere though thouſand men wyſ • loue • em lyſt ſwer • witneſſe yet fals wytneſſe dare vnto trouthe dwelle loue telle thus fader gylteles ye haue herd nethele • dome put al ſone wyte ſpecyal ſhal comonlyche fayle al though tyme faylle fals wytneſſe cauſe ſpede vpon poynt falſheede ſhal afterward kyd wherof ſo betyd enſample ſuche thynges blynde cronyke wryte fynde hic ponit exemplum de illis qui falſum teſtificantes amoris innocenciam circumu • niunt et narrat qualiter • achillem filium ſuum adoleſcē tem muliebri veſtitum apparatu aſſerens eſſe puellam inter regis lichomedis filias ad educandum produxit et ſi • achilles • cepto rege filie ſue deidamie ſocia et cubicularia effectus ſuper ipſam pir • um geniut▪ qui poſte mire probitatis mil̄iciam aſſecutus mortem patris ſui apud troiam polix ene tirannice vindicauit goddeſſe ſee thetis ſone name achilles kepe warde whyle yong ward thought hym ſaufly take ſhe whiche drad ſake ſayd prophecye troy • ſhold dye cyt • byleyn thy ſo bokes ſeyn caſt hyr wyt ſondry wyfe hou ſhe hym myght ſo deſguyſe man ſhold body knowe ſo byf • lle ylke throwe whyle ſhe thou • vpon dede kyng whiche lychomede hote wel begone fayre doughters many one duelt f • r oute yle ſhalt thou wonder wyle quene whiche moder achilles vpon ca hyr ſ •• e mayden lete cloth •• ſame gere whiche longeth vnto womanhede yong toke •• hede ſuffreth al • hat ſhe hym dede wherof ſhe hath hyr woman bede chargeth othe • alle hou ſo afterward byfalle dyſcouer nought •• ng feyne make knoulechyng vpon counſeyl whiche nom • euery place come telle wytneſſe hyr lady doughter ryght ſuche maner wiſe bad ſhold done ſeruyſe achilles vnderfongeth yong lady belongeth honoure ſeruyce reuerence thetys grete dylygen •• hym hath ſo taught affayted hou ſo 〈◊〉 awayted ſobre go • tely contenaunce ſhold womanhede auaunce none ſoth knowe myght euery man ſyght ſhold ſeme pure maide ſuche wiſe ſhe hym ſaide achilles whiche ilke yong vpon hym ſmyle bigan ſo beſein thus bokes ſein frette perle vpon hede al freſſhe bitwene white rede ſhe whiche tho tendre age stood colour viſage loke vpon cheke ſeen childy maner eke woman beholde moder tolde ſhe ſoo begone cauſe ſhe thought gone lichomede thilke tyde ſhe ſayd ſhold abyde among doughters duelle achilles herd moder telle wyſt nonght cauſe netheles ful buxo •• ly redy ſ • e bad wherof mode • ryght glad lychomede forth went whe • • kyng knewe entent ſ • youg doughter cam vnto ere ſuche record ſuche wytneſſe ryght grete gladneſſe ſoth ſawe herde wote hou ferde vpon counſeyl nede al kyng lychomede hath toward hym doughter take thetys moder ſake put hyr companye duelle deydamye owne doughter eldeſt fayreſt comlyeſt al doughters whiche loo thus thetys cauſe lad left ther achilles feyned whiche hath hym ſelf reſtreyned al euer may oute maner man took womannyſſh chere wherof vnto bedfere deydamye hath nyght kynde wold hym ſelue • yght philoſophers ſeyn may wyght ther ageyn thylk tyme ſene long nyghtes hem bytwene nature whiche may forbere hath made hem bothe ſtere kyſſen fyrſt ouermore hyghe wey loues lore gone al done dede whorof loſt maydenhede aud afterward wel know byfel ylk throwe troye ſyege lay vpon cauſe menelay quene dame eleyn • greg • y hadden moche p • yne al day fyght aſſayle myght nought auayle soo noble cyte wynne pryue counſeyll begynne ſondry wyſe tret • laſt among grete▪ fellen vnto acord phor • eu record whiche aſtronomyen eke grete magycyen▪ shold calculacyon serche conſtellacyon hou cyte myghten gete whiche nought foryet • belongeth clerk ſtudy ſet vpon werk long aboute wytte caſt tyl fond oute • laſt yf hadden achylles • werre ſhal endeles oner told hem pleyn manere byſeyn place ſhal founde soo within lytel ſtounde vlyxes forth dyomede vpon poynt lychomed • agamen geder ſent vlyxes forth went whiche one mooſt wyſe ordeyned hath ſuche wyſe mooſt rycheſt aray wherof woman may gay hym took manyfolde ouermore told harnoys luſty knyght whiche burued ſyluer bryght ſwerde plate eke mayle though ſhold doo batayle took alſo hym ſhyp thus geder felauſhyp forth dyomede hope tyl myghten ſee place achylles wynde ſtood • mys euery topſeyle cole blewe tyl vlyxes march knewe lychomede regne ſtyreſman ſo wel hym lad comen ſauf londe gone oute vpon ſtronde burgh foūd kyng whiche hath facounde vlyxes dyd meſſage counſeyl courage cam told nought vndernethe bethought maner myght aſpye achilles deydamye fro theſe ful many luſty lady pleyd day two fortuned ſo fel tyme ſuche wyſe bachus ſacryfyce theſe yong ladyes ſhold make ſo ſtraunge mennes ſake come fro ſyege troye maden wel ioye reuel daunſyng euery lyf whiche couthe ſyng luſty woman route freſſhe carolle hath ſonge aboute al netheles grekes vnknowe achilles degre • outhen wyte whiche ne voys ne paas vlyxes vpon caas thyng high prudence hath wrouȝt thylk aray whiche hath bouȝt yeue among woman let • fetten al gere forth knyghtes harnoys eke al countre ſeke men ſholden nought fay • er ſee euery thyng degre endelong vpon boorde leyde lychomede preyde euery lady cheſ • ſholde thyng al ſhe wold take wey yefte hem ſelf ſhold ſhefte ſayde owne wylle achylles ſtood nought ſtylle bryght hel • e beheld ſwerde hauberk ſhelde hert felle therto anone al▪ wold none knyghtes ge • e vnderfongeth thylk array whiche belōgeth vnto woman forſoke wyſe ſeyth booke knowen whiche goth forth grete paas chambre lay anone made delay armeth hym knyghtely wyſe better man deuyſe fortune ſholde falle cam forth fore hem alle whiche tho glad inough lychomede thyng lough ſawe ferde wyſt wel herde doughter forleyn ſo ouerſeyn wonder ouergoth wyt cronyke wreton yet thyng whiche ſhal neuer foryete hou achilles hath byge • e pyrrus vpon deydamye wherof cam oute trecherye fals wytnes ſayde hou achylles mayde thyng ſene tho ſyege go forth vlyxes dyoinede loo thus proued dede fully ſpoke thylk whyle one woman another begyle ony ſekyrneſſe thetys whiche goddeſſe deydamye hath ſo beiaped hou ſhal ben eſcaped tho woman who innocence al day thorugh ſuche credence deceyued ofte ſene men ſuche vntrouthe mene ben ſlye ſuche wyſe ſleyghte queyntyſe fals wytneſſe bryngen inne doth hem ofte wynne worthy therw thy ſone doo ſoo fader fals wytneſſe trouthe maner expreſſe touchend loue hou bath ferd ye haue told haue wel herd ye ſayden otherwyſe hou thylk vyce couetyſe hath yet periure acord thou lyſt ſom record telle another tale alſo loues cauſe tyme ago thyng forſwore wolde preye therfore wherof myght enſample take good ſone thy ſake touchand ſhal fulfylle thyn axyng thyne owne wylle matere ſhal declare woman deceyued ſo tender herbe men ſo ſwere cometh thaſſay ther fynde fals another day iaſon dyde medee whiche ſtant yet auctoryte tokne memoryal wherof tale ſpecyal book troye wryte whiche ſhal wyte hic amoris cauſa ponit exemplum contra perinros et narrat qualiter iaſon priuſ quam ad inſulam col chos pro aureo vellere ibidem conqueſtando tranſmearet amorem couiugium regis othonis filie iuramento firmius ſe aſtrinxit ſed ſuo poſtea completo negocio cū ipſā ſecū nauigio ī greciā perduxiſſet vbi illa ſenectā patris ſui eſonis floridam iuuentutem mirabili ſciencia reformauit ipſe iaſon fidei ſue ligamento alijs que beneficijs poſt poſitis dictam medeam pro quadam cauſa regis creontis filia periurus dereliquit grece whylome kyng fame knoulechyng byleueth yet peleus hyghte felle hym thus fortune hyr whele ſo lad chylde owne regne deceſſe broder netheles who ryght name eſon hath worthy knyght iaſon bygoten whiche euery lond al paſſed hond armes ſo beſt named worthyeſt ſought worſhyp oueral herkne telle ſhal auenture ſought whiche afterward ful dere bought ile whiche colchos cleped therof awos grete ſpeche londe aboute ſuche meruayle none oute al wyde world nowhere tho ile ſhepe told whiche flees bare al gold ſo goddes ſette ne myght wey fette power worldes wyght yet ful many worthy knyght aſſayed dorſt euer fel hem worſt wold nought forſake knyghthode vndertake doo thyng therto belongeth worthy iaſon ſore alongeth ſee ſtraunge regyons knowe condycyous march went cauſe hoole entent ſet colchos ſeke therupon dyde▪ ſpeke peleus eme kyng wel payd thyng ſhope anone paſſage suche lygnage knyghtes whiche chees hym toke hercules whiche ful chyualrye iaſon wente companye moneth may colde ſtormes away wynd good ye ſhyp yare took hyr leue forth fare toward colchos weye hem byfelle long ſeye hou lamedon kyng troye whiche ought wel haue made hem ioyr reſt whyle hym preide oute lond hem congeyde ſo felle dyſſencyon whiche afterward deſtructyon cyte men may matere thus worthy folk here away paſſed ben cold ſhoures ryght ſo recouereth floures loo myght ony man deuyſe woman ſhewe ony wyſe hertely loue ony ſtede medea iaſon dede fyrſt ſhe made hym flees wyn alle kyth kyn grete treſour hym ſhe ſtal fader forth al elde hath torned youthe whiche thyng none man couth hou hyr • uyt remembraunce duelleth yet kyng peleus eme deed iaſon bare coroune beede medea hath fulfylled wylle ſhold ryght fulfylle trouthe whiche hyr afore • le colchos swore tho medea mooſt deceyued hath another receyued whtch • doughter kynge creon creuſa ſhe byght thus iaſon loue vntrewe medea left toke newe afterward ſore abought medea hyr art hath wrought cloth gold mantel ryche whiche ſemeth worth kynges ryche vnto creuſa ſent name yeft preſent ſuſterhood hem bytwene yong freſſhe quene mantyl lappyd hyr aboute none therof fyre ſprang oute brent hyr bothe fleſſhe bone tho cam medea iaſon ſones hond ſayd thou euery lond mooſt vntre creature loo ſhal thy forfeture ſhe bothe ſones ſlough byfore eye oute drough ſwerd wold haue ſlayn hyr tho fare wel ſhe goo vnto pallas court aboue ſhe pleyneth vpon loue ſhe goddeſſe left grete dyſtreſſe thus myȝt thou ſee ſorow doth ſwere othe whiche ſoth loues cauſe namely ſone wel ware thy kepe thou forſwore whiche haue told tofore ouyde telleth euery dele fader may leue wele haue herde ofte ſeye hou iaſon toke flees aweye fro colchos yet herd nought fyrſt thyder brouȝt good thou lyſt prayere telle wold byſeche ſone wol ſeche bokes may fynde wryte netheles yf thou wolt wyte maner thou haſt preyde ſhal telle hou ſeyde nota qualiter aureum vellus pardes inſule colchos primo deuenit athemas rex philen habiut coniugem 〈◊〉 qua faxum genuit et hellen mortua autem hellen athemas iunonem regis cadmi filiam poſtea 〈◊〉 vxorem dnxit que nouerce di • tos infā te tantum recollegit odi • que ambo mari proici penis regem procurauit vnde iuno compaciens quemdam arietem grandem aureo veſtitum vellere ad litus natantem deſtinauit • ſuper cuius dorſum pueros apponi iuſſit quo facto aries ſuper vndas regreſſus cum ſolo frixo ſibi adherente colchos applicuit vbi iuno dictum arietem cū suo vellere prout alijs canitur • coni • ſub • ta cuſtodia collocauit fame thylk ſhepes felle colchos bifelle al gold ſhal neuer deye wherof thynke ſeye hou cam fyrſt ile kyng thylk whyle wardes grece athemas cronyke name wyf whiche phylen hyght whome ſo fortune dyght chyldren yong two fay • fyrſt tho man chylde ryght fayre doughter eke whiche men call hellen hade wyf ther may man lyf endure vpon erthe worthy quene thou myȝt er chyldren age took ende paſſage grete worſhyp bygraue thyng lyketh god haue grete reaſon ben thy thys kyng ſo grete ſuffraūce vnderfongeth afterward hym belongeth tyme wedde newe wyf toke bedde whiche iuo hyght mayde eke doughter men ſayde cadme whiche kyng alſo holde thylke dayes tho iuo kynges make caſt hou ſhe myght make theſe chyldre hyr fadre loth ſhope wyle ayene hem vnto kyng vnknow yere two ſhe ſete doo ſowe lond ſoden whete aboute wherof corn may ſpryngen oute thus ſleyghte couyne aroos derthe famyne thorugh oute lond ſuche wyſe soo kyng ſacryfyce vpon poynt dyſerrſſe cere whiche goddeſſe corne hath ſhape hym yeue loke yf may foryeue meſchyef whiche lond ſhe whiche knewe fore hond cyraimſtaunce al thys thyng ageyn comynge kyng temple hath ſhape ſoo hyr acord al tho whiche temple preſtes haue ſayd ful declared vnto kyng yf ſo deſyuer countre fryxus hellen bothe whome goddes ben ſo wrothe whyle tho chyldre ben within suche tylthe ſhal man begyn wherof gete hym ony corn thus ſayd thus ſworn al preſtes ſhe whiche cauſeth al fare seyd eke therto ſhe wolde euery man tolde soo quene hem preyd kyng whiche bath ere leyd leueth al euer herde vnto tale thus anſuerde ſeyth leuer hym cheſe chyldren bothe leſe hym al remenaunt hem whiche apperdendunt vnto lond whiche ſhal kepe bade wyf take kepe manere beſt done delyuerd ſone oute world ſhe anone two men ordeyneth gone fyrſt ſhe made hem ſwere chyldren ſhold vnto ſee none knowe hem therin throwe child ſee ben lad wyſe yuo bad theſe men redy doo goddeſſe whiche iuno hote appereth ſtede hath vnto men forbede chyldren ne ſlee▪ bad hem loke ſee taken hede ſyghen ſwam ſheepe fore hyr eyen whoos flees burned gold al goddeſſe forth al comaundeth withoute let ſhold anone chyldre ſet aboue vpon ſhepes bak al ryght ſhe ſpak wherof men gone home ageyne felle ſo bokes ſeyne hellen yong mayden tho whiche ſee wo bego pure drede hyr hert hath lore fro ſhepe whiche hath hyr bore ſhe ſwounend feynt felle hyr ſelf deeynt frixus ſhepe forth ſwam tyl ile colchos cam iuno goddeſſe fond whiche toke ſhepe lond ſ • tte ſuche wyſe thou fere haſt herd deuyſe wherof cam • al wo iaſon forſwore ſoo vnto mede • ſpoke fader hath broke trouth ye haue told worthy loue ne beloued ſemeth euery loue ne quemeth hym whiche newe fangle netheles thou lyſt taken hede vpon ſhryfte procede loues cauſe ayene vyce couetyſe auoryce wold wyte ſone fynde wryte yet one thylk brood whiche worldes good make treſoure moneye put al conſcyence weye wherof thy confeſſyon name condycyon ſhal afterwarde declare whiche maketh one ryche another bare plus capit vſura ſibi quam debetur et illud fraude colocata ſepe latenter agit sic amoz exceſſus quam ſepe ſuos vt cuarus spirat et viuus tres capit ipſe loco hic tractat de illa ſpecie auaricie que vſura dicitur cuius creditor pecunia tantum numerata plus quam ſibi de iure debetur incrementum lucri ad auget • pon benche ſyttend hyȝ auaryce vſure ſyghe ful clothed owne ſute whiche good maketh chaſe ſute brocours renne aboute lyche vnto ratch route suche lucre none aboue ground whiche ratch founde ſee beyete ſterte ſhal hem wyſe aſterde dryue net lucre whiche vſure hath ſet vſure ryche duelleth al euer byeth ſelleth hath ordeyned ſleyghte meſure • double double weyghte outward ſelleth laſſe maketh taſſe wherof hous ful withynne retcheth nought ſoo wynne though leſe ten twelue loue al toward hym ſelue none ſee may wynne ſuche thre ſhal ought yeue lene wol ayene ward take bene hath lent ſmal peſe ryght ſo ther many theſe louers though they▪ loue lyte ſcarſely wold weye myte yet wold haue pound ageyne doth vſure bargeyn certes ſuche vſure vnlyche falleth vnto ryche al wel loue beyete vnto hem grete ſayth ſymple pouer ſelden recouer yf thorugh greete deſerte netheles men ſee pouerte purſute contenaunce ful ofte make grete cheuaunce take loue auauntage helpe brocage maken ſeme nought thus ful ofte loue bought lytel mochel take fals weyghtes make ſone ſayd aboue thou woſt vſure loue telle thy ſo thou wylt thou therof hoſt ony gylt fader nay ought tho poyntes ye tolden wol trouth aſſure weyghte loue meſure hath large certeyn euer took loue ageyne ſo yet couthe neuer ſleyghte take ageyne double weyghte loue haue yeue alſo wy mote ſhryue haue remyſſyon ſynne ſoo yet couthe neuer wynne ne yet ſoo mochel ſoth ſeyn euer myght haue half ageyn ſo ful loue haue lent myn hop ſo wel went hoole myght haue half thynketh goddeſſe half vſure wold haue double conſcyence trouble byd neuer dele hole haluen dele none exceſſe thynketh netheles forthynketh wel wote wol euery day better ſee ho • ſo euer yeue lene loue place mene ought euer axe craue nothyng ayeneward haue wol lete ſo befalle beyete ne ſhal yeue lene loue al thought ſoo clene toward ſhal nougt byleue yf ſhe hyr good leue rewarde wold nought ageyn wote laſt bargeyn shal ſtonde vpon ſo grete loſt may neuer coſt recouer world tyl dye soo touchend partye may wel excuſe ſhal ſpeke forth al ouy brocour went poynt cam neuer myn entent soo meruayleth thyng lady eyleth al myn herte al tyme hath doo better byme haue herd ſayd thouȝt fre netheles pryuete fader ben myn hole ſhryfte dar myn hert wel dyſcloſe touchend vſure ſuppoſe whiche ye tellen loue vſed lady may ben excuſed one lokyng hyr eye myn hool herte hath tyl deye al euer may hath wonne hyr man wherof thynketh good reſon wolde ſhe ſomdele rewarde ſholde yeue part ſhe hath al falle herafter ſhal yet dare ſeyne hyr lyſt neuer yeue ageyne good word ſuche wyſe wherof myne hope myght aryſe greete loue compenſe hou ſhe hyr conſcyence excuſe wol vſure large weyghte grete meſure hath loue haue nought whiche haue dere abought myne herte haue payde al aſyde layde go loueles aboute hyr ought ſtonde ryght grete doute tyl ſhe redreſſe ſuche ſynne ſhe wol al loue wynne yeueth lyue nought alſo moche graunt mercy hyr lyſt ſeye whiche myght greete peyne alyght poynt lo thus fare payeth chaffare byeth dere yet hath none mote nedes pouer gone thus bye dere haue loue ne may come aboue wynne loue none encrece wylle neuer leſe touchend vſure loue acquyte yf lady wyte pray god ſuche grace hyr ſende ſhe tyme muſt amende ſone thou haſt anſwerd touchend vſure haue al herd thou loue haſt wonnen ſmale thou telleſt thy tale thy lady therof accuſiſt thynketh thy wordes thou myſuſiſt thyne owne knowlechyng thou ſaiſt ſhe one lokyng thy hole herte fro ſhe took may ſuche hyr one look worth herte many fold haſt thou thy herte wel ſold whan thou haſt worthy alſo thou telleſt thy hyr weyght loue vneuen maye thy ſemyng vnder heuen stonde euer euen balaunce ſtondeth loues gouernāce suche ſtatute lawe though thy loue drawe peyſe balaunce thou may aſke ageyn ther fore doubte grace loue lord euery place may lawe hym iuſtyfye • eddour ne companye ne wylle wylle hym liketh ſpede ſpille loue man may wel begynne whether ſhalle leſe wynne wote man till laſt therfore coueyte faſt ſone abyde thyn ende per c • al may good wende thou haſt told ſaid one thyng ryght wel payd thou ſleyghte ne gyle brocoure haſt whyle engyned loue ſuche dede venged rede hic ponit exemplum contra iſtos marituss ▪ qui vltra id quod proprias habent vxores ad noue voluptatis crementum alias company mayden ful trechery ſhe euer one acord iubiter hyr lord gete hym loues newe thorugh ſuche brocage vntrew al wyſe hym nedeth ſhe whiche ſhame dredeth queynt wordes ſlye blynded ſuche wiſe ladyes eye ſhe whome iuno tryſt ther ſhe thyng wyſt ſo pryuely may thyng ne cometh knowlechyng thyng yt done derk nyȝt knowen whan day liȝt befelle laſt al ſlyghe mayden caſt ouer caſt ouerthrowen arte pryue theſe doynges ful oft thy beſynges deceyued haſt day whyle wel quyte may thou haſt counceyled lord hath deled ſhalle ſet ſuche kynde euer vnto worldes ende al thou hereſt thou ſhalt telle
