delyueraunce til ageyne eue felle per chaunce whylo bicam nyght poure man bardus hyght come forth walkend aſſe gadred hym taſſe grene ſtykkes drye▪ ſelle whome wold hem bey • lyuelode myght ſuche loode towne aſſhe carye felle hym tarye ſame tyme nyhe pytte truſſe faſt knyt •• herd voyce cryed dymme ere brymme hath leyd herd man ſeid help adryan wylle geue al good poure man vnderſtood wold gladly wyn lord within ſpak ſaid yf ſaue ſikernes ſhalle haue couenaunt afterward thow wilt gyue ſuche reward thou behyghteſt beforne hath othe ſworne heuen goddes alle myght ſo bifalle hym oute pytt brought goodes ought ſhal haue euen haluendele bardus ſeid wold wele word aſſe anon • vntruſſe therupon doune goth co • pyt whiche hath ende knyt ſtaf wherby ſaid wold adryan hym ſhold hold thenne per • fallen pytte ſo fallen ape whiche throwe whan rope doune cam lowe ſodenly therto ſkypte bothe armes clypte bardus aſſe anon hym hath vpdrawen gone ſawe ape wend ben • iape fayry ſore hym dradde adryan eftſones gradd • help cryed faſt eftſones cord caſt whan come vnto grounde grete ſerpent hath bewound • whiche bardus anon vp drough hym thought wel ynough hit fanton b • yet herd voyce therto anſwerd arte thou goddes name quod adryan ſame whiche good thou ſhalt haue euen half od bardus god half thyrd tyme aſſay ſhall caſte cord forth pytte came hym lord rome nam • therupon hym hath dreſſid hond ful ofte bleſſi • bad bardus hale vnderſtood tale bitwene hym aſſe al ſofte hath drawen ſet hym vp lofte without • harme eſyly ſaid one graunt mercy forth hym went cyte lete poure bardu • neuertheles ſymple ••• couenaunt ſo ca • hath aſked ye anſwerd ſaid yf ſo yt hym vp braide ought hath ſpoken done ſhall wroken hym ſoone hym better dede none rede aſſe ageyne caſt truſſe hyed hym homeward faſt cam home bedde told wyf ſpedde fynally ſpeke ought • nto lord dradde hym ſore one word durſt ſey • ſo vpon morowe ageyne maner recorde forth aſſe cord gader woode er goth cometh ther • nto place wold gan ape anone behold whiche gadred al aboute ſtykkes rowte leyd hem redy hond wherof made • iſſe bonde fro day day wyſe thus profered ſeruyſe woode ynough vpon tyme drough toward woode ſawe beſide grete gaſtly ſerpent glyde til ſhe came preſence hir kynd reuerence hath hym done forth ſtone bryght caſtalle oute hir mouthe way lete doune falle went hir way ſhold adrad thenne poure bardus gladde •• end god ſtone goeth taketh vp anone hath grete wonder wytte beeſt hym hath quytte man hath failed whome mooſt trauayled put goddes honde torn • home fond • nto wyf hath ſhewde bothe lewd • ••• den ſhold ſelle l • nger wold dwelle forthe anone vpon tale ſtone profereth ſale ryght hym ſelf ſette •• wler anone hym fette gold made payement therof none delayement thus ſtone boȝt ſold homeward ioye many fold bardus goth came home hows nam • gold oute purſe within fond alſo ſtone therin wherfor ioye hert playd wyf thus ſaid ••• gold loo ſton • wyf wonder therupon aſked hym myght trouthe quod dare ſwere vpon book marchaunt took went knowe entent thurgh god grace thy morow place • wyl aſſay ſelle yf wol hym dwelle •• pe purſe ageyne dare ſauely ſwere ſeyn • • vertue ſtone morowe cam gone 〈◊〉 aboute ſtede ſtone ſelle ſo dede left chapman • whan cam e • preſence wyf home oute p • r anone nome gold fond ſtone • thus felle hym ••• ral ſold dyuerſe place suche fortune grac • ſo wel maye thyng b • hyd ne laſt kyd fame goth aboute rome • ferforth wordes come emperour iuſtynyan lete ſend man aſked hym bardus told hym • ſerpent eke beſ • al though made none biheſte trauaylle wel quyt mannes wyt made couenaunt mouthe ſwore therto al couthe parte gyue halue good hath forgeten ſtood wold trouthe holde emperour al tolde hath herd vnkyndeneſſe ſeid wold hym ſelf redreſſ • thus courte iugement adryan ſent quarell • dyence declared preſence emperour many moo wherof moche ſpeche tho grete wōdryng among p •• ſ • laſt neuertheleſe party whiche hath pleyned lawe hath demed ordeyned hem auyſed webe ſhall haue haluendel • thorugh oute adryans good thus vnkynde blode stondeth memorye vnto day thorugh yt euery wyſe mā may enſamplyn hym took mynde ſhame vnkynde ageyne whiche reſon debateth euery creature hateth thy ſone thy offyce rede thou flee ylke vyce right • cronycle ſ • •• adryan feyth forgate worldes cou • fyſ • ful oft ſuche maner wyſ • louers man may ſee ful many vnkynd •• wel promyſe euyl laſ • lyf laſt whan haue hir •• ylle done hir loue gone ſoone ſaiſt thou ſoone • fader wol ſaye allas euer ſuche man borne • hen hath trouthe ſworn • hath loue wold ony tyme ſhold euer berde fynd • fals vnkynde fader touchend may ſtonde degre took neuer loue • e may goo therby doo profi • e el ony ſpede fynd may wel thynk al • dare ſpeke ou •• yf durſt ſo befell • • nto athenis • ere ſent ſo bare hym lygnage suche pryde tooke courage 〈◊〉 forgeten hath ſcoles ryote among fooles dyd many thynges wrong vſed lyf ſo long til laſt wrought fond meſchyef yt whiche ſouȝt thorugh felle yt ſlayn fader whiche herd ſayn wrothe euer myght men armes hym dyght ſtrong power forth went vnto athenis brent pleyne countre al cytees ſtode hym doute defence hadde ageyne power ladde egeus kyng coūceylle took vppon thynge cyte soo pee trete bitwene mynos egeus fele ben acorded thus kyng mynos fro yere yere receyue ſhal thou ſhalt oute athenys truage men myghty age perſones nyne whiche ſhall wyll doo ſpecial vengeaunce ſonnes deth none grace ne geth take iuyſe done ſuche wyſe whiche ſtood wonder ca tyme ſo wherof men yet rede ſynge kyng mynos kepyng cruel monſtre ſeith geſte half man half beeſte mynotaurus hote whiche bigoten ryote vppon phaſyfe owne wyf while oute vpon ſtrif greete ſyege troye ſhe loſt hath al ioye ſhe ſawe mouſtre bore bad men ordeyne another fore felle ſame tyme thus clerk one dedalus ben hir aſſent hir world hath myſwent made owne wyt wherof remembraunce yet mynotaure ſuche hows ſo ſtrong merueylous man within went ſoo many dyuerſe went ne ſhall come oute go amaſyd al aboute hows loke warde mynotaurus put warde lyf therm cam man beeſt ouercam ſlewe fedde hym therupon wiſe many one athenys truage deuoured rage euery yere ſhopen hem ſo athenys go toward thylke woful channce ſet ordynaunce vpon fortune lot caſte til theſeus laſt whiche ye kynges ſonne amonges felle lot vppon chaunce felle knyght worthy al whan ſawe chaunce falle ferd though took hede al euer myght ſpede hym felauſhip forth grece goth ſhip kyng mynos ſought profereth al hym ought vpon poynt hir acorde ſterne kyng cruel lorde toke euery day one nyne put hym diſciplyne mynotaure deuoured theſeus ſo fauoured kepte till laſt mene whyle caſt mene thyng hym beſt felle adryane tho whiche douȝter mynos herd worthy los theſeus myght ſawe luſty knyght hole herte hym ſhe layd alſo loue hir prayd ferforth alone ordeyned anone maner ſhold hym ſaue ſhope ſo ſhe dyd hym haue clewe threde wiche withynne fyrſt atthe dore ſhal begynne wold ageyn ward wende hym take one ende •••• go ſame wey ouer ſo ſey ſpeche ſhe tooke hym pelot whiche ſhold throte mynotaure caſt ryght suche wepen alſo hym ſhe dyght reſon may fayle make ende batayle ſhe hym taught dyuerſe wyſe tyl cōnyng enpryſe beſt ſhold kylle thus ſhortely telle mayden hym taught theſeus monſtre faught ſmote hede ye nam thred ſo cam gothe ageyne til oute grete wonder al aboute mynos tribute hath rebeced ſo werre al ſeced bitwene athenis hem crete ſpeke ſwete who beaute withoute wane fayre mayden adryane ſhe ſaw theſeus ſounde neuer yet vppon grounde gladder wyght ſhe tho theſeus dwellyd day two mayden ſpak rowned ſhe hym abandouned euer ſhe couthe hyr luſty youthe al pryuely bytwene hem twey firſt floure took awey ſo fayre hyr behyght euer whyle lyue myght ſhold hyr take wyf owne hertes lyf ſhold hyr loue trouthe hyr bere ſhe myght forbere ſore loueth hym ageyne euer wold ſeyne al hir hert ſhe leuyth thus purpoos acheuyth aſſured trouthe hym ſhe went routhe fedra hir yong ſuſter eke luſty mayden ſobre meke fulfilled al curtoſye ſuſterhode companye loue whiche hem bytwene ſee hir ſuſter made quene hir fader lefte forth ſhe went hym al firſt entent forgate within litel throwe al ouerthrowe ſhe wend ſhold ſtonde ſhip blowen fro londe wherin lay ſailend adryan mochel fere wyndo ſo lowde blewe ſhe ſee ne knewe praid reſte whyle ſo felle vpoon yle nyght ben dreue hyr leue hath yeue ſhe ſhall londe take hir reſt nothyng hir beſt ſhe londe brought whiche yt tyme thought nouȝt al trouthe took kepe hath layd hir doune ſlepe ſhe long hath ben forwatched certes ſhe euyl matched fer loues kynde beſt vnkynde theſeus whiche trouthe kept yonge lady ſlept fulfylled vnkyndeſhip hath forgeten al godeſhyp whiche adryan hym done bad ſhypmen ſoone hale vp ſaile abyde forth gothe ſame tyde toward athenys londe left lady ſtronde slepend til ſhe awoke whan ſhe caſt vp hyf loke toward ſtronde saw wyȝt hyr herte ſore aflyght ſhe ne wyſt thynke drowe hyr water bryncke ſo ſhe biheld ſee large ſawe ſhip ſhe ſawe barge ferforth ſhe myght kenne lord ſhe ſaid ſuche ſynne al world ſhal vppon woful woman worthy knyȝt hath done wroȝt wend loue bought ſo deſerued nede ſtode vppon drede alſo loue behyght grete wondre myght towardes vnkynde ſoo lete mynde thyng ſaid owne mouthe whan couthe drawen worldes fame ſhalle hynderyng name wel wote ſoo wote gaf trouth bodyly honoure ſhold kepe word ſhe gan wepe ſorowed ynough hyr fair treſſes ſhe drough hyr ſelf ſhe took ſuche ſtrif ſhe bitwene deth lyf swounend lay ful oft among hym long whiche loue vnkynd ſo wherof wrong ſhall euermo stonde cronycle remembraunce alſo aſketh vengeaunce vnkynde loues ca theſeus al though noble knyght lawe loues ryght forfeyted hath alwey adryane putt awey whiche grece vnkynde dede ſo rede fedra ſuſter took ſtede hyr fel afterward mekel tene vyce whiche mene vnkyndeſhip whore falleth trouthe mannes herte palleth good dede acquyte may ſtonde meryte towardes god alſo men calle hym worldes ſoo fende vnto another mannes frende al toward hym ſelf alone thy ſone thy perſone vyce aboue flee fader ye teche thynk doo matere ouer wold fayn wherof ſhal ſhryue good ſonne thy lore reule couetyſe ſhalle propyrte deuyſe euery vyce herken wel ware thervp viribus ex clara re tollit luce rapina floris et iuncta virgine mella ca pit hic tractat ſuper illa ſpecie auaricie que rapina nuncupatur cuius mater extorcio ipſam ad deſeruiendum magnatum curijs ſpecialius commendauit 〈◊〉 lygnage audry •• ſone yet vyce ryght name rauyne whiche hath route couyne rauyne among mayſtres dwelleth ſeruaūtes men telleth extorcion witholde rauyne mennes folde maketh lord payeth nought euer may ſought hows ther ſhall thyng lack ful ofte abyeth pack poure men dwellen aboute thus ſtōdeth comyn peple doute whiche doo none amendement whan hym fayleth payment rauyne maketh none ſkyle taketh ſtrengthe ben ſame wyſe louers ſhal deuyſe whan el may auayle anone ſtrengthe aſſayle gete loue ſeſyne ſee tyme rauyne loue certes fader lady loue ſoo though pompey al world wold obey el ſuche aliſandre wold ſuche ſclaundre good man ſoo doth good feyth ſone thou ſeyſt ſooth wol purueannce ſuche weye luſt auaunce ſhal ſore abye yf theſe old example lye good fader telle one conne many one touchend loue matere lyſten ſone thou ſhalt hath befallen loues cauſe man take rauyne pray whiche femenyne hic ponit exemplum contra traciam ſorore viſitacionis cauſa ſecum quadam vice perduceret concupiſcenciā philoment tanta ſeueritate itinere dilapſus eſt quod non ſolum ipſe violencia ſue rapine virginitatē oppreſſit ſed et gouernaunce ſo thynketh therupon name kyng pandyon two doughters wyf whiche loued lyf firſt doughter proygne hyght ſecond ſhe wel myght called faire philomene felle moche tene fader purueaunce doughter proygne wold auance gaf hir vnto maryage worthy kyng lygnage noble knyght alſo honde kyd euery lond trace hyght thereus clerk ouyde telleth thus thereus wyfe home ladde luſty lyf hir hadde till felle vppon tyde proygne ſhe lay hym beſyde bethought hyr myght ſhe hir ſuſter myght ſee hyr lord hir wylle ſhe ſaid goodly wordes hym praid ſhe hyr myghe goo yf lyked hym ſo wold hym ſelf wende el ſomme ſende whiche myght hir • ſufter grete ſhape myght mete hir lord anone herd gaue acord thus anſwerd wille ſaid youre ſake wey youre ſuſter take ſelf bryng hir yf may ſhe ſhe lay • igan hym hir armes clyppe kyſſed hym hyr ſofte lyppe ſaid ſyre graunt mercy ſone redy tooke leue go ſory tyme dyd ſoo thereus goth forth ſhippe hym felauſhippe ſee right cours nam countrey til cam philomene dwellyng hyr ſuſter tydyng told glade mochel ioye hym made fader moder bothe leue hir doughter lothe yf preſence neuertheles reuerence hym wolde hym ſelf trauaile wold ſhold faile praid gyue hir leue ſhe wold behynde leue al haſt made hir • toward hir ſuſter fare thereus forth ſhe went hole entent ſhe fro hir frendes gone ſottith hym hyr loue anone eyen myght witho •• ne muſt hyr behold ſight gan delyueraunce euer among lady wept thought ſhe neuer kept worldes woman ſhe wyſſhed euermore • vnto ſufter dere hir •• ſpeketh manere ſaid ſuſter ye knewe myn eſtate ye wold rewe trowe delyueraunce ye ſhold knowe ſhope therfore thereus thyng wyſt yet ryght hir ſeluen lyſt hir ſuſter delyuerd ſoone oute pryſon mone proigne ſhe brouȝt nyght •• ſyght chambre alone made many pit • u mone proigne moſt ſorowe made whiche ſawe hir ſuſter pale fade ſpecheles diſhonoured ſhe ben de •• oured alſo vpon hir lord ſhe thought ſo vntruely wrought ſpouſede broken made vowe ſhold wroken word ſhe kneled doune wepyng grete deuocion vnto cupide venus praid ſaid thus ye whome thynge aſterde loue may euery herte ye knowe ye ben aboue god goddeſſe loue ye wyte wel euer yet wylle al wyt sith firſt ye ſhope wedde lay lord bedde haue ben trewe degre euer thought neuer loue place al kyng trace whiche lord wyf allas woful ſtrif hym thus ageynward fynde moſt vntre moſt vnkynde euer lady armes lay well wote ne may amend it▪ wrong ſo grete ful lytel lete myne owne ſuſter tooke wyf forſoke loo thus venus cupyde praid ferthermore ſhe cryde vnto •• ollo hyheſt ſaid myghty god reſt thou doo vengeaunce debate ſuſter al hir eſtate thou knoweſt▪ ſhe hath forlore hyr mandenhede therfore al world ſhall blame ſuſter hath ſhame thereus hir ſent wel thou knoweſt myn entēt al worſhyp good lord geueſt lyues fode euery wyght pray woful ſuſters ben late v lothe ben thyn owne woman lothe thus playneth proigne aſketh wreche though hir ſuſter tack ſpeche hym al thyng wote hir ſorowe leſſe hote herd hem two hym ought haue ſorowed euermo ſorowe hem bitwene ſignes pleyneth philomene proigne ſeith ſhe ſhall wreke world therof ſhall ſpeke proigne ſykenes feyned wherof vnto hir lord ſhe pleyned praid ſhe myght hir chambre kepe hir lyſteth wake ſlepe hir graunted ſo thus gedre two wold hym lytell good herken herafter ſtood woful auentures felle theſe ſuſters ben bothe felle hem alonge grete wronge whiche thereus hem done purpoſe venge hem ſoone thereus proigne wyf ſone lyf beloued hyght moder wyſt wel ſhe myght • reus greue ſlee child ſo leue thus ſhe yt ſaid madde wo whiche hath ouerladde withoute inſight moderhede forgate pyte loſt drede hir chambre pryuely child withoute noyſe cry ſlewe hewe hym al peces dyuerſe ſpyeces fleſſhe hewe taketh made therof ſewe fader mete ſerued gan hym ete ne wiſt ſtood thus owne fleſſhe blood hym ſelf deuoured ageyne kynde hym fore vnkynde vp ryſe herte ſhold agryſe ſhewe hym child dede philomene took vp hede bitwene two diſſhes al wrothe cam forth ſuſters bothe ſetten borde proigne began word ſaid werſt wykke conſeyence whome prykke may ſtere loo thou haſt doo lo ben ſuſters two rauener loo thy praye whome ſo falſely way thou haſt thy tirannye wrought lo ſomdele bought better ſhall thy dede world ſhall euer ſynge rede remembraunce thy defame thou loue haſt done ſuche ſhame ſhall neuer forgete ſterte vp fro mete ſhoue boord flore caught ſwerd anone ſwore ſhold hondes deye vnto goddes crye bigan ſo lowde ſteuene herd vp heuene twynkelyng eye goddes meſchyef ſeye formes chaunged al thre eche hem degre torned birdes kynde delyuerly men may fynde ſeate ynne formes ſet twynne telleth tale firſt nyghtingale ſhapen philomene whiche wynter ſene leues falle naked • en buſſhes alle ſhe byrde hir wylle euer hyd dwelle pryue place •• noman ſhold ſee hir face ſhame myght laſſid thyng paſſid whan ſhe loſt hir maydenhede euer vpon hir womanhede though god wold hir chāge thynketh ſtraunge holdeth hir cloos wynter day whan wynter goth awey nature goddeſſe wylle hir owne fre largeſſe herbis floures bothe tſe feldis medowes clothe alſo woodes greues ben hylled grene leues byrd hir hyde may bitwene mar apryl may • e wynter held cloos pure ſhame aroos whan ſhe ſawe bowes thyck bare ſtyck 〈◊〉 hyd leuys grene wode cometh philomene maketh hir playnte nyght day say • ng euery man may ne yet mayde ſoo old wyſe ſaid whiche vnderſtoode ſhe ment hir note ben ſuche entent eke ſaid ſonge maketh grete ioye myrthe amōg ſaid bird face may hyd though haue loſt maydenhede shal man ſee chekes rede thus medleth ſhe ioye wo hir ſorowe myrthe alſo soo loues maladye maketh dynerſe melo • ye ſaid loue woful blyſſe wyſdom man wyſſe luſty feuer wounde ſoft note ſhe reherceth ofte hem vnderſtond tale haue nyghtyngale whiche erſt cleped philomene told al euer ſhe wold mene bothe hir forme hir note wherof men may ſtory note hir ſuſter proigne fynde ſhe torned oute kynde ſwalowe ſwyft wynge alſo wynter lyeth ſowyng ſhe may thyng ſene world woxen grene comen ſomer tyde flyeth ſhe forth begyn chyde chatereth oute hir langage falſhede maryage telleth maner ſpeche termes ſpouſe breche wol woodes dwelle ſhe wold openly telle alſo ſhe ſpouſe amōg folkes ſhe cometh howſe doo theſe wyues vnderſtonde falſhede hir huſbonde ware hem alſo many vntrewe tho thus ben theſe ſuſters byrdes asthe ben ward men ſo lothe ne wylle pure ſhame man honde tame euer dwelleth hir mynde fond man vnkynde fals thereus ſuche one among v note condycyon men ſaye euery regyon within wne eke withoute regneth comonly aboute namely remembraunce wyll declare vengeaunce goddes hym ordeyned ſuſters pleyned anoue chaunged owne kynde ſtraunged lapwenche made thus hoppeth gras hede ſtondeth vp ryght creſt token knyght yet vnto day men ſeith lapwenche hath loſt feyth byrd ful • eſt alle confeſſor ware ſone ye ſo falle yf thou 〈◊〉 ſuche couyne gete loue rauyne thy luſt may falle thus befelle thereus amans fader god forbede leuer fortrede wyld horſes drawe er ageyne loue lawe dyd ony thyng lowde ſtylle whiche ladyes wylle men ſeyen euery loue hath drede foloweth hir drede hir loue ſo dredeth pleſe loue ſerue hym nedeth thus maye ye knowe ſkylle rauyn doo wyll ageyne hir wylle ſuche weye whyle lyue wylle obeye abydynge hir curtoſye ony mercy wold hyr ply • thy fader wote haue doo amys ferthermore ſhalle byſeche thou ſom poynt ye teche aſketh forth yf ought may better taught • iu • vt ex ſpolijs grandi quam ſepe tumultum quo graditur p • pul • latro perurget iter sic amor ex 〈◊〉 ſu poterit quo carpere predam si locus eſt aptus cetera multa timet hic loquitur ſuper cupiditatis ſpecie quam furtum vocant cuius miniſtri alicuius legis offenſam non metutes tam amoris cauſa quā ali • r ſaam quam ſepe conſcienciam offendunt whan couetyſe poure eſtate stondeth hym ſelf vpon debate thurgh lack myſgouernaunce vnto ſuſtenaūce ne none wey fynde gete hym good blynde whiche ſeeth ſhalle falle ylke vyce yt mē calle robbery taketh honde thorugh water londe thyng men forſwynke geteth hym clothe mete drynke hym retcheth begyn though theft ſoo may wyn thy make purchaas lyeth waytyng paas thyng yt ſeeth ther paſſe taketh paas laſſe ought worth take pakkes wel renſake pryncly bereth none gold ne fyndeth oute • ewel taketh propyrte wodes feldes eke thus robbery goth ſeke may purpoos fynde right ſo ſame kynde good ſone thou myght ſpeke loue matere make veray reſemblaunce right thefe maketh cheueſāce robbeth mennes goodes aboute woode feld goth oute ben theſe louers ſome wylde ſtedes come fynd woman able therto ſpace couenable withoute let fare take parte home comyng whan cometh home eue anone maketh wyf leue ſhe el ſhold knowe telleth hir hūte gan blowe houndes haue wel ronne ſhone mery ſonne hawkes flowen wele • e wold telle hir neuer dele • e loue thryes example ſuche robberyes fynde wryten thou ſhalt acordynge vnto matere hic loquitur contra iſtos amō • cauſa predones qui cum ſuam furtiue concupiſcenciam aſpirant fortuna contra • ū operatur maid wherfor kepe hir ſelf pee ſuche amadryades clexed maydens tho nymp • e eke alſo▪ vpon ſpryng freſſhe welles ſhope dwelle nowhere ell •• thus cam caliſtona wode tegea ſhe vyrgynyte behyght vnto dyane therto plygh • hir trouthe vpon bowes g •• ne kepe hir maydenhede clene whiche afterward vpon day pryuely ſtolen away iubiter thorugh queyntyſe hir toke ſuche wyſe ſodenly forth alle hyr wombe aroos ſhe ſwalle myght hydde therupon betydde dyane whiche herd telle pryue place vnto welle nymphes al companye comen aragerye ſaid ſhe bathe wold bad euery mayden ſhold hyr al naked bathe alſo began preuy woo c • liſtona wex rede ſhame knewe game whome ſuche thyng befalle none made hem naked alle thyng wold hyde ſhe withdrewe hir euer aſyde netheles flode dyana hir ſelue ſtood thought come vnperceyued therof ſhe deceyued ſhe cam lytell nyghe dyana wombe ſeygh ſaid awey thou fowle beeſt thyn eſtate honeſte chaſt water touche thon haſt ſuche touche whiche neuer may hole ageyne thus goth ſhe forleyn ſhame nymphes fledde til nature hir ſpedde ſonne hyght archas named ſhe delyuerd iuno wyf iubiter wrothe haſtyf purpoos doo vengeaunce came forth vpon chaunce caliſtona ſhe ſpakke ſet vpon hyr many lacke ſaid thou arte take thou thy werk may forſake thou vngoodly ypocryte thou arte gretely wyte thou ſhalt fnl ſore abye ylke ſtelthe mycherye thou haſt bothe take doo wherof thy fader lychao shall glad wote doughter ſoo hote ſhe hath broken hir chaſt vowe ſhall chaſtyſe thy grete beaute ſhal torned thorugh whiche yt thou haſt myſtorned thy large fronte thy eyen gray ſhall hem chaunge way feture thy face ſuche wyſe ſhall deface euery man ſhal forbere forth lykenes fer • took forſhapen anon within tyme therupon byfelle bowe honde hunte gamen fonde woode gothe playe hir ſone archas waye happed came ſhe good hede name ſtood vnder bowe knewe hym well hym drowe though ſhe hir forme lore loue loſt therfore whiche kynde hath ſet vnder lawe ſhe vnder woode ſhawe hyr child belhed ſhe ſo glade ſhe hir armes ſprade though ſhe womanhede toward hym come took hede bare bowe bente arowe ſente gan tyſe bowe none knowe beeſt wylde inpiter wold ſhylde moder ſone alſo ordeyned hem bothe ſo euer ſaue thus ſone thou myght haue enſample flee robbe vyrgynyte yong innocent awey euer ouy wey old bookes rede sache robberye drede namely goode whiche euer woman goode deſyreth kepe hold ſomtymes dayes old yf thou tale wel thou may ſomde • old enſample take heede floure maydenhed • tyme holden pry ſo ſo ſo ſhall euer ſtonde thou ſhalt vnderſtonde herkene tale next ſewend maydenhede commend hic loquitur de virginitat •• comm • dacione vbi dicit quod nuper imperatores obſtanti ſtatus dignitatem virginibus ſedebant via rome amōg geſtes old fynde valery told man ſo euer emperour rome ſhold honoure vyrgyn weye hir mete ſhold obeye worſhyp vyrgynyte grete dignyte woman tho chaſte men alſo commended ouerall ſpeke therof ſpecial hic loquitur qualiter phirinus iu uenū rome pulcherrimus vt ill • ſā ſuā virginitatem conſeruaret ambo oculos • ruens vulti ſui decorem abhominabilem conſtituit touchend men enſāple fynd phirinus yt mās kynd aboue al fayreſt rome alſo comlyeſt well hyr myght behold haue hym ſyght thus tempted ofte ſore wold among woman ſo coueyted beaute face ſtreyted hath threſt oute bothe eyen wymmen hym ſeyn afterward hym ne rought thus maydenhede bonght may proue wil thy aboue al vnder ſky maydenhede preyſe vertues wold peyſe apocalipſis recordeth caſt heuen beſt acordeth hij ſequntur agnum quocumqȝ • erit may ſhewe wel therfore haue told bere fore heuen erthe alſo except bothe two oute fleſſhe man leuen gregory hath enſample geuen carne preter carnem viuere pocius vita angelica eſt quam humana ierom ſeyth ſhall rather told lyker angel many fold lyf man kynde reſon fynde thorugh grace aboue fleſſhe withoute fleſſhely loue man lyue chaſt neuertheles man may ſuche haue ben yet ben vertu ſelden wonne mater haue begonne thynke telle therof whiche ſone thy lor • lyſt take hede trete vpon maydenhede vt roſa de ſpinis ſpineto preualet orta vt filij flores ceſpite plura valēt • c ſibi virgiuitas carnis ſpōſalia vin cit eternos fetus que ſine lahe parit bookes ſeyn māns lyf vpon knyghthode werre ſtrif ſet among enemyes right ſo freel fleſſh who nature ay redy ſpurne falle fyrſt foman alle werre redy ay werreth nyght werreth day man hath neuer reſt therfore knyght beſt thorugh myght grace god ſonde whiche bataill may withſtōde wherof dwelleth memorye hem ſomtyme vyctorye dedely werre hadden hyhe proweſſe ye hadd • thorugh ye ſowle ſtood amended vpon erthe yet commended hic loquitur qualiter valentinianus imperator ipſe octogenarius plures prou • ncias romano imperio belliger ſub iugauit dixit ſe ſuper ōnia magi gaudere de eo quod contra ſue carnis concupiſcenciam victoriam op •• nuiſſet nam et ipſe virgo omnibus diebus vite ſue caſtiſſimus permanſit emperour old dayes al aſſayes worthy knyȝt honde ſuche myght amounte ageyn one poynte hath nomen fleſſhe hath ouercomen virgyn ſayde batayle pry laid lo ſone auyſe fader may wel al ſoo world men ſone ag • lawe men may fynde god man lawe kynde hath ſet world multyplye wylle hym iuſtyfye doo lawe neuertheles youre good ſawe good kepe ſo may wol ageyne ſeye nay ſone take ſay maydenhede taken away withoute lawes ordynaunce may fayle vengeauuce yf thou wylt ſooth wyten behold tale whiche wryten kyng agamenon cyte l • ſbon wonuen mayden fond faireſt londe tyme men wyſt hir hym lyſt wherof ſhe daungerous ye thyng yt whiche moſt precious fayre mayden cleped creſeyde doughter cryſys whiche tyme ſpeciall tyme biſſhop pryncipal phebus ſacryfyce wel vyce agamenon way troyward tooke way mayden hym ladde grete luſt hir hadde phebus yt whiche grete diſdeyne yt maiden forleyn anone troye came mengeaunce vpon dede name aud ſent comune peſtylence ſought hir euydence made calculacion knowe condicyon deth cam ſodenly laſt redyly cauſe alſo man fonde forth ſame ſtounde agamenon oppoſed whiche hath knowleched ye ca foly hath wrought therupon mercy ſought toward god dyuerſe wyſe prayer ſacryfyce mayden home ſende gafe hir gold ynough ſpende euer whyles ſhe wold lyue thus ſyn forgyue peſtylence ſeced loo encrecid loue whiche ylle wonne letter vnbegonne take thyng withoute leue whiche thou muſt nedes leue yet haue maugre forth thy robben ouerall loues cauſe yf thou begynne eaſe thou ſhalt wynne fader ſo wyl wy ſone wel ware youre examplarye loue cauſe robberye haue right wel vnderſtonde ouer ſo ſtonde yet wol wyte youre apryſe thynge couetyſe • idiando latens tempus rimatur et horam fur quibus occulto tempore furta parat sic amor inſidijs vacat et ſub tegmine laudes prēdere furtiuos nocte fauente queat hic tractat ſuper illa cupiditatis ſpecie que ſecrum latrocinium dicitur cuius natura cuſtodire rerum neſciente ea que cupit tam per diem quam per n • c tem abſqȝ ſtrepitu clauculo fnratur wyth couetyſe yf fynde ſeruaunt ſame kynd ſteleth hote myche • ye hym euer companye whome yf ſhall telle ſooth ſtalketh pecok doth taketh pray ſoo couerte man wote aperte wote lord home wold ſtalke aboute come thyng fynt way ſawe men away ſteleth goth forth al therof man knowe ſhal eke • uf oft goth nyght withouten mone ſterre lyght craft dore vnpykyth taketh therin hym lyketh yf dore ſo ſhet entre lette wylle wyndowe crept whyle lord faſt ſlepe ſteleth thyng hym beſt lyſt goth wey wyſt ful ofte alſo lyght day yet wold ſtele make aſſay vnder cete hond put knyf purs cut receyueth fynde therin thus auntreth hym wyn bereth horne bloweth man counceyll knoweth may gete mychyng al bylle vnder wyng hound goth fold hath taken wold mouth vppon gras wypeth ſo feyned chere hym ſlyketh euer ſhepe ſtrangle man therof ſhall iangle knowe dede ryght ſo doth ſtelthe euery ſtede hym lyſt pray take ſo wel cauſe make ſo wel feyne ſo wel gloſe ne ſhalle man ſuppoſe innocent thus mannes eye blent craft may vſe withoute helpe ony refuſe ben louers degre hir luſt pryuete ſey geten al ſtelthe ther atteynen grete welthe tyme laſteth loue awayteth euer caſteth may ſtele catche pray therto may fynde way nyght day taketh parte may yf may doo yet wol ſtele kyſſe two telle yf thou euer dydeſt ſo ony wyſe thy lady vnto fader ſone thus thou haue ſtolen ony kus thyng therto longeth man ſuche theues hongeth telle thy ſey trouthe fader nay routhe wylle thefe ſhe mooſt lef • yet durſt neuer pryuete mot one take byr kne ſtele hir yf durſt wote wel netheles yf lye ſtelthe ne robberye loue whiche felle thought hir dyd neuer nought mē ſeyn herte fayled ſhalle caſtel aſſayled though hertes ten ſtrong men myn owne man dare vſen may ſelf recouere though man neuer ſo pouere bere herte aud soo faileth wyt ſhold myn acorde ſeruaunt lede ayenſt lord yf foote wold owhere go hondes wold el • herte ageyne remenaunt veyne thus lacketh al weele yet ne dare ſteele thyng whiche longeth vnto loue eke ſo hie aboue may wel therto areche ſo tyme ſpeche ful ſeld yf ſtele may word two go way betwyxt hir eſtate comparyſon may none fele wel wote al heuy hote ſet hond withoute loue thus mote algate leue ſtele may take wyſe mote forſake • en thefe ageyne wylle thyng whiche may fulfylle ſerpent whiche neuer ſlepte flees gold ſo wel ne kepte colchos tale told lady thouſand folde bet • er yemed bewaked ſhe clothed naked kepe hir body nyght day hath wardey • • dy ay whiche ſo wonderful wyght hym man myght ſwerde ne wepen may daunte ne ſleyghte charme enchāt • wherof myght made tame daunger right name whiche vnder lock vnder key man may hyr ſtele awey al treſoure vnderfonge vnto loue may longe leſt lokyng hir eye mote ſtole yf ſeye ſo grutcheth ſo lyte wold ſone ſet wyte hym wold ſtelle greueth wonder ſore prouerbe euer newe ſtraunge lokes maken • trewe • wolden ſtele pyke ſo wel man ſyke hym nether mene whome daunger wold • eue lene treſoure hath kepe though wold ſtalke crepe wayte eue eke morowe daunger ſhall thyng borowe ſtele wote wel may nouȝt thus right wel bethought daunger ſtondeth offyce ſtelthe whiche clepeth vyce ſhall gylty neuermo therfore wold ago fet neuer hym hert • ſo afterward ferd myght afterward perca • loue make ſomme purchaas ſtelth ſomme way ſtont fro fer away fader ye told aboue ſteleth goth nyght loue maye wele poynte forſake oftymes ne wake nyghtes ſlepe pray take kepe loked ſuche wyſe nyght may aryſe ſomme wyndowe loken oute ſee howſyng al aboute may chambre knowe whiche lady trowe lyeth hir bedde ſlepeth ſofte hert thefe ful ofte ſtonde behold long nyghtes ben cold thynk hyr lyeth wyſſhe wy nectanabus • l protheus couthen nygromance lykenes ſemblaūce ryght hem lyſt hem ſelf tranſforme yf ſuche forme ſaye wold flee hir chambre ſee ony grace wold falle myght vnder palle somme thyng loue pyke ſtele thus thynke thoughtes fele though therof thyng ſooth yet caſe tyme doth laſt whan fynde falle mynde ſce haue ſtond long haue profyte vnderfonge ſtalk bed within thynke begyn loue whan ſhall nyght wylle good myght lacketh bothe grace ſoo thought enbrace yet haue better ferde fader • oo haue ye herde ſtelthe • oue haue doo wylle hath therto worthy penaunce put vnto youre ordynaunce ſone ſtelthe byhete though tyme ſwete ende doth lytell good enſample ſtood whilome maye telle pray yow fader telle ſone hym whiche gothe day wey ſtelthe aſſay loues cauſe taketh pray ouyde ſaid ſhal ſay methamor tolde tale whiche good holde hic amoris cauſa ſuper iſto latelcinio quod dietim contingit ponit exem p •• et narrat quod cum linchotor orchanni filia camer • ſub archa mat •• cuſtodia virgo conſeruabatur phebus eiue pulchritudinem concupiſ hen conclaue domus clara luce ſub • ntrans virginis pudiciciam matre abſente deflorauit vnde ipſa inpregnata • ratus pater filiam ſuam ad ſepeliendū •• ua effodit ex cuius tumulo florem ſol ſequium vocant dicunt conſequenter primitus accreuiſſe poete vpon matere ſi • lth wrote manere venus hath ye law hāde thyng whiche may withſtād • ſhe treſour toward loue hath within hyr ward phebus loue hath ſo conſtreyned withoute reſte payned herte coueite mayde whiche warded ſtreyte within chambre kepte ſo cloos ſelden whan ſhe diſcloos goth hir moder play lenchoter ſo men ſay mayden hyght orc • anus hir fader befelle thus doughter kept ſo dere ben bifore yere yere vnder hir moder diſcyplyne clene malden vyrgyne vpon whoos natyuyte comelyhede beaute nature hath ſet al ſhe may lyche vnto freſſhe may eyther monethes yere sourmounteth ſo withoute pere mayden feiture wherof phebus oute meſure hyr loueth euery ſyde waiteth yf ſo may betyde thorugh ony ſleygthe myght hir luſty maydenhede vnright whiche al worldes welth thus lurkyng vpon ſtelthe awayte ſo longe lay till befelle vppon day thorugh hir chambre wall came al ſodenly ſtalle thyng hym ſo lyefe woo whyle yt thefe venus whiche enemy thylk loues mycherye diſcouerith playne caa • befelle toward phebus concubyne ſhe lete couyne thylk loue dedely • brothe pleyne vpō mayde goth told hir fader ſtood wherof ſorowe well nyhe woode vnto hir moder thus ſaid loo kepe mayd phebus dare thyng ſpeke vpon ſhall wreke soo theſe maydens mowe take enſample ſuffre maydenhede ſtole ſhe deth may thole bad go make pytte wherin hath doughter ſette wold pyte haue ſhe al quyck graue deed anone preſence phebus reuerence ſhe ben loue hath wrouȝt thoruȝ power aboue ſhe ſprong vp oute molde floure named gold whiche ſtonte gouerneth ſonne thus loue euyll wonne ful ofte cometh repentayle fader meruayle counceyll wreyed oftyme loue hath pleyed ſtole many pryue game whiche neuer yet cam blame thynketh hydde youre tale betydde venus diſturbed caas eke alſo brode daye phebus ſuche fylthe wrought wherof maide blame brought afterward ſhe ſo fore ye ſeyden fore ſtelth loue goth nyght doth thynges oute ſyght therof luſt alſo tale lyche matere wherof myght enſample take good ſone thy ſake befelle dayes olde ſo poete told vpon nyghtes mycherye herken tale poeſye hic ponit • yemplum ſuper eodem quod de notte contingit▪ et narrat qualiter hercules cum eola quadam ſpelunca nobili thophis dictum ſub mō te thimolo ibi ſilua bachi ē hoſpicio pernoctarunt et cum ipſi varijs lectis ſeperatim iacentes dormi • runt contigit lectum herculis veſtimentis eole lectum qȝ eole pelle leonis contra hercules induebatur operari ſuper quo fobnns ſilua deſcendeus ſpeluncam ſubintrauit temptans ſi forte cum eola ſue concupiſcencie voluptatem neſciente hercules furari poſſet et cum ad lectum herculis muliebri palpata veſte ex caſu perueniſſet putans eolam fuiſſe cubiculum nudo corpore ingreditur quem ſenciens hercules manibus apprehēſum ipſum ad terrā ita fortiter al liſit vt inpotens ſui corporis effectus vſaȝ mane ipſum requieuit vbi saba cum nymphis ſilueſtribus ſuperue niens ipſum ſic illuſum deridebat myghtyeſt men hercules eolen whiche ye loue courage geder vpon pylgremage toward rome ſholden goo felle hem way ſo vpon day caue within roche founden haue whiche ryall gloryous entayle curious name thopis hote ſonne ſhone tho wonder hote ſomer tyde hercules whiche ſyde hath eolen loue thylk caue ſeid thought beſt ſhe three hir reſte thylk day thylke nyght ſhe luſty wyght euery thyng hym obeyd • • lyketh hir al ſeide long day ſo befelle caue vnder hylle thymolus whiche •• growe wet • e thylk throwe fanus saba goddeſſe nimphus hir kyndeneſſe thylke tyme ſtood gouerned place lerned nyghe whiche bachus woode hyȝt fanus took grete inſight c • len nyghe whan th • hir beaute ſyghe • ute wyt aſſoted herte hath ſo noted forſoke nymphes alle ſaid wold ſo falle aſſay another wynne herte thought withynne ſet caſt myght loue pyke aw • nyght day wyſe ſtele myght ſuffyſe therupon tyme wayt • th take gode b • de loue affa • teth hym loue al oueroome faire eolen ſhe come hercules caue •• said ſo • wold haue 〈◊〉 fire bothe ech • hem ſheld clothe doo right ſhe bade hath hir clothes clade caſt hir gypyon whiche ſkyn lyon made vpon wey ſlough euer thus pley took grete mace alſo knytted hir gyrdel ſhe lyche man awyd hercules hath aſſayd clothen hym array thus iape forth day till hir ſouper redy •• hadden ſouped ſhopen hem goo reſt thought hem beſt bad thylke nyght two ſondry beddes ſhold dyght • e geder lygge nold cauſe offre wold vpon morowe hir ſacryfice ſeruaunte dyn offyce ſondey beddes made anon • reſt gone eche hem ſelf ſondry place fair eolen hath ſet mace beſides beddes bede aboue clothes hir loue hylled hir bedde aboute whiche thyng douts hir wympel wonde aboute chek • hir kyrtel hir mantell eke abrode vpon bedde ſpredde thus ſlepen bothe bedde trauayle wyn ſeruaunt lyke dronken ſwyn bygan rowte faſt fanus whiche ſtelthe caſt comen caue fonde al ſaue withoute noyſe went derk nyght ſyght blent yet happed hym god eolen bed tho leyd alone ſlepe wold take kepe whoos bed made aſſay • lyon lay cote found eke feleth mace herte ke • eth durſt abyde ſtalketh vpon euery ſide ſought aboute hond • bed till fond lay wympled vyſage tho glad courage hyr kyrtell fonde alſo eke hir mantell bothe two beſpred • pon • ed • oft made hym naked ſoft bed vnware crepte hercules tyme ſlept wende well ſhe thus ſtede eole anone profereth hym loue whiche felt man aboue hercules hym threwe ground ſore haue hym fond lyggend therupon morowe tho lytel ſorowe fanus hym ſelf made • nt el al glade loghen hym ſcorne aboute saba nymp •• route • doune loke ferd ſooth herde beiaped oueral ſone thou ware al vſe ſuche mycheryes yf thou haue better aſpy •• aunture yf ſo betyde fanus thylke tyde wherof thou myght ſhamed ſo holy fader certes yf right good leue suche mycherye thynke leue myn faynt herte wol ſerue maugre wylle deſerue thylke place loue ye tolden aboue couetyſe pyllage lygnage whiche toucheth ſhuft pray therof ye wold aſſay may vyce eſchewe sone thou haſt herd ſhewe vyces ſtont rowe cou •• yſe thou ſhalt knowe yet one whiche laſt ſacrylege thou faſt god hym ſelf debateth wherof •• e henen hym hatet • sacrilegus tantum furto loca ſacra prophanat vt ſibi ſint agri ſic domus • dei nec locus eſt quo nō temptat amans quod amat si que poſſe nequit carpere • elle capit hic tractat ſuper vltima cupidita • ſpecie que ſacrilegium dicitur cuius fructum ea quam altiſſimo ſanctificantur bona depredans ••• leſie tantum ſpolijs inſidiatu • hyhe god good purueyeth hath man fode clothes mete drynke bade adam ſhold ſwynke geten hym ſuſtenaunce eke ſet ordynaunce vpon lawe moyſes though man haueles ſhall theft ſtele dayes ther fele wol labour vndertake maye ſtelthe take hold ſykerlyche wonne thus lawe ouercome whiche god hath ſet namely hem ſoo vntrewe • goddes robbe holy chirche theft whiche wyrch • name cleped ſacrylege ayene whome thynke allege condicion telle whiche rifeleth book belle forth remenaunt goddes hows appertynaunt ſhold • ydd • bede doth theft holy ſtede taketh fynt therin ſeeth may wyn wendeth curſidneſſe ne briketh holyneſſe doth god reuerence hath loſe conſcyence though preſt therfor corſe ſeyth fareth worſe ſpeke otherwyſe man laſſeth fraunchyſe taketh holy chirche pray note bede ſhall pray frō god hath yeue al propirte ſpeciall whiche vnto criſt hym ſelf due bynemeth may wel eſchewe payne comyng afterward hath made forward ſacryl • ge dwelle whiche hath herytage helle yf rede old lawe fynde wryte thylke dawe prynces thre comparable al degre one hem cleped thus prowde kyng antyochus nabuzardon hyght whiche enforced al myght temple deſtroye waſte ſo • e dyde al haſt thyrde whiche ſhamed nabogo donoſer named ieruſalem put vnder ſacrylege many wonder holy temple wrought wiche balthaſar heyre abought mane techel phares wryt walle thou myȝt wyt • byble hath declared • ſpared yet day men pylle maken argument ſkylle ſacrylege belongeth man therafter longeth taketh hede doth right ſo telle ſooth loues cauſe yf ſhall trete ben ſuche ſmale grete leyſer fynde el wyll leten belle ne though ſee preeſt maſſe wol leten ouerpaſſe fond loue ſtande telle ere aſke god none grace whyle ben hooly place go ſomme ananntage wylle haue ſome pyllage goodly wordes byheſte el take leſt oute hir hond ryng gloue nyhe weder wyl ſhoue ſhe ſaid ſhe ſhall forgete token hir gete thus halowe hye feſte suche thefte may chirche areſte al leful hem lyketh whome el myſlyketh eke right ſelf kynde grete cytees men may fynde luſty folk make hem gay wayte vpon holy day chirches mynſtres eke gone woman ſeke ſuche one gooth ſore fayreſt al route ſytten al rewe wylle body moſt ſhewe croked keyned theron ſet ouche chapelet whiche late come greues el one grene leues ſhold ſeme freſſhe thus loketh fleſſhe ryght hauke whiche hath ſiȝt vpon fowle ſhall lyght fayrye ſhe weth hym fore • ye 〈◊〉 hooly place ſytte al make hir hertes flytte eye nowhere wol abyde loke pry euery ſide hym heſt lyketh otherwhyle among ſyketh thynketh hem ſo ther thynken two thre yet loueth none alle euer chaunce falle netheles ſey ſoothe cauſe ſo doeth ſtele herte two ouce chirche go ſaid aboue ſacrylege loue wel may ſteleth away neuer yelde may telle thy ſone anon haſt thou doo ſacrylege none haue ſaid manere fader matere wylle yow telle redyly haue doo bnt truly maye excuſe myn entent neuer chirche went ſuche maner ye ſhryue man lyue cauſe haue laſt may vnto craft thyng able ſtele though neuer ſo fele bnt yet wylle ſey lady whome lyeth hooly quarelle ſhe chirche chappelle goo matens maſſe tyme wayte wel paſſe chirche come ſtonde though take look hond • contenannce look bnt toward hyr al loke yf ſo falle pray vnto god ſomwhat ſay pater noſter crede al wold ſpede bede holy chirche myght ſomme myracle wirche lady berte chaunge whiche euer hath ſtraunge deuocion al myn contemplacion al herte courage ſet hyr ymage euer wayte vpon tyde ſhe loke ony thyng ſyde maye hir auyſe anone couetyſe ſmyt • leef holy chirche theef ſtele veſtyment thyng talent wold ſtele yf myght glad word goodly ſyght euer ſeruyce profere namely ſhe goth offre lede yf may ſomwhat wold ſtele away beclyppe hir waſt yet laſt ſtele taſt whyle graunt mercy ſeith▪ ſo wynne therby luſty touche good word eke al remenannt ſeke fro purpoos wonder ferre may ſay ſaid erre hooly chirche yf wowe conſcyence yet wold allowe ſoo vpon amendement myght gete aſſignement wherfore ſpede place suche ſacrylege hold grace thus fader ſooth ſey chirche right wey myght ought loue take suche hanſell haue forſake fynally confeſſe holyneſſe whyle hir ſee ony ſtede yet onght euer dede ſacrylege hyr took word looke el yf herd frede toward offryng hir lede take therof take may el • ere nought away though wold ought • l haue thynges ben ſo ſaue kepte ſuche pryuelege may doo ſacrylege god wote wylle netheles though muſt nedes kepe pee gree ſone myn lete paſſe wyl therto laſſe myght otherwyſe awey thy fader yow prey telle thou thynkeſt therupon therof haue gylt none thy wylle ſone blame remenaunt game haue told yet take lere thy wyt thyng hath tyme ſtede whiche ſerueth bede •• e chambre another ſpeche yf thou wyſteſt wreche ſacrylege hath abought • ow ſholdeſt vſe ryght nought thou ſhalt amende tale wol diſpende hic amoris cauſa ſuper iſtius vi 〈◊〉 articulo ponit exemplum et narrat pro • quod paris pr • ami regis filius •••• nam menelai vxorem quadā g •• inſula templo veneris ſacrile •• abduxit illa troye famoſiſſima •• ſidie per vniuerſum orbis climita di nulgata precipue cauſabat ita qd huiuſmodi ſacrilegium non ſolum ad ipſius regis patriam omnium az ſuorū interitum sed ad perpetuam vrbis de ſolacionem vindicem fomitem miniſtrabat al men ſaith know ye world thoruȝ blow troye lamedon hercules iaſen toward colchos oute gr ••• ſee ſeylyng vpon pece londe troye reſte preyde wrongfully conueyde found hym ſo vyleyne cam grece ageyne power gete myght towardes troye haue hem dyght took ſuche vengeaunce wherof ſtant yet remembraunce deſtroyed kyng alle leften brent walle grekes troyes many ſlowe pryſoners took ynowe among whiche one kynges doughter lamedone eſyona fayre thynge whiche vnto lamon kyng hercules aſſent hole parlement wylle yeue graunted thus hath grete troye dannted hym torne ſuche manere ſhalt thou cauſe tale telle vpon chaunces bifelle kyng lamedon whiche dyed thus ſone one priamus whiche thylke tyme home herd come fond cyte falle whiche bygan vpon walle made cyte newe whiche londes knewe tho ſe • den lyme ſtone world ſo fayre none one ſide towne kyng lete make ylyowne hye toure ſtrong place whiche adrad manace quarell none engyne though men wold make myne man craft myght approche ſet vpon roche walles towne aboute hem ſtode al world doute proporcyon syx gate toun ſuche enforme ſuche entayle hem ſee grete meruayl • dyches brode depe fewe men myght kepe al world ſemeth tho yf goddes foo grete prees vnto cyte drowe peple ynowe burgeys therin dwellen may man tong tellen cyte ryche good made wel ſtood kyng pry • mu tho hym bethought grece whylome wrought hir ſwerd deuoured ſuſter diſhououred thelamon awey ladde thynkyng wex vnglad ſet anone parlement whiche lordes aſſent many wyſe ſpoke myghten ben awroke laſt netheles ſeid al acord pee ſetten eyther party reſt thought hem al beſt reſonable amendement thus anthenor forth ſent aſke eſyona ageyne wyte wold ſeyne paſſeth ſee barge grece ſey charge whiche ſaid redyly vnto lordes ſpak grece aboute herd wordes ſtoute namelyche thelamon mayden wold gone ſaid maner thynge bad hym gone home kyng gate none amende ought couthe doo ſende anthenor ayene goth home vnto kyng come told grece herd thelamon anſwerd hir aboue wol neyther pee ne loue euery man ſhall done beſt men ſeyen nyght hath reſt kynge bythought hym ye nyȝt erly day lyght took counceyll matere acord manere withouten ony let certeyne tyme ſhold ſet parlement ben auyſed wyſe anyſed parlement ſet day moneth may priamus ſight wyf hecuba ſhe hyght whome tyme ſhe sone fyue doughters thre beſide two thyrty mo knyghtes al tho vpon wyt bygete el myght hem get whiche knowe suche world ylk throwe ſo child ryche therof man hym lyche parlement day come ben lordes al ſome tho prouounced purpoſed cauſe hem diſcloſed anthenor grece ferde ſytten ay ſtylle herde tho ſpak euery man aboute alledged many doute many prowde word ſpoke alſo mooſt partye tho wyſten beſt werre reſt withoute fere hector among lordes tale told ſuche wyſe ſaid lordes ye ben wyſe ye knowen wel aboue al mooſt worthy stant grete manhode worthynes knyghthode ſo wel agrope hem bylongeth al europe whiche thyrd parte euen alle world vnder heuen folke fewe reſon eſchewe perylle falle therin better leue bygyn thyng whiche may acheued wyſe fynde hym greued doth ſo greue loketh fore wylle ſee behynde may ful ofte harmes fynde wyck ſtrif haue worſe haue encheſon corſe wote wel hate grekes debate hem ben ſuche myght ful good euery wyght hym ſelf ryght wel bythought thus ſey nought whyle lyf may ſtonde ye taken werre honde falle beſt werſt ſhall ſeluen ferſt greue hem euer may ſtylle one ſay nay thyng yt coūceil demeth vnto wel quemeth werre certes pee ſay netheles belongeth ſay ſhape ye beſt way whan hector ſaid deuyſe next hym tho ſpak paryſe whiche broder alyed hym beſt thought thus ſeid strong thyng ſuffer wrong ſuffre ſhame ſtronge haue ſuffred two al yet haue doo ſoo myght reforme wrong ſhame better forme sente anthenor ye wel knowe hir grete wordes blowe vppon hir wrongfull dedes eke wol hym ſelf meke pee lyſt reſon take men ſeyn reſon wyll hym forſake multitude men ſtrengthe ten hath ſene trewe quarele ayene honderd haluendele hath better goddes grace thus hath befalle many place yf lyke vnto yow alle wylle aſſay ſo bifalle oure enemy yf may greue haue caught grete byleue vpon pleyne poynt wol declare yonder day gan fare hunte vnto grete herte whiche fore houndes ſterte euery man went ſyde hym purſewe ryde bigan chaſe ſooth ſay within whyle oute way rode nyſt ſlope caught graſſe beſide welle leyd doune ſlepe vyſyoun god mercurye came goddeſſes thre hym name mynerue venus iuno hond appel tho held gold lettres wryte thus dyd wyte put hem vpon fayreſt hem thre gold appel ſhold gyue eche hem ſhryue echone faire behyght venus ſaid yf ſhe myght appel gyfte gete wold neuermore forgete ſaid grece londe wold brynge honde al erthe fayreſt thought beſt hyr yaf appel tho thus hope well yf goo ſhe wylle ſo ordeyne matere pleyne shal haue come ageyne haue ye herd wold ſeyne saye ye ſtont youre auyſe euery man tho ſaid ſondry cauſes recorde laſt acorde parys ſhall grece wende thus parlement took ende caſſandre ſhe herd whiche parys ſuſter anone ſhe gan wepe wayle ſaid ala may v ayle fortune hir blynd whele ne wylle lete v ſtonde wele dare wel vndertake yf parys wey take ſeid ſhal doo ben euer fordoo mayden caſſandre hyght al world bereth ſyght bookes men fynde wryte sybell whome ye wyte al men yet clepen ſage whan ſhe wyſt vyage parys ſhold grece fare woman myght werſe fare ne ſorowe ſhe dyde ryght ſo ſame ſtede ferd helenus whiche hir broder prophecy ſuche another al holde iape purpoos whiche ſhape hem leef hem lothe holde grece goth parys retenaunce felle vpon chaunce grece londeth yle hym told ſame whyle folk whiche began freyne tho wás yle quene eleyne eke countrees aboute ladyes many lufty rowte mochel worthy peple alſo comen thedertho cauſe ſtood ſuche wyſe worſhip ſacryfyſe venus wold make fore vndertake good wyll ſome biheſte hir hyhe feſte within temple whiche whan parys wyſt anone ſhope ordynaunce gone te done obeyſaunce venus hir hooly day dyd vpon beſt aray grete rycheſſe hym behongeth ſuche lord longeth armed netheles londe pee thus gothe oute ſhip taketh hym felauſhip ſuche maner yow ſay vnto temple hold way tydyng whiche gothe oueral grete ſmal forth come quenes ere told parys come wold doo ſacryfyce vnto venus whan ſhe herd telle thus thought euer ſhe wylle hym abyde ſee couthe manere worldes ſuche pleſaunce took al hir acqueyntaunce ferforth herte lay ſtale went away goth forth took leue thought anon eue wold done ſacrylege many man ſhal abyge ayene ſhip come hym hath counceyll nome deuiſed matere ſuche wyſe thou ſhalt within nyght al pryuely men warneth armed redy ſoone certeyn thyng done anon redy alle eche gan calle wente hem oute vpon ſtronde took purpoos al ſodenly al one ſet ſkrye hem whiche temple fr tho moche peple bnt defence bote ſuffre ſuffre mote parys vnto quene went hir armes hent hym felauſhip forth bere ſhip vp goth ſayle forth went ſuche wynd fortune hem ſent till hauen troy caught oute ſhip anon ſtrauȝt gone hem forth toward toun whiche cam proceſſion ayene parys ſene pray euery man began ſay parys felauſhip al couthen worſhip none ſo lytel man troye ne made myrthe ioye parys wonnen eleyn al nyght ſorowe peyn helenus caſſandre token ſhame ſklaundre loſſe al comon grace parys oute hooly place ſtelthe hath take man wyfe wherof hem delycious hath owne hou • men ſeyn ofte ſo auyſe hem wel ſo ſpeke way ful oftyme haue herd ſay whiche hath loue acheued hym thynkth releued though lady make hym chere ſhe may good manere hir honoure hir name ſaue yf ſurplus myght haue thyng withſtondyng hir eſtate loue delycate ſet hir chere delyte haue appetyte ſone yf ſo telle hooly fader delycate ſuche wyſ • loue ye deuyſe ne neuer yet gyltyf yf ſuche wyfe ye ſpeke ſhold wold neuermore luſt ony womanhede herte vpon none fede yf dyd waſte withoute ſuche repaſte ſuche ye told aboue wyf yet loue faſte may foode gete lack deynte mete whiche herte may fedde go faſtyng bedde myght geten told mochel lady wold fede hir glad ſemblannt • though lacke remenaunt yet ſhold ſomdele abeſſhed tyme wel refreſſhed certes fader ſhe ne doth good feyth tellen ſooth trowe though ſhold ſer • ue wold eye ſwerue herte one goodely looke fede thus ſuche cooke may goo faſtyng euer mo yf ſo ony woo may fede man herte wele therof haue euery mele plente ynough hym ſelf ſo cough ſtomak may defye loo thus delycacye loue whiche herte fedeth thus haue lack nedeth al yet netheles ſey gyltles ſomdele delycate el fully mate yf ſomme luſty ſtound • comforte eſe founde take loue ſomme repaſt though ful taſte luſt loue may ſtele honge • otherwyſe kele ſmale luſtes whiche pyke tyme yet lyke ye wyſten mene good ſone ſhryue clene ſuche dayntees ben good ay tyme dome day looke vpon hir euer one yet whan ſhold fro hir gone myn eye wold though faſte ben honger ſtoruen alſo faſt til efte ayene hir ſye suche nature myn eye luſt ſo deyntefull whiche man ſhold full ſtomak vnderfongeth euer one myn eye longeth loke gouſhauk tyreth ryght ſo doth whan pyreth tutyth hir womanhede may neuer fully fede luſt euer lyche ſore hym hongreth ſo deſyreth fedde algate thus eye made gate thugh ye deyntees thouȝ • luſt ben myn herte brought ryght eye look myn herte luſty cook • loues fede delycate ryght ſo ere eſtate eye may ſerue wel myn eres thonk deſerue feden hym fro day day ſuche fode may thus oueral come ſpecial may lady pryce one ſey ſhe wyſe another ſeith ſhe good ſomme men ſeyn worthy blood ſhe one alſo fayre none ſoo ſome preiſe hir goodly chere thus euery thyng may whiche ſowneth lady good herte luſty foode eke ere hath ouer deynte feſte ſo maye hir ſelum ſpeke anone faſt breke ſuche wordes ſhe ſeyth ful trouthe ful feith ben ſo good debonaire debonair • hir luſt ſpeke faire vertu hir goodly ſpeche verily hertes leche ſo bifalle among ſhe carole vpon ſonge ſo fedde fro lyf ſo ledde though paradys certes myn auys hir vois ſteu • thynketh blyſſe heu • eke vois alſo ful oftyme falleth ſo myn ere good petaunce fed redyng romaunce ydome amadas whilome ca eke many ſtore loueden long bode hir loues redde myn ere tale fedde luſt hir ſtorye somtyme drewe memorye ſorowe maye euer laſt ſo cometh hope laſt none foode knowe endureth throwe right chery feſte counten leſt yet eſeth ſomdele herte appeſeth thyng ere ſpredeth whiche pleſaunt ſomdele eſeth wordes ſuche ſhe may gete luſt ſtede mete loo thus fader ſey luſt whiche eye hath ſey eke ere hath herd ful ofte haue better ferd two bryngen thyrd whiche hath herte amydde place take aray luſty foode whiche aſſay mete namelyche nyghtes lacketh al ſightes heryng awey redy wey rere ſouper make whiche hertes fode take luſty cooke name hoote thought whiche hath euer pottes hote loue boylyng fyre fantaſye deſyre whiche full ofte ſhe fedde herte bedde ſet vppon lorde bothe euery ſight euery word luſt whiche haue herd ſeyn yet feſt pleyn wordes fiſſhes therof haue full diſſhes felyng taſte yet myght neuer haue one repaſte thus ye haue herd forn lycke hony thorne ſeith vpon brydell chewe ſo ydell effecte fode haue man wold hym ſaue ſyke medycyn ryght ſo loue famyn fond euer may fede drynke forth day til may haue gretter feſte whiche al honger myght areſte loo ſuche ben luſtes thre thynke ſee take loue fedyng withoute taſtyng felyng poure doeth heyre lyue good eſpyer • none ſuche delycacye trowe glotenye netheles youre auys hooly fader ben wy recommaunde myn eſtate haue ben delycate ſone vnderſtonde well thou haſt told euerydele thynketh thy tale ben delytes wonder ſmale wherof thou takeſt thy loues foode ſone yf thou vnderſtood ben delycious thow woldeſt curyous vpon luſt thyn eſtate ben fore delycate wherof thou reſon excede bookes thou myght rede mannes wyſedome ſhall ſhewed ought wel ben eſchewed loue wel wey theſe hooly bookes ſey bodely delyces alle euery poynt ſo falle vnto ſowle done greuaunce take remembreunce tale acordaunt vnto wiche grete vnderſtondyng man ſoule reſonable thynke telle fable hic ponit exemplum contra iſtos de licatos et narrat de diuite et laȝaro quorum geſtns euangelio lucasuidencius deſcribit criſtes worde declare wr • te englyſ • thus bigan criſt ſeith ryche man myghty lord grete eſtate eke ſo delycate clothyng euery day purpir bice made hym gay ete drank fylle luſtes wylle whiche ſtood al delyce took hede thylk vyce ſhold ſo betyde poure laȝar vpon tyde came gate axeth mete myght thyng gete dedely honger ſtaunche whiche ful paunche luſtes bord ne deyneth ſpeke word onlyche cromme yeue wherof peure myght leue vpon yeft almeſſe thus lay poure grete diſtreſſe ac • lde hongred gate whiche myght goo gate woful beſene lay grene houndes comen fro halle ſike man falle lay dye woundes maladye lyeken done hym eſe full ſuche dyſeſe may deth eſcape tyme ſhape ſo wle fro body paſſeth whome thyng ouerpaſſeth hyghe god vp heuen hym took hath ſet hym euen abraham barme hyghe heuens ioyr ſighe haue wold felle befalle ſhold ryche man ſame throwe ſodeyne deth ouerblowe forth withouten ony went helle ſtreyght went fende fire hym drough peyne ynough flamme whiche euer brenneth eye aboute renneth toward heuen caſt loke ſawe hede tooke laȝar ſet ſee ferre euer myght ſee abraham prayde vnto patriarke ſayde sende laȝar doune fro thylk ſete doo fynger wete water ſo may droppe vpon tonge ſtoppe grete hete whiche hrenne abraham auſwerd thenne ſeid hym wyſe ſone thou myght auyſe take thy remembraunce lalar grete penaunce whyles lyf thou al thy luſty iolyf bodely delytes ſoughteſt thy ſo thou wroughteſt ſhalt thou take thy reward dedely payne herafter ward helle whiche ſhall ener laſt laȝar laſt worldes payne ouer ronn • heuen hath lyf begonne ioye whiche endeles thou praydeſt neuertheles ſhal laȝar ſende water fyngers ende thyne hote tonge kele thou ſhalt ſuche grace fele folble place ſynne euer whiche thou ſhalt ben inne cometh none place thidder ne none yow maye come hydder thus ye parted two ryche ayeneward cryed tho abraham ſith hit ſoo laȝar may doo whiche haue axed place wold pray another grace haue yet bretheren fyue fader ben alyue geder dwellen one hows whome thou arte gracious pray thou woldeſt ſende laȝar ſo myght wende warne hem world wēt afterward ſhent ſuche peynes drye loo pray crye may hem ſelf amende patriarke anone ſende prayer anſwer nay ſaid hym euery day bretheren myght knowe moyſes erthe prophetes mo hem beſt ſaid yf myght man aryſe deth lyf ſuche wyſe tellen hem ſeyd thenne pure fere ſholden beware therby quod abraham nay ſikerly yf wylle obeye ſuche teche hem wey al day preche al day telle ſtont heuen helle wylle taken hede though befelle ſo dede ony dede man ſo arered ben hym better lered another man lyue thou ſone canſt deſcryue tale cryſt hym ſelf told thou ſhalt haue cauſe hold ſee ſo grete euydence ſooth experyence hath ſhewed openlyche eye bodely delycacye hym whiche yeueth almeſſe shal falle grete diſtreſſe ſene vpon riche ne wold vnto lyche crōme yeuen brede afterward dede droppe water hym werned thus may mannes wytte lerned hem ſo delytes taken deth ben ouertaken erſt ſwete ſowre gouernoure worldes good yf wyſe within herbe ſet pryce al world yet vſeth good nothyng refuſeth whiche lord thynges ouches ryche thynges clothe gold perrye taketh yet delycacye leueth though beſt mete eteth drynketh beſt drynke taketh none hede thynke delycacye put awaye whiche goth right waye fede clothe body ſowle bothe taken otherwyſe luſtes ben none wyſe whylome ſhewed eke thou theſe old bookes ſeke wel reſon kynde old enſamples men fynde hic loquitur de deſicacia newnis qui corporalibus delicijs magi adherens ſpiritualia gaudia minus obtinuit man yt wold hym wel auiſe delycacye deſpyſe whan kynde acordeth wherof enſample ſpecial new whylome may told whiche ayens kynde many fold luſtes took till laſt god hym wold ouercaſt whome cronyke ſo pleyne luſt hym ſeyne netheles glotonye bodely delycacye knowe ſtomak ferd man fore herd whiche wythin hym ſelf bethought wonder ſubtyle thyng wrought thre men vpon election age complexion lyche hym ſelf al way toke wardes hym play ete drank wel therof dyerſyte euery day whan ete tofore • ca withoute reſon loue herte ſet hym thynketh myght bet though fully mete luſt loue eure ſvete loo thus geder felauſhip delycacye dronkeſhip wherof reſon ſtant oute herre haue made full many man erre loues cauſe mooſt alle ſo euer falle wytte reſon vnderſtonde late gouernannce ſtonde wylle whiche wexeth ſo wild hym ſelf ſhyld fro perylle oute fere way ſecheth hym retcheth vppon fyde oftyme goth beſyde doth ſuche thyng withoute drede wherof hym ought wel drede whan loue aſſoted ſore paſſeth men lore luſt ordeyneth ther mannes myght reſtreyneth god taketh none hede lawes withoute drede purpoos wol acheue ayenſt poyntes byleue tempteth heuen erthe helle afterward ſhal telle dum ſtimulatur amor quicquid iubet ordo voluptas audet et aggredi tur nulla timenda timens omne quod aſtra quem herbarum ſiue poteſtas seu vigor inferni ſingula temptat amans quod nequit ipſe deo mediante parare ſiniſtrum demonis hec magica credulus arte parat sic ſibi non curat ad opus que recia tendit dūmodo nudatam prendere poſſet auem hic tractat qualiter ebrietas et deticacia onus pridicicic contrarium inſti tantes inter alia ad carnalis concupiſcencie promocionem ſacrilegio magicā requirunt dare thyng whiche loue ne dare loue euery lawe vnware lawes beſt fiſſhe fowle man beeſt al worldes kynde loutith loue whiche thyng douteth▪ mannes herte ſytte cometh toward wytte woo nomore wele hete chele wete drye lyue dye fore ne behynde ſeeth thyng blynde withoute inſight courage doth mecuayles rage thyng hym draw god lawe whome taketh heede baiard blynde ſtede tille falle dyche mydde goth ther man wyll hym bydde ſtant ſo ferforth oute rewle wytte may hym reule thus telle hym ſooth ful many thyng doeth better laft among whiche ſuche craft ſomme men clepen ſorcerye whiche wynue drewry many circumſtaunce vſeth poynte whiche refuſeth craft whiche saturnus founde make prykes ſounde geamaunce cleped ful ofte vſeth amys flood idromaunce fyre romaunce queſtions echone tho tempteth ofte eke alſo acremaunce iugement loue bryngeth aſſent theſe craftes fynde man may doo wey kynde ſo good entent goth al another went rather ſhold faile nygromancye wold aſſayle make incantacion hote manere toure vpon penſel wrought vlixes knewe token nought praid wyte ſomme party • thyng myght • ygnyfye ſigne whiche anſwered empyre forth ferd al ſodenly ſaid vlyxes oute ſlepe brayd ryght ayene day lenger ſlepen ne may ayene man hath knowlechyng saue hym ſelf thyng owne chaunce man knoweth fortune hym throweth yet neuer ſo wyſe clerke whiche myght knowe al goddes werk ne ſecrete whiche god hath ſette ayene man may lette vlyxes though wyſe wytte auyſe ſweuen acounteth leſſe wote amounteth calculacion ſeeth none demonſtracion al pleynly knowe ende netheles ſo wende drad hym owne ſone maketh hym wel ye aſtone ſhope therof anone within caſtel walle thelamon ſone ſhette tyl myght knowe bette ſooth ne knewe til fortune hym ouerthrewe netheles ſykerneſſe myght wyte geſſe place harde make ſuche ordynaunce loue ne acqueyntaunce erly late ſhold bete yate mauer man ſo betydde ſo hym ſelf bydde al myght hym auayl • whome fortune wyll aſſayle may reſiſtence whiche myght man make defence al ſhall muſt fal algate cyrces whiche ſpake tate whome vlyxes hath bigete childe though haue foryete tym • came wonne delyuerd ſonne whiche cleped thelogonus child bore thus aboute moder ful age reſon langage good eſtate drawe forth ſo mochel w •• th ſtonde mannes ſtede circe moder hath hym bede ſhall fader go told hym al geder tho man hym bega • • lelogonus herd ware ful knowlechyng fader kyng prayd moder fayre go fader ſhe hym graunted ſhall made hem redy forth tyme ſuche vſaunce euery man cong • yſaunce countre bare honde went ſtraunge londe thus euery man therfore well knowe bore eſpyall myſt • wynges dyde ſuche thynges euery man may knowe • bifelle throwe thelogonus ca contre ſigne thre fiſſhes whiche ſholde bere vpon pynon ſpere thus arrayd harneys aſſayd redy euerydele moder bad hym fare wele ſaid hym ſhold ſ • ythe fader grete thouſand • ythe thelogonus moder ky •• took leue wyſt fader way name til vnto nachare came whiche lond chyef cyte cleped aſketh kyng ferde ſooth herde kyng vlix • alone vpon ho • grete paas rood • hym forth honde bare ſignall londe fiſſhes thre haue told thus went hold owne fader dwelleth cauſe came telleth vnto kepars gate wold haue cemen ther ate ſhortely hym ſaid nay fayre euer may beſought told hem kyng fader proude wordes grete biganne manace threte go fro gate faſt wold hym take ſet faſt fro wordes vnto ſtrokes thus felle ſo thelogonus ſore hurte wel nyhe dede ſharp ſperes hede maketh defence ſo falle wan yate vpon hem alle hath ſlayne beſt fyue aſeryeden belyue thorugh oute caſtel al aboute euery ſyde men came oute wherof kynges herte aflyght al haſt yt myght ſpere caught oute goeth nyhe woode wroth ſawe yates ful blood thelogonus ſtood ſawe alſo ne knewe man hym threwe ſpere ſterte oute aſyde deſteny whiche ſhold betyde befelle ylke tyme ſo thelogonus knewe thyng tho man hym caſt whyles owne ſpere laſt al ſigne therupon caſt vnto kyng anone ſmote hym dedely woūde vlix • felle anone grounde tho euery man kyng kyng began crye thyng thelogonus whiche ſawe caas knee felle ſeid ala haue myn owne fader ſlayn wold deye wonder fayn • ſlee euer wylle certes right good ſkylle cryeth wepeth ſeid therfore ala euer bore vnhappy deſtyne wofully cometh kyng yet hath life ynoug • herte ayene vnto hym drough voyce ere leyd vnderſtood ſeid gan ſpeke ſaid hyghe bryng man whan ſyghe thelogonus thought ſet vpon ſweuen whiche met axeth myght ſee ſpere whiche fyſſhes thre ſawe vpon penſel wrought tho wyſt wel faileth nought bad hym telle ſhold fro whens came wold thelogonus ſorowe woo myght told tho vnto vlixes caas cyrces moder ſo forth ſeid hym euery dele moder grete hym wele wyſe ſhe hym ſent tho wiſt vlixes ment tooke gym armes ſofte al bledyng kyſt hym ofte ſaid ſone whyles lyue infortune foryeue ſone haſt ſente bigan hym haſ • cam vnto fader ty • e ſaw hym ſuche plyte wold haue ronnen vpon anone ſlayne owne broder ne ben vlixes bitwene hem made acord pe • heyre thelamacus thelogonus al power hir natyuyte fell holde hir luſt biholde prayd people aboute ſhope hir ryde oute mete al openly anone al men redy monethe may luſty quene good aray ſet vpon mule whyte ſene grete delyte ioye eyte made freſſhe thynges glade noble • une al behonged euery wyght ſore alonged ſ • e luſty lady ryde grete myrthe euery ſide paſſeth ſtrete th • full many tymbre bete many mayde carolyng thus thurgh yt • un hym nyghe lady ſyghe hir beaute hede tooke •• uthe withdrawe loke ſee nought elles felde ſtood hir biheld clothyng chere al vnlyche hapneth laſt quene vpon hym hir eye caſt knewe ſ • raūge anone biheld hir euer one withoute blemyſſhyng cheere took good • ede h • manere wondreth dyd ſo bad men ſheld hym goo came dyd hir reuerence ſhe axeth ſylence whome came wold ſobre wordes told ſeyth madame clerke yow meſſage cam whiche may tellen yf lyke yow muſt ſaid al pryuely none ſhal ye thus tyme tooke leue day goth forth till eue euery man mote lete werk ſhe thought euer vpon clerk thyng wold men wyſe abode quene paſſeth ouer thylk nyght till moro lyght ſend hym came hym aſtrolahe name whiche fyne gold precious poyntes cercles merueylous eke heuenly fygures wronght book full peyntures took til ye conceyue child word▪ ſhe wex al myld • ſomdele bicame ſhame axrth hym goddes name whiche ſo wol done companye ſeid amos luby ſhe ſaid may leue yf ſee better preue madame quod nectanabus token
